# CLAUDE.md тАФ Webnua Platform

> This file is read at the start of every Claude Code session. It is the standing
> instruction set for this project. Keep it concise тАФ bloat costs context every session.
> **When something goes wrong, fix the instance AND add a line here so it never recurs.**

---

## What this project is

The Webnua platform тАФ **one application, two roles, role-based access:**

- **Client view** тАФ what a Webnua customer (a business owner) sees: their funnels, tickets, integrations, websites, settings.
- **Admin/operator view** тАФ what the Webnua team sees: all clients, the Proof Page pipeline (audit тЖТ build тЖТ generate), internal automations, the cross-client integrations matrix, ticket inbox.

These are **not two apps.** They are one codebase, one component library, one design system, with routing and layouts that branch by role. A large share of components are **shared** between the two views. Treat shared-by-default as the assumption; role-specific is the exception that needs justifying.

---

## Agency / sub-account model (the operator's two tiers)

The operator view is a **two-tier agency model** (GoHighLevel-style). The agency does two kinds of work, separated by *what* is being managed:

- **Agency level** тАФ HQ. Cross-sub-account policy: default rules, capability floors, integration defaults, seat limits, plan catalog (Cluster 9). Done in **agency mode** (no sub-account selected). No drilldown.
- **Sub-account level** тАФ one client. Their funnels, automations, campaigns, leads, integrations, profile. Reached by picking the sub-account from the sidebar `AdminClientPicker` тЖТ **sub-account mode**.

Mode is **state-driven** (`useIsAgencyMode()` from `lib/workspace/workspace-stub.tsx`), not URL-driven. Surfaces that exist at both levels **dispatch on the mode** тАФ the settled pattern (`/dashboard`, `/website`, `/settings/access`; `/settings/*` joins it in Cluster 8). URL stays clean.

**Layered resolution.** Every agency-level setting resolves down the stack:

1. **Platform defaults** тАФ code constants (`CLIENT_DEFAULTS`, section registryтАж).
2. **Agency policy** тАФ what the agency sets HQ-wide.
2.5. **Assigned plan** тАФ the billing plan's policy bundle (**Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 1** inserted this layer; see `lib/billing/`). A plan supplies a `Partial<PolicyValueMap>` тАФ keys it omits fall through to Layer 2.
3. **Sub-account** тАФ inherits Layer 2/2.5; may **override** it. Override-anywhere model: every policy key is overridable per sub-account, flagged `inherited` vs `overridden`.

Effective value = resolve down the stack: `override ?? assignedPlan.policy[key] ?? agencyPolicy[key]`. Generalises the existing capability pattern (role defaults + grants). Built in **Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 2** as `lib/agency/` тАФ agency policy store + per-sub-account override store + a typed `resolvePolicy` resolver returning `{ effectiveValue, source: 'agency' | 'plan' | 'override', agencyValue, planValue }`.

**Policy keys тАФ the closed typed union.** A policy key is something that flows through the resolver. This is the *complete* set тАФ the resolver is typed to this union, **NOT** `Record<string, unknown>`:

| Key | Value type | Cluster 8 status |
|---|---|---|
| `defaultClientCapabilities` | `Capability[]` | wired (S3/S4) |
| `integrationDefaults` | integration provider config | wired (S3/S4) |
| `defaultSeatLimit` | `number \| null` | wired (S3/S4) тАФ resolves the misplaced seat-limit |
| `brandDefaults` | brand tokens (font / accent) | typed now, wired later |
| `automationDefaults` | `Record<string, boolean>` on/off flags | typed now, wired later |
| `pricingDefaults` | currency + buffer rules | typed now, wired later |

Deferred keys are named in the union *now* so Session 2's resolver is shaped right. Don't add a key outside this list without amending it here first тАФ "we'll discover them as we go" is the grab-bag warning sign.

**NOT a policy key тАФ structured templates (deferred, needs its own design).** Agency-provided *default funnel structures, default automation flow copy, default review-request templates* are nested structured data, not flat policy. "Override-anywhere" means something different there (override a whole template? a field? fork it?). Bigger shape тАФ out of Cluster 8, and explicitly **not** shoehorned into the policy resolver.

**Webnua-as-sub-account тАФ deferred, kept drop-in-ready.** The agency's own marketing account (Webnua) is structurally identical to a client sub-account but is *not* in the sidebar picker yet (deliberate). Cluster 8 must not introduce anything that makes the future drop-in harder тАФ sub-account surfaces stay shape-agnostic about *which* client is active; no `clientId === 'webnua'` special-casing.

**Settings classification.** `/settings/*` becomes mode-dispatched in Cluster 8. Tab homes:

- **Agency-level** (agency mode): Workspace (agency identity), Team (agency operators), Access (cap policy + drill), Integrations (cross-client matrix + nudges + the agency connection policy), Defaults, Default seat limit, Plans (catalog тАФ Cluster 9), API & services (platform plumbing + API keys + webhooks), Danger zone.
- **Sub-account-level** (sub-account mode / client role): Profile, Integrations (per-account keys/overrides), Notifications, Billing (assigned plan), Team (client teammates + seats), Danger.
- **User-level** (orthogonal axis тАФ the signed-in person, not a workspace): Login + security. Help is global/static.

---

## Stack тАФ these are decided. Do not introduce alternatives.

- **Framework:** Next.js (App Router) + React + TypeScript
- **Styling:** Tailwind CSS, themed to the prototype's design tokens (see Design System below)
- **Primitives:** shadcn/ui тАФ the canonical primitive layer. Button, Input, Dialog, Card, Badge, etc. come from here.
- **Backend (in progress тАФ see `reference/backend-schema-design.md`):** Supabase. Frontend is built now; build the data layer with Supabase's shape in mind (role-based row access, the auditтЖТproof-page record relationship). Do not invent a placeholder data pattern that will be ripped out. **`@supabase/supabase-js`** is a dependency as of Phase 2 (real auth) тАФ the first runtime dependency added since the stack was frozen; the typed browser client lives at `src/lib/supabase/client.ts`.
- **Data layer:** TanStack Query (React Query) is the data-fetching spine тАФ caching, revalidation, loading/error state, optimistic updates. `@tanstack/react-query` is installed as of Phase 3's first wired surface (the leads inbox); the `QueryProvider` lives at `src/lib/query/QueryProvider.tsx` and is mounted in the root layout. Supabase Realtime is added *selectively*, only on genuinely-live surfaces (tickets, approvals, notifications). Failures surface as `AppError` тАФ a `queryFn` throws it, React Query catches it into a typed `error` (see Error handling below). Per-surface data-access modules live beside their feature (`lib/leads/queries.ts`, тАж).
- **TypeScript:** strict mode, from line one. No `any` without a written reason.

If a task seems to need a library not listed here, **stop and ask** before adding it. Every dependency is a decision.

---

## The cardinal rule: check before you build

**Before creating ANY component, hook, util, or type тАФ search the codebase for an existing one.**

- Grep `src/components/` and `src/lib/` for anything that does this or is close.
- If something close exists: **extend it or compose with it.** Do not create a parallel version.
- If you're unsure whether something exists: **search, don't assume.** An unnecessary search is free; a duplicate component is technical debt.
- If a genuinely new component is needed, check whether it belongs in `ui/`, `shared/`, or a route folder (see Structure) before creating it.

Duplicate components for the same concern are the #1 failure mode this project is guarding against. One canonical Button. One canonical FindingCard. One canonical Stepper.

---

## Project structure тАФ where things live

```
/reference          тЖТ the HTML prototypes + spec docs. READ-ONLY. Never import from here.
/src
  /app              тЖТ Next.js App Router. Layouts branch by role here.
    /(client)       тЖТ client-role routes + client layout
    /(admin)        тЖТ admin-role routes + admin layout
    /(auth)         тЖТ login / role resolution
  /components
    /ui             тЖТ shadcn primitives + low-level building blocks. Canonical. Shared by everyone.
    /shared         тЖТ composed components used by BOTH client and admin views
    /client         тЖТ composed components used ONLY by the client view
    /admin          тЖТ composed components used ONLY by the admin view
  /lib              тЖТ utils, helpers, hooks, types, constants
  /lib/types        тЖТ shared TypeScript types тАФ the single source of truth for data shapes
```

**Placement rules:**
- A component used by both roles тЖТ `components/shared/`. Default here.
- A component used by one role тЖТ `components/client/` or `components/admin/`.
- A primitive (does one small thing, no business logic) тЖТ `components/ui/`.
- If a `client/` component starts being needed in `admin/`, **move it to `shared/`** тАФ don't copy it.

---

## The prototypes тАФ how to use them

Two HTML prototypes live in `/reference`. They are the **visual and behavioural specification.** They are NOT source to port.

- **Design tokens тЖТ extract verbatim.** Colours, fonts, radii, spacing from the prototype CSS go into the Tailwind config. Pure extraction.
- **Primitives тЖТ build fresh, once.** Match the prototype's styling, build the canonical shadcn-based version.
- **Composed components тЖТ build fresh from primitives**, using the prototype as the visual + behaviour spec.
- **The prototype HTML тЖТ never imported into `src`.** It is read-only reference. Look at it to know what to build; never copy from it.

Do not "convert the HTML screen by screen." That produces one-off components. Build the token layer, then primitives, then compose.

---

## Design system

The look comes from the prototype. The tokens (lift these into `tailwind.config` and the CSS variables):

- **Colours (Webnua palette тАФ source of truth):** paper `#f5f1ea`, paper-2 `#ebe5d9`, paper-3 `#e0d8c8`, ink `#0a0a0a` (with ink-soft `#2a2a28`, ink-mid `#4a4a45`, ink-quiet `#6e685c`), rust `#d24317` (with rust-deep `#8a3815`, rust-light `#e8743b`, rust-soft `#f4dccd` тАФ the Perth landing page uses `#d24317`; the tools used `#d45b1a`, **standardise on `#d24317`**), good `#1e6b3a`, warn `#c44444`, info `#2d7d8a`, plum `#6b4ea6` (category swatch тАФ campaigns), amber `#c8941e` (category swatch тАФ reviews), rule `#c9c0b0`.
- **Two utility vocabularies, one bright line.** `globals.css` also exposes shadcn role aliases (`primary`, `secondary`, `background`, `foreground`, `card`, `popover`, `muted`, `accent`, `destructive`, `border`, `input`, `ring`) pointing at the Webnua palette. These are NOT a parallel palette тАФ they're a role layer used internally by shadcn-derived primitives. **Bright line:** shadcn-derived files (anything pulled from `npx shadcn add ...`) keep the shadcn role vocabulary they ship with тАФ don't fight upstream. Everything Webnua-authored тАФ custom primitives in `ui/` like `Eyebrow`/`StatusDot`, and all of `shared/`, `client/`, `admin/` тАФ uses the Webnua palette names (`bg-paper`, `text-ink`, `border-rule`, `text-rust`, etc.). The test is "did this file come from shadcn or did we write it" тАФ no judgment call. **One sanctioned exception:** `bg-card` тАФ the white-surface alias (`#ffffff`). Webnua-authored files may use `bg-card` for white card surfaces, because the Webnua palette has no white token (`paper` / `paper-2` / `paper-3` are all off-white). Until a dedicated `bg-surface` token is introduced, `bg-card` IS the canonical white surface in Webnua-authored code тАФ it is the only shadcn role token allowed outside shadcn-derived files. (If you reach for any other role token тАФ `bg-primary`, `text-foreground`, `border-ring`, etc. тАФ that's the bright-line violation.)
- **Fonts:** Inter Tight (display + body), JetBrains Mono (eyebrows, data, technical labels).
- **Feel:** light theme тАФ paper backgrounds, ink text, rust accent. Heavy uppercase Inter Tight for display headings, tight letter-spacing. Mono eyebrow tags. Generous section rhythm.

When a design decision isn't covered by a token, **ask rather than inventing** тАФ design drift is hard to undo later.

---

## Workflow rules тАФ how we work together

1. **Plan before code.** For anything beyond a trivial change, explain the approach and list the files you'll touch *before* writing. Wait for confirmation on anything non-obvious.
2. **One screen or one feature per session** where possible. Small, focused scope. Large unfocused sessions are where redo/undo happens.
3. **Don't refactor unrelated code while doing something else.** Fixing a bug? Fix the bug. See something else messy? Mention it, don't touch it.
4. **Respect what's working.** Do not "improve," reformat, or restructure code that wasn't part of the task. If existing code looks wrong but works, ask before changing it.
5. **If a change touches more than ~5 files, stop and confirm** the approach before proceeding.
6. **Commit at every working state.** A clean git history is the undo button. Suggest a commit whenever something works.
7. **No silent scope expansion.** If the task turns out bigger than it looked, say so and re-confirm тАФ don't just keep going.

---

## Code conventions

- **Components:** one component per file, named export, file named after the component (`FindingCard.tsx`).
- **Component internal layout:** consistent order тАФ types/props at top, the component, helpers below. Predictable structure makes debugging navigation, not archaeology.
- **Types:** shared data shapes live in `src/lib/types`. Don't redefine the same shape in two places тАФ import it.
- **Naming:** descriptive and specific. `ProofPageStepper` not `Stepper2`. No numbered suffixes ever тАФ a numbered suffix means a duplicate that should have been a reuse.
- **State:** local state for local concerns. Lift only when genuinely shared. Don't reach for global state by default.
- **Error handling:** `Result<T>` + a discriminated `AppError` тАФ `src/lib/errors.ts` (rationale in `reference/backend-schema-design.md` ┬з8). Data-access boundaries either **return** `Result<T>` (`{ ok: true, data } | { ok: false, error }`) at imperative call sites, or **throw** `AppError` inside a TanStack Query `queryFn`/`mutationFn` (React Query catches it into a typed `error`). `AppError.kind` is one of `auth | forbidden | not_found | validation | conflict | unexpected`. Throwing a plain `Error` is reserved for genuine programmer error (a broken invariant), never an expected failure.
- **`useSyncExternalStore` snapshots MUST be reference-stable.** `getSnapshot` cannot return a fresh array/object each call (no `.filter()`/`.map()`/`{...}`/`.sort()` inline) тАФ React then sees the store "change" every render and spins into an infinite loop that crashes the route in production. The Supabase-backed in-memory caches (agency-policy / overrides / plan-catalog / plan-assignments / client-invites / seat-limit / roster) bump a version counter on every write and only rebuild the snapshot when the version changes тАФ same shape, different mechanism. Any new store accessor read through `useSyncExternalStore` must do the same.
- **No dead code.** Don't leave commented-out blocks "just in case" тАФ git remembers.

---

## What NOT to touch

- `/reference` тАФ read-only, ever.
- Generated files, lockfiles, `.next/`.
- The `@theme` block in `src/app/globals.css` (the Webnua design tokens тАФ palette, fonts, radii, shadows) and `tsconfig` strict settings тАФ these are deliberate. Tailwind v4 is CSS-first, so tokens live in `@theme`, not `tailwind.config.*`. Changing them needs a conversation.
- Any config that's clearly intentional тАФ ask first.

---

## Known component inventory

> Keep this list current. When a shared component is built, add it here so future sessions
> find it instead of rebuilding it. This is the map that prevents duplication.
> Format: **`Name`** тАФ purpose тАФ variants/sizes/notable props.

### `ui/` тАФ primitives

**shadcn-derived (keep shadcn role vocabulary; don't fight upstream):**

- **`Button`** (`button.tsx`) тАФ canonical action element. Themed to prototype: `h-10 px-[22px]` default, `rounded` (8px), `font-bold`. Variants: `default` (rust/primary), `secondary` (paper-2 with border), `outline` (white with border), `ghost` (transparent, muted text), `link`, `destructive`. Sizes: `sm`, `default`, `lg`, `icon`. Supports `asChild` via Radix `Slot`.
- **`Input`** (`input.tsx`) тАФ single-line text input. `h-10`, white card bg, 14px├Ч10px padding, `rounded-md`. Inherits `bg-card`/`border-input` from alias layer. Standard HTML input props; supports `aria-invalid` styling.
- **`Textarea`** (`textarea.tsx`) тАФ multi-line text input. Same shape as Input but `min-h-20`, `font-mono`, `field-sizing-content` (auto-grows).
- **`Select`** + `SelectTrigger` / `SelectContent` / `SelectItem` / `SelectGroup` / `SelectLabel` / `SelectSeparator` / `SelectValue` / `SelectScrollUpButton` / `SelectScrollDownButton` (`select.tsx`) тАФ Radix-backed dropdown. Trigger has `sm` / `default` sizes. Content opens below by default (popper, start-aligned). Use for any dropdown with discrete options.
- **`Dialog`** + `DialogTrigger` / `DialogContent` / `DialogHeader` / `DialogFooter` / `DialogTitle` / `DialogDescription` / `DialogClose` / `DialogOverlay` / `DialogPortal` (`dialog.tsx`) тАФ Radix-backed modal. **`DialogContent` accepts `size`: `sm` (480px) / `default` (560px) / `lg` (920px).** White card surface, `rounded-2xl`, `p-10`, paper backdrop. Close button auto-renders top-right (suppress with `showCloseButton={false}`).
- **`Card`** + `CardHeader` / `CardTitle` / `CardDescription` / `CardContent` / `CardFooter` / `CardAction` (`card.tsx`) тАФ white-on-paper surface panel (`.auto-card` in proto). `rounded-xl`, `border-border`, `shadow-card`, `py-6`. Use for any bordered content surface; compose with the sub-parts.
- **`Badge`** (`badge.tsx`) тАФ small pill label, `rounded-full`. Variants: `default` (rust filled), `secondary` (paper-2), `muted` (paper-2 + quiet text тАФ most common in proto), `destructive`, `outline`. Supports inline children including `StatusDot` for dot-prefixed status pills.
- **`Tabs`** + `TabsList` / `TabsTrigger` / `TabsContent` (`tabs.tsx`) тАФ Radix-backed tabs. `TabsList` has `default` (filled pill) and `line` (underline) variants. Default orientation horizontal; vertical supported via `orientation="vertical"`.
- **`Tooltip`** + `TooltipProvider` / `TooltipTrigger` / `TooltipContent` (`tooltip.tsx`) тАФ Radix-backed tooltip. **Wrap the app (or section) in `TooltipProvider`** for tooltips to function. Ink-on-paper styling with arrow.

**Webnua-authored (use Webnua palette tokens; bright line in design-system above):**

- **`BrandMark`** (`BrandMark.tsx`) тАФ canonical "Webnua тЧЖ" wordmark: rotated rust diamond + Inter Tight wordmark, `font-extrabold tracking-[-0.03em]`. Sizes: `sm` / `default` (sidebar size) / `lg` (auth screen). Color is inherited via `text-*` on the parent тАФ set `text-paper` on ink backgrounds, `text-ink` on paper. No business logic. **`SidebarBrand` composes this**; don't duplicate the glyph elsewhere.
- **`Eyebrow`** (`eyebrow.tsx`) тАФ mono uppercase tag used as section/eyebrow label across both prototypes (`.sidebar-section-label`, `.modal-tag`, etc.). JetBrains Mono, `text-[10px]`, `tracking-[0.14em]`, `font-bold`, uppercase. Tones: `rust` (default, brand), `ink`, `quiet`. Optional `bullet` prop renders a leading colored dot via `::before`.
- **`StatusDot`** (`status-dot.tsx`) тАФ 6px colored circle used as inline status/severity indicator (matches `.status-dot` in proto). Tones: `good` (default), `warn`, `info`, `rust`, `quiet`. Composable inside `Badge`/`Eyebrow` for dot-prefixed pills.
- **`Switch`** (`switch.tsx`) тАФ bespoke 44├Ч24 toggle, Radix Switch under the hood. Matches `.toggle` in proto exactly: rule-bg off / good-bg on, 18px white knob slides 20px on activate. Optional `label` prop renders a mono uppercase label adjacent (quiet off, good on тАФ peer-data driven). Use for any boolean on/off control.

### `shared/` тАФ app shell + cross-role composed components

- **`AppShell`** (`AppShell.tsx`) тАФ top-level grid wrapper for the authed app. `grid-cols-[280px_1fr] min-h-svh bg-paper`. Takes `sidebar` slot + `children` (the main area). The 280px sidebar + 1fr main matches both prototypes exactly.
- **`Sidebar`** (`Sidebar.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg, sticky-to-viewport, scrollable column. Structure only; children are passed in (brand, sections, items, footer). Compose via `ClientSidebar`/`AdminSidebar` rather than using directly.
- **`SidebarBrand`** (`SidebarBrand.tsx`) тАФ sidebar-header composition: `BrandMark` (rendered `text-paper` on the ink sidebar bg) + a mono meta line below. Prop: `meta` (e.g. `"Client workspace"` / `"Operator console"`). For the plain wordmark on other surfaces, use `BrandMark` directly (e.g. the auth screen).
- **`SidebarSectionLabel`** (`SidebarSectionLabel.tsx`) тАФ mono uppercase eyebrow used between sidebar groups (`// Your business`, `// Overview`, etc.). Renders `// {children}` styled paper-on-ink quiet.
- **`SidebarItem`** (`SidebarItem.tsx`) тАФ nav row inside the sidebar. Icon + label + optional badge. Wraps `next/link`. Auto-detects active state from `usePathname`. Active state = left rust rail + lifted bg + rust-light icon. Takes a `NavItem` (`{ label, href, icon, badge? }`).
- **`SidebarUser`** (`SidebarUser.tsx`) тАФ bottom-of-sidebar user card. Avatar circle + name + role meta. Props: `initial`, `name`, `role`.
- **`Topbar`** (`Topbar.tsx`) тАФ page-level top bar inside `main`. `'use client'` (reads `useRole()` for the role-conditional chrome). Slots: `breadcrumb` (left), `middle` (centred, optional тАФ admin step-tracker), `search` (centred, optional тАФ an explicit `GlobalSearchInput`, e.g. `/search` seeding the current query; mutually exclusive with `middle`), `hideSearch` (boolean тАФ opts a page out of the operator search auto-render; set on pages with their own in-body search: the admin leads + tickets inboxes), `actions` (right, optional). Sticky to the main area with rule border. **Two role-conditional fixtures, auto-rendered with no per-page wiring:** client-role users get a `NotificationBell` ahead of any `actions`; operator-role users get a `GlobalSearchInput` in the centre slot (Cluster 6 ┬╖ 2 added the slot; Session 7 made it the operator default тАФ the mirror of the bell). Explicit `middle`/`search` win over the auto-render; `hideSearch` suppresses it. See `client/notifications/` and `shared/search/` below.
- **`TopbarBreadcrumb`** (`Topbar.tsx`) тАФ helper that renders `trail / trail / current` in mono uppercase. Pass as the `breadcrumb` slot of `Topbar`.
- **`PagePlaceholder`** (`PagePlaceholder.tsx`) тАФ placeholder body block used by Phase-4 stub routes and any not-yet-built page. Eyebrow + title + description + a dashed-border "wiring only" hint card. Replace with real page content as each route is built.
- **`PageHeader`** (`PageHeader.tsx`) тАФ canonical page-top block: rust mono `eyebrow` (string, rendered through `Eyebrow tone="rust" bullet`) + 40px Inter Tight `title` (ReactNode, so callers pass `<>Your <em>clients</em>.</>` for rust em-highlight) + optional `subtitle` (ReactNode, `<strong>` segments render ink-bold). Matches the `.screen-title-block`/`.greeting-block` pattern from both prototypes. Default `mb-8` rhythm.
- **`StatCard`** (`StatCard.tsx`) тАФ single white-card stat tile: mono quiet `label` + 30px Inter Tight `value` (ReactNode, supports `<em>` for rust highlight) + optional `trend` line. `trendTone: 'good' | 'quiet'` (default `good`). Matches `.client-stat-card` (admin) and `.c-landing-stat` (client) 1:1. Compose in a `grid grid-cols-4 gap-3.5` row тАФ no `StatRow` wrapper, the grid is too thin to abstract. **Cluster 6 ┬╖ 1b** added an optional `chart` slot (ReactNode, rendered below the trend тАФ additive, never replaces value/trend) for hosting a `MiniTrendBars` sparkline.
- **`MiniTrendBars`** (`MiniTrendBars.tsx`) тАФ small bar sparkline: `data: number[]` (oldest тЖТ newest) + optional `labels` (default `3W / 2W / LW / NOW`). Bars scale to the series max; the final (newest) bar is rust-highlighted, the rest sit in the rule colour. Built for the overview hub's vs-prior stat cards (`StatCard`'s `chart` slot).
- **`CapabilityGate`** (`CapabilityGate.tsx`) тАФ wraps any control with capability-aware presentation. Props: `capability: Capability`, `mode: 'hide' | 'disable' | 'request'`, `children`, optional `disabledExplainer` (overrides the default `CAP_EXPLAINER` tooltip text), optional `requestContext: { pageId?, sectionId?, fieldKey? }`, optional `onRequestChange`. Has the cap тЖТ renders children. Lacks + `hide` тЖТ renders null. Lacks + `disable` тЖТ renders children inert (opacity-55, pointer-events-none) with a `Tooltip` showing the explainer. Lacks + `request` тЖТ renders `<RequestChangeAffordance>` with the cap's `requestLabel`; clicking it routes to the `/tickets/new` submit form prefilled with the field context via `buildRequestChangeHref` (`lib/tickets/request-change.ts`), unless the caller passes `onRequestChange` to override. **`request` mode auto-falls-back to `hide` when the cap's `requestLabel` is empty** (currently: `viewBuilder`, `approve`) тАФ deliberately so a labelless cap doesn't render a broken affordance.
- **`RequestChangeAffordance`** (`RequestChangeAffordance.tsx`) тАФ hover overlay surfaced by `CapabilityGate mode="request"`. Children render visually-present-but-inert (opacity-55, pointer-events-none); a rust-soft/rust-bordered button absolutely-positioned on top reveals on `group-hover` / `focus-visible` showing `{label} тЖТ` in mono uppercase. Fires the `onClick` callback (`CapabilityGate` wires this to the `/tickets/new` submit form by default). Reusable standalone тАФ anywhere you want the "hover to reveal request-change affordance over an inert control" pattern.
- **`WorkspaceContextBanner`** (`WorkspaceContextBanner.tsx`) тАФ small pill that reinforces which workspace context the operator is in. Agency mode тЖТ paper-2 pill, `тЧЖ All clients ┬╖ birds-eye`. Sub-account mode тЖТ rust-soft pill with pulsing dot, `Sub-account ┬╖ {clientName}`, plus an inline `тЖР Back to agency` `Button` (suppress with `hideReturnButton`). Used on context-aware page headers (currently just `/settings/access`) so the operator always knows where they are even with the sidebar scrolled out of view. Returns `null` until hydrated to avoid SSR mismatch. Optional `agencyLabel` override.
- **`FilterChips`** (`FilterChips.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` rust-active / paper-inactive filter chip strip with optional count badges. Generic `{ id, label, count? }` chip type. Single-select; supports uncontrolled (`defaultActiveId`) or controlled (`value` + `onChange`). Mono `label` prop (e.g. `// CLIENT`) sits to the left of the chip row. Extracted in Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 3 from the previously-separate `LeadFilterChips` + `CalendarClientFilterBar` (both deleted) once the third surface (`/automations` admin filter) made the third data point. Distinct from `shared/ChipSelector` тАФ that's a single-select **pick** (ink-active, no badges); this is the filter-chip vocabulary (rust-active, optional count). Used by: admin leads inbox, admin calendar, admin automations.
- **`ConfirmDialog`** (`ConfirmDialog.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` branded confirm modal, the in-app replacement for native `window.confirm` on user-facing actions. Built on `Dialog` (`size="sm"`). Props: `open` / `onOpenChange`, `title`, optional `description`, `confirmLabel`, `cancelLabel` (default "Keep it"), `tone: 'default' | 'destructive'`, `onConfirm`. Confirm fires `onConfirm` then closes. Used by the booking-detail "Cancel booking" actions; reuse for any future destructive/irreversible confirm.

### `shared/settings/` тАФ settings + integrations screen pair (Phase 5 sessions A + B)

> **Architectural note тАФ settings lives outside the role route groups.** Routes whose URL space is **shared** between roles can't live inside `(client)` or `(admin)` тАФ Next.js refuses two route groups resolving to the same URL. Three such shared route trees exist at the top level: **`app/dashboard/`** (admin home + client home), **`app/settings/`** (the entire `/settings/*` tab space), and **`app/tickets/`** (`/tickets`, `/tickets/[id]`, `/tickets/new`). Each has its own `layout.tsx` ('use client', reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, also mounts the `DevRoleSwitcher`). For `/dashboard` the page itself is a `'use client'` dispatcher with `_admin-content.tsx` / `_client-content.tsx` siblings тАФ **plus `_hub-content.tsx`**: the admin branch dispatches a second time on `useIsAgencyMode()` (Cluster 6 ┬╖ 1a), agency mode тЖТ `_admin-content` (the cross-client roster), sub-account mode тЖТ `_hub-content` (the single-client overview hub, Screen 20). For settings, role-specific tab slugs (`/profile`, `/workspace`, `/team`, `/notifications`, `/security`, `/help`, `/defaults`, `/api`, `/danger`, `/seats`) are reached only from the correct role+mode's nav, so their pages render statically without re-checking role; shared-slug tab pages (`/settings/integrations`, `/settings/billing`) are `'use client'` and dispatch on `useRole()` тАФ per-role bodies live as `_admin-content.tsx` / `_client-content.tsx` siblings (underscore = naming convention, not a Next.js private rule); for both, the admin body dispatches a second time on workspace mode with a `_sub-account-content.tsx` sibling (integrations тЖТ Cluster 8 ┬╖ 4b; billing тЖТ Cluster 9 ┬╖ 3). **Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4a тАФ `/settings/*` is workspace-mode-aware.** The nav set is resolved at runtime by `useSettingsNav()` (role + `useIsAgencyMode()`); the settings `layout.tsx` carries a guard that bounces an operator who reaches a wrong-mode tab by direct URL (agency-only: workspace/defaults/seats/api; sub-account-only: profile/notifications) back to the mode-aware `/settings` index redirect. No tab page passes a static nav anymore. The resolver-backed sub-account *content* (per-account integration overrides, seat-limit resolution) lands in Session 4b. Admin-only URLs that aren't shared still live inside `(admin)` тАФ e.g. `/clients/new` (the create-client flow). The cross-client integrations matrix is **not** a standalone route тАФ it renders inside `/settings/integrations` agency mode (`_admin-content.tsx`) as the matrix + nudge cards + the agency connection-policy section. Platform plumbing (Stripe / Resend / Twilio / Anthropic / Vercel) lives separately on `/settings/api` ("API & services"), not on the Integrations tab. When real auth ships, the shared-route layouts become the place to check the JWT role and 404/redirect on mismatched access; nothing else moves.

- **`SettingsShell`** (`settings/SettingsShell.tsx`) тАФ wraps `PageHeader` + `SettingsContextBanner` + the two-column settings layout (`220px` nav left + `1fr` panel right, `gap-7`, `items-start`). Used by every tab page under `app/settings/*` (see the architectural note below тАФ settings lives **outside** the `(client)`/`(admin)` route groups because the URL space is shared between roles). Props: `eyebrow`, `title`, `subtitle`, `children` (the right-column panel content). **No `items` prop** (Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4a) тАФ the nav resolves itself from role + workspace mode. Provides the page padding (`px-10 py-10`) тАФ each tab page renders `Topbar` separately above it.
- **`SettingsNav`** (`settings/SettingsNav.tsx`) тАФ vertical tab nav rendered as `next/link`s. Active state from `usePathname` (matches exact `href` or any deeper path under it). Active style = ink-bg + paper text; inactive = ink-quiet text on paper, hover bumps to paper-2 + ink. **Resolves its own items via `useSettingsNav()`** (Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4a) тАФ no `items` prop. `useSettingsNav` (`lib/nav/use-settings-nav.ts`) dispatches on role + `useIsAgencyMode()`: client тЖТ `clientSettingsNav`; operator + agency mode тЖТ `adminSettingsNav` (the agency HQ set); operator + sub-account mode тЖТ `subAccountSettingsNav`.
- **`SettingsContextBanner`** (`settings/SettingsContextBanner.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` wrapper mounting `WorkspaceContextBanner` on every settings page via `SettingsShell`. Operators only тАФ renders null for client-role users (no agency/sub-account axis). Replaces the per-page manual banner mounts.
- **`SettingsSection`** (`settings/SettingsSection.tsx`) тАФ vertically-stacked section block inside a `Card`. Props: `heading` (ReactNode, supports `<em>` for rust highlight тАФ covers both the plain `settings-section-h` and the `*-content-h` rust-em variants from the prototype), `description` (ReactNode, `<strong>` renders ink-bold), `children`. Auto-separates from the next section with `border-b border-paper-2 pb-7 mb-7`, and removes the border + bottom rhythm when it's the last child (`last:border-b-0 last:mb-0 last:pb-0`).
- **`SettingsFieldRow`** (`settings/SettingsFieldRow.tsx`) тАФ single label/value row inside a `SettingsSection`. Props: `label` (string), `sub` (optional string under label), `value` (ReactNode тАФ wrap a span in `className="mono"` for the JetBrains Mono treatment), `action` (optional ReactNode тАФ typically a "Edit тЬО" / "Request change тЬО" inline affordance). Grid `220px 1fr`, dotted bottom rule between rows, no rule on the last row.
- **`IntegrationCard`** (`settings/IntegrationCard.tsx`) тАФ the integration row used on the `/settings/integrations` pages and the `/settings/api` platform-services list. Logo block (56├Ч56, brand-tinted) + name + status pill (inline with name on both roles тАФ converged on the better layout) + description + optional `meta` line + action button. Props: `name`, `description` (ReactNode), `status: 'connected' | 'warning' | 'missing' | 'partial'`, optional `statusLabel` to override the default ("Connected"/"Needs reauth"/"Not connected"/"Partially connected"), `logo: { initial, tone? }` where `tone` is `'gbp' | 'meta' | 'ga' | 'gads' | 'stripe' | 'generic'` (defaults to generic = ink-bg / rust-light glyph), optional `meta` (ReactNode тАФ colour shifts to warn on `warning` status), and `action: IntegrationAction` (`{ label, href?, variant?, kind? }` тАФ when `kind` is set the action opens the `ConnectIntegrationModal` in that mode instead of acting as a link; `kind` takes precedence over `href`). Re-exports `IntegrationStatus`, `IntegrationLogoTone`, `IntegrationAction`, `IntegrationCardProps`.
- **`ConnectIntegrationModal`** (`settings/ConnectIntegrationModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Dialog-based integration connect flow (admin prototype Screen 25). One status-driven component: a four-step OAuth-style display whose per-step state + framing copy switch on `mode: 'connect' | 'reauthorize' | 'manage'`. `connect` = fresh flow (step 1 current), `reauthorize` = token refresh on an already-linked account (steps 2-3 done), `manage` = all steps done / connected view. STUB тАФ the footer actions just close the modal. Props: `open` / `onOpenChange`, `mode`, `integration: { name, logoInitial }`. Re-exports `ConnectIntegrationMode`, `ConnectIntegrationTarget`.
- **`ConnectIntegrationButton`** (`settings/ConnectIntegrationButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` trigger pairing a `Button` with `ConnectIntegrationModal` open state, so `IntegrationCard` stays server-renderable (same pattern as `AddBookingButton`). `IntegrationCard` renders this whenever `action.kind` is set. Props: `mode`, `integration`, `label`, `variant`.
- **`IntegrationProgressHero`** (`settings/IntegrationProgressHero.tsx`) тАФ the ink-bg rust-tagged progress band at the top of the client `/settings/integrations` page. Props: `tag` (rust mono pill string), `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust highlight, 26px headline), `subtitle` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = paper-bold), `connected` + `total` (numeric тАФ drives the big mono fraction + the rustтЖТrust-light gradient fill), `remainingLabel` (ReactNode for the right-of-bar caption). For the admin cross-client matrix's different hero shape (stat tiles, not a single fraction), see `admin/integrations/IntegrationMatrixHero`.
- **`SettingsPanel`** (`settings/SettingsPanel.tsx`) тАФ extracted from the inline `<Card className="py-7"><CardContent className="px-8">` pattern (parked-decision trigger fired on second-use). White-card surface that holds a sequence of `SettingsSection` children with the correct vertical rhythm. Single `className` knob; no other props. Every tab page uses this; no tab page should re-inline the `Card` + `CardContent` composition.
- **`NotificationRow`** (`settings/NotificationRow.tsx`) тАФ single notification preference row used on the client Notifications tab. Props: `label`, optional `sub`, `channels: NotificationChannel[]` (e.g. `['sms','email','push']` тАФ declares which channels are valid for this notification), `active: NotificationChannel[]` (which are currently on). Renders each channel as a dot+label pill тАФ good-green when on, ink-quiet when off. Re-exports `NotificationChannel` type.
- **`BillingPlanCard`** (`settings/BillingPlanCard.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg plan card used at the top of both client + admin `/settings/billing`. Props: `tag` (rust-light mono string), `name` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust-light highlight, 26px headline), `meta` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = paper-bold), `action` (ReactNode тАФ typically a `Button`). The action slot is open so each role can use its own button styling (client uses a quiet secondary "Talk to Craig"; admin uses the rust primary "Change plan").
- **`InvoiceList`** (`settings/InvoiceList.tsx`) тАФ bordered table of invoice rows used on both billing tabs. Takes `invoices: Invoice[]` where `Invoice = { id, date, description, amount, status: 'paid' | 'pending' | 'failed' }`. Includes a mono header row + a per-status colour-coded status pill + a rust "PDF тЖУ" affordance per row. Re-exports `Invoice`.
- **`SecurityRow`** (`settings/SecurityRow.tsx`) тАФ bordered row used on the client Login + security tab (credentials + 2FA sections). Props: `heading`, optional `status: { tone: 'verified' | 'warn', label? }` (renders an inline dot-prefixed pill, good-green for verified, rust for warn/recommended), `description` (ReactNode), `action: { label, variant? }` (rendered through `Button`). Re-exports `SecurityRowStatus`.
- **`SessionRow`** (`settings/SessionRow.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` single active-session row in Login + security. Props: `icon` (emoji glyph), `device`, optional `isCurrent` (renders the rust "THIS DEVICE" pill and suppresses the revoke action), `meta` (mono ink-quiet metadata), `when` (right-aligned mono timestamp). Dotted bottom rule between rows, no rule on the last. Revoke opens a destructive `ConfirmDialog`; confirming collapses the row session-locally (not persisted тАФ no backend).
- **`SignOutOtherSessionsButton`** (`settings/SignOutOtherSessionsButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` "Sign out of all other sessions" trigger on `/settings/security`; owns a destructive `ConfirmDialog`. STUB тАФ confirming just dismisses (no backend).
- **`HelpFaqItem`** (`settings/HelpFaqItem.tsx`) тАФ collapsible FAQ entry on the Help tab. Uses native `<details>` for state (no JS), so it works in server components and degrades gracefully. Props: `question`, optional `answer` (ReactNode тАФ items without answers render as question-only, matching the prototype's "expand to see answer" UX), `defaultOpen`. The `+`/`тИТ` glyph toggles via `group-open:` Tailwind variants.
- **`TeamRow`** (`settings/TeamRow.tsx`) тАФ admin Team-tab member row. 5-column grid: avatar (rust-gradient circle) + name & email + role & sub-role + status pill (good for active, rust for pending тАФ dot-prefixed) + actions (mono action chips, with `tone: 'danger'` flipping the hover to warn-bg).
- **`ApiKeyRow`** (`settings/ApiKeyRow.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` admin API & services tab. 4-column grid: name + masked token, created mono meta, used mono meta, revoke action. Mono token uses JetBrains Mono. The created/used meta slots are `ReactNode` so callers can pass `<>Created <strong>21 Mar 2026</strong></>` for the ink-bold treatment. Revoke opens a destructive `ConfirmDialog`; confirming collapses the row session-locally (not persisted тАФ no backend).
- **`WebhookEventRow`** (`settings/WebhookEventRow.tsx`) тАФ single webhook-delivery log row. 3-column mono grid: time (quiet) + event name (rust bold) + status (right-aligned good for `ok`, warn for `failed`). `statusLabel` defaults to `тЬУ 200 OK` / `тЬЧ Failed` but is overridable.
- **`GenerateApiKeyModal`** (`settings/GenerateApiKeyModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` `Dialog` stub behind the `/settings/api` "+ Generate new key" button. Two phases: name `Input` тЖТ Generate reveals one stub `whk_live_тАж` token, shown once with a Copy affordance + warn line. STUB тАФ nothing persists; closing discards the key.
- **`GenerateApiKeyButton`** (`settings/GenerateApiKeyButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` trigger pairing a `Button` with `GenerateApiKeyModal` open state (same pattern as `ConnectIntegrationButton`), so `/settings/api` stays server-renderable.
- **`DangerRow`** (`settings/DangerRow.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` warn-tinted destructive-action row on the Danger zone tab. Props: `heading`, `description` (ReactNode), `action: { label, solid?, tone? }`. `solid: true` renders a filled destructive `Button`; otherwise `tone: 'neutral'` (ink-bordered, for non-destructive actions like Export) or `tone: 'destructive'` (warn-bordered, the default). Border + bg colour-coded across the whole row. The action opens a `ConfirmDialog` (destructive tone unless `tone: 'neutral'`); STUB тАФ confirming just dismisses (no backend).
- **`CapabilityToggleGrid`** (`settings/CapabilityToggleGrid.tsx`) тАФ admin-only `/settings/access` grid. Renders one card per client user (operators are excluded тАФ they have workspace-wide access through their role); inside each card, one row per website the user has access to; inside each row, a wrapping flex of `<Switch>`-with-label cells (one per capability). Role-default caps (currently just `viewBuilder` for clients) render as always-on disabled switches тАФ clients can't be revoked below their role floor. Props: `users: CapabilityToggleGridUser[]` (`{ id, displayName, email, role, websites: CapabilityGridWebsite[], capabilities: Set<Capability> }`), `onToggle: (userId, websiteId, capability, enabled) => void`. `CapabilityGridWebsite` is a minimal local display shape (`{ id, clientName, domain }`) тАФ decoupled from the full `Website` type so the grid doesn't pull in brand/version/page-tree fields it never reads. Callers (e.g. `/settings/access`) project from `Website` to this shape. Stateless тАФ the parent owns the grant store via `setUserGrant` on the user-stub context.
- **`ForcePublishLog`** (`settings/ForcePublishLog.tsx`) тАФ read-only audit log shown below the cap grid on `/settings/access`. 3-column grid (timestamp / event narrative / version id). Each row: mono timestamp, ink-bold actor + page + rust client name in the body, italic ink-mid reason quote, mono version id. Empty state renders a dashed-border card describing what the log will hold once force-publish actions begin firing. Props: `entries: ForcePublishEntry[]`.
- **`AccessClientRosterRow`** (`settings/AccessClientRosterRow.tsx`) тАФ single row in the `/settings/access` **agency-mode** client roster. 5-col grid (logo / name+meta / user count / caps-granted summary / drill-in button). Empty clients (no users) get a dimmed logo + paper-2 swatch + ghost "Open тЖТ" button; populated clients get rust-light glyph on ink + secondary "Drill in тЖТ" button. The button calls `onDrillIn(clientId)` which the page wires to `useWorkspace().setActiveClientId` тАФ clicking it switches workspace context and re-renders the page in sub-account mode.

### `shared/tickets/` тАФ tickets inbox + detail (Phase 5 sessions A + B)

> **Architectural note тАФ tickets lives outside the role route groups, same reason as settings.** Both roles need `/tickets` and `/tickets/[id]`, so `app/tickets/` lives at the top level with its own `layout.tsx` (`'use client'`, reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`). The inbox page (`app/tickets/page.tsx`) and the detail page (`app/tickets/[id]/page.tsx`) are both `'use client'` dispatchers тАФ per-role bodies live as `_admin-content.tsx` / `_client-content.tsx` siblings (same `_`-prefixed convention as `/settings/integrations`). `/tickets/new` is the ticket submit form тАФ a `page.tsx` Suspense wrapper over the `'use client'` `NewTicketForm` (`_form.tsx`); reached from the client inbox's "+ New ticket" CTA, the funnel-detail "Request a change" CTAs, and the page editor's request-change affordance (`?from=request-change` with field context тАФ see `lib/tickets/request-change.ts`). Submitting inserts a real `tickets` + `ticket_messages` row via `useCreateTicket` (Phase 3), then routes to `/tickets`. The `[id]` segment matches any non-`new` slug тАФ it is the ticket's display `reference` (`TKT-NNNN`); the detail pages fetch by it (`lib/tickets/queries.tsx`).

**Inbox (session A):**

- **`TicketsHero`** (`tickets/TicketsHero.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg rust-tagged hero band at the top of both `/tickets` pages. Props: `tag` (mono pill string), `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust highlight, 30px headline), `subtitle` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = paper-bold), `right` (ReactNode slot тАФ client passes a "+ New ticket" `Button`; admin passes a row of `TicketsHeroStat`s). Standalone тАФ NOT extracted into an `InkHero` primitive (see parked decisions). Sibling export **`TicketsHeroStat`** renders one of the admin hero's right-aligned numbers + mono label, with `tone: 'warn' | 'rust' | 'neutral'` controlling the `<em>` colour.
- **`TicketTabsBar`** (`tickets/TicketTabsBar.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` pill-tab strip with optional counts. Active tab = ink-bg paper-text rounded-full + count chip on paper/15; inactive = ink-quiet text + count chip on ink/8. Props: `tabs: TicketTab[]` + `defaultActiveId?`. Local `useState` active state тАФ fine for the stub layer; lift when real filtering wires up.
- **`CategoryTile`** (`tickets/CategoryTile.tsx`) тАФ colored mono-glyph square used in the client-variant `TicketRow` as the left-cell category indicator. 6 categories ├Ч 6 colors (websiteтЖТrust, marketingтЖТinfo, campaignsтЖТplum, reviewsтЖТamber, billingтЖТgood are all Webnua palette tokens; `other` still uses inline `#5a5a5a` тАФ flag if a third use lands and we'll tokenise that too). `size: 'sm' | 'md'` (md is the row size; sm available for tighter contexts).
- **`pills.tsx`** (`tickets/pills.tsx`) тАФ four small pill primitives exported together so all status/category/urgency colour decisions live in one file: **`StatusPill`** (open/in_progress/blocked/done with `reviewAware` flag тАФ when true, `in_progress` + `awaiting === 'client'` renders as a rust-outlined "Review" pill; optional `label` overrides the default text for e.g. "Open ┬╖ awaiting your reply" in the detail header), **`UrgencyPill`** (rush/soon/none), **`CategoryPill`** (admin row's pill-style category cell), **`AttentionPill`** (rust-filled "Reply needed" / "Draft ready"). Webnua-authored тАФ uses Webnua palette tokens directly (not `Badge`, which keeps shadcn role vocab).
- **`TicketRow`** (`tickets/TicketRow.tsx`) тАФ the single canonical row, discriminated by `variant: 'client' | 'admin'`. Both variants are `next/link` rows with shared "needs attention" treatment (left rust rail + faint rust bg) тАФ converged from the prototype's `.attention` (client) and `.unread` (admin) variants per the agreed unification. Client variant: `auto 1fr auto auto auto` grid тАФ `CategoryTile` + title+preview (with inline `AttentionPill` when `awaiting === 'client'`) + category label + `StatusPill reviewAware` + age. Admin variant: `20px 180px 1fr 110px 120px 110px 80px` grid тАФ checkbox + client mini-card (tone-tinted avatar + name + mono meta) + title+preview + `CategoryPill` + `StatusPill` + `UrgencyPill` + age. Re-exports `TicketRowProps`, `ClientTicketRowProps`, `AdminTicketRowProps`.

**Detail (session B):**

- **`TicketDetailLayout`** (`tickets/TicketDetailLayout.tsx`) тАФ 2-column grid wrapper for the detail page: `1fr 320px`, items-start, gap-4.5. Wraps `main` in a bordered white card (rounded-[14px], border-ink/8); the right `side` column is a plain flex-col so each `RailCard` carries its own surface. Used by both role detail-content files.
- **`TicketDetailHeader`** (`tickets/TicketDetailHeader.tsx`) тАФ sits at the top of the detail main card. Renders a `next/link` back button + pills row (slot тАФ caller composes `TicketIdLabel` + `CategoryPill` + `StatusPill` + `UrgencyPill`) + 24px ink title (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust) + optional `meta` line (ReactNode, `<strong>` = ink-bold; admin uses this slot to inline a client mini-avatar + "From X" line). Sibling export **`TicketIdLabel`** renders the TKT-0247 mono semibold label тАФ kept inline because it's just decorated text, not a pill.
- **`TicketThreadMessage`** (`tickets/TicketThreadMessage.tsx`) тАФ single message bubble: 36px avatar + bubble with author header (name + role chip + time) + body. `author: 'client' | 'operator'` toggles the surface (paper-2 + ink for client, ink + paper for operator). `children` is the bubble body тАФ pass `<p>...</p>` paragraphs. Same component handles both prototypes' message shapes (the client `.ctd-msg` and admin `.td-msg` markup converged 1:1).
- **`TicketReply`** (`tickets/TicketReply.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` reply composer: optional mono `label` ("// Reply to Craig" on client; admin omits), optional `chips` (click-to-fill quick-reply buttons above the textarea тАФ client only), `Textarea` (auto-resizing, paper card on paper-2 bg), tools row + `Button` send. `tools: { icon, title }[]` lets each role supply its own toolbar (client: attach/image/voice; admin: attach/link/template). Defaults to a single attach tool if omitted. The chip-to-textarea population is local state тАФ wire to real send when backend lands.
- **`TicketStatusCard`** (`tickets/TicketStatusCard.tsx`) тАФ discriminated by `mode: 'display' | 'pick'`. **Display** renders a static `<em>Open</em> ┬╖ awaiting your reply` headline (statusLabel is ReactNode so the caller wraps the highlighted word in `<em>` for rust-light) + an ink-bg dot + optional description paragraph. **Pick** renders an interactive list of `{ status, label }` options with a rust-light `тЬУ` on the active row; local `useState` tracks active (lift when real status mutation wires up). Both modes use `RailCard tone="dark"` underneath. (The card wrapper + property row are the shared `RailCard` / `RailPropertyRow` тАФ see the `shared/` rail-primitives entry below.)
- **`TicketActionRow`** (`tickets/TicketActionRow.tsx`) тАФ single icon+label row. Bordered ghost (`border-ink/10 тЖТ border-rust` on hover). Renders a `next/link` when `href` is set, else a `<button>` (`onClick`); `disabled` drops it to an inert `opacity-55` state. Rows auto-space with `mt-1.5` (first row resets via `first:mt-0`).
- **`TicketActionList`** (`tickets/TicketActionList.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` wrapper that renders a ticket's `TicketDetailAction[]` as `TicketActionRow`s and dispatches each by `kind`: `link` тЖТ routed `TicketActionRow`; `confirm` тЖТ opens a shared `ConfirmDialog` (owns the open state; `confirm.thenHref` routes via `useRouter` on confirm); `inert` тЖТ a disabled row (honestly-neutralized actions with no backend тАФ currently Edit original request / Add a reference file / Add internal note / Convert to subtasks). Both ticket-detail content files (`app/tickets/[id]/_*-content.tsx`) render `<TicketActionList actions={t.actions} />` inside the `// Actions` / `// Quick actions` `RailCard`. `TicketDetailAction` (`lib/tickets/client-detail.ts`) is the `kind`-discriminated union it consumes.

### `client/` тАФ client-shell-only composed components

- **`ClientSidebar`** (`ClientSidebar.tsx`) тАФ thin composition: `SidebarBrand` + `ClientWorkspaceCard` + `clientNav` rendered through `SidebarSectionLabel` + `SidebarItem` + `ClientSupportCard` + `SidebarUser`. Pulls data from `src/lib/nav/client-nav.ts`.
- **`ClientWorkspaceCard`** (`ClientWorkspaceCard.tsx`) тАФ rust-tinted single-workspace identity block that sits below the brand in the client sidebar. Props: `initial`, `name`, `status`. The status renders with a small good-green dot prefix.
- **`ClientSupportCard`** (`ClientSupportCard.tsx`) тАФ "// Managed by тАж" support block above the user footer. Takes a `contact: { label, org, description, ctaLabel, ctaHref }` prop тАФ the contact is config, not hardcoded, because the support contact will change.

### `client/dashboard/` тАФ client dashboard (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 7 ┬╖ Screen 1)

> The client home тАФ client `/dashboard`. Like the operator hub it is **pure assembly**: `app/dashboard/_client-content.tsx` composes these four dashboard-specific components with reused ones (`PageHeader`, `StatCard`, `MiniTrendBars`, `ActivityFeed`, and the shared `FunnelConversionBars`). The route dispatcher (`app/dashboard/page.tsx`) renders this for client-role users; admin role dispatches to the agency roster / hub.

- **`ClientDashboardHero`** (`dashboard/ClientDashboardHero.tsx`) тАФ the urgent ink-hero at the top of the client dashboard (Screen 1). Built on the `lib/ink-hero.ts` recipe. Big 84px rust-light callback count + label + a sub-line **composed from the structured `callouts`** (`{ name, age, note }[]`) тАФ never a stored sentence + an inbox CTA `Button`. Takes `hero: DashboardUrgentHero`. The `threshold` field drives the mono tag (`overdue` тЖТ `// NEEDS YOU NOW`).
- **`DashboardQueueCard`** (`dashboard/DashboardQueueCard.tsx`) тАФ a queue card: header (heading + count `Badge` + link) over a list of avatar rows (inner `QueueItemRow`). Used twice on the dashboard тАФ follow-ups due and today's jobs. Each `DashboardQueueItem` carries an avatar `initial` + optional `avatarTone` (`good`/`rust`), title, sub, optional inline `tag` (`urgent`/`done`/`next` colour key), time, and optional `href` (whole row links). Takes `queue: DashboardQueue`.
- **`LandingSnapshotCard`** (`dashboard/LandingSnapshotCard.tsx`) тАФ the landing-page snapshot: card header (domain + status meta) over a 4-up grid of reused `StatCard`s. Takes `snapshot: LandingSnapshot`.
- **`FunnelSummaryBand`** (`dashboard/FunnelSummaryBand.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg strip below the funnel bars. Composes plain prose from the structured `ClientFunnelSummary` (weak-point transition + drop count + operator note + health note) + a rust mono CTA. **Sibling of the operator hub's `HubInsightBand`, not a reuse** тАФ that component consumes a structured `FunnelInsight` (severity + suggested-action); the client framing is plainer and carries an operator-note slot instead. Two clean siblings beat one component with conditional slots.

### `client/notifications/` тАФ notification feed panel (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 3 ┬╖ Session 5 ┬╖ client Screen 10)

> The client notification bell + feed popover. Client-only тАФ the admin notification surface is not built. Mounted automatically inside `Topbar` for client-role users (see the `Topbar` entry above); no per-page wiring. **Wired to live data** тАФ the feed reads the `notifications` table and read-state **persists** through the `notification_reads` join (`useMarkNotificationsRead`); `NotificationBell`'s `Set<string>` is only an optimistic overlay for instant feedback ahead of the query invalidation. New notifications arrive live via `RealtimeProvider` (Phase 9). The footer "View all notifications" link from the prototype is intentionally **not** built (no `/notifications` route) тАФ the footer renders an inert caught-up line instead.

- **`NotificationBell`** (`notifications/NotificationBell.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'`. The 36px paper-2 bell button with a rust unread dot (shown while unread count > 0) + the popover. Owns `open` state + a `Set<string>` optimistic-read overlay; renders `NotificationPanel` in a `top-right`-anchored absolute popover with a fixed transparent click-catcher to dismiss (no Popover primitive exists; `Dialog` is the wrong shape). Reads the feed via `useNotifications`; marking read persists via `useMarkNotificationsRead`.
- **`NotificationPanel`** (`notifications/NotificationPanel.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'`. The card: ink header (title + "Mark all read" + тЪЩ link to `/settings/notifications`) + tab strip (All / Unread / Leads / Bookings / Reviews тАФ counts on All + Unread) + scrollable list (`max-h-[460px]`) + the inert footer line. Owns active-tab local state; filters the items by tab. Stateless about read-state тАФ the parent owns it.
- **`NotificationItemRow`** (`notifications/NotificationItemRow.tsx`) тАФ single feed row. `36px 1fr 70px` grid: kind-tinted icon glyph (`lead`тЖТrust-softтЬЙ / `review`тЖТamberтШЕ / `auto`тЖТinfoтд┐ / `booking`тЖТgoodтЦд / `alert`тЖТwarn!) + title (ReactNode, inline `<strong>`) + action chips + relative time. Unread rows get a rust-soft bg + a left rust dot. Action chips: `Mark read` chips call `onMarkRead`; chips with `href` are `next/link`s; others are inert stubs.

### `shared/funnels/` тАФ conversion-bar funnel

- **`FunnelConversionBars`** (`funnels/FunnelConversionBars.tsx`) тАФ six horizontal conversion bars (Landing visits тЖТ тАж тЖТ Reviewed), each a gradient bar scaled by `pct` + count + pct. Header carries a reused `FunnelPeriodToggle`. Distinct from `FunnelFlow` (3-step cards) and `CampaignTrendChart` (grouped bars). Takes `funnel: HubFunnelConversion`. **Promoted from `admin/hub/` to `shared/` in Cluster 7** (second-surface trigger тАФ the operator hub Screen 20 and the client dashboard Screen 1 both use it).

### `admin/` тАФ admin-shell-only composed components

- **`AdminSidebar`** (`AdminSidebar.tsx`) тАФ thin composition: `SidebarBrand` + `Overview` section + `AdminClientPicker` + `Workspace` section + `AdminWorkspaceBlock` + `SidebarUser`. Pulls data from `src/lib/nav/admin-nav.ts` + `admin-clients.ts`.
- **`AdminClientPicker`** (`AdminClientPicker.tsx`) тАФ collapsible client switcher in the admin sidebar. **Wired to the workspace context** (see `lib/workspace/workspace-stub.tsx`): closed state shows the active sub-account OR the agency-mode "All clients тЧЖ" identity; open state lists an "All clients ┬╖ agency birds-eye" entry first (rust-active when in agency mode), then every client (rust-active when that's the active sub-account), then "Add new client" + "View all clients". Clicking a client calls `setActiveClientId`; clicking the agency entry calls `clearActiveClient`. Takes `clients: AdminClient[]` (no `activeClientId` prop тАФ pulled from context).
- **`AdminWorkspaceBlock`** (`AdminWorkspaceBlock.tsx`) тАФ **static block**, not a selector. There's only one workspace ("Webnua") for now. Renders `// Workspace` label + workspace name above the user footer. Grow into a real selector if multi-workspace lands.
- **`ContinueSetupHero`** (`ContinueSetupHero.tsx`) тАФ admin-dashboard "mid-setup" hero card. White surface with rule border, `rounded-3xl`, `px-10 py-9`, two-column grid (content + right-aligned CTA). Props: `tag` (rust mono eyebrow), `title` (ReactNode, supports `<em>` for rust), `description`, `meta` (`ReactNode[]` тАФ segments are separated by `┬╖` and any `<strong>` renders ink-bold), `ctaLabel`, `ctaHref` (rendered through `Button asChild` + `next/link`). Lives in the operator dashboard; admin-only тАФ no client analogue.
- **`ClientListRow`** (`ClientListRow.tsx`) тАФ admin-dashboard live-client row. White card surface, `rounded-lg`, 6-column grid (`32px 1fr 120px 100px 120px 80px`). Composes a 32├Ч32 ink-bg avatar tile with a rust-light glyph, name + meta lines, a status-dot pill (`good`=live, `rust`=setup), `leadsPerWeek` (rust number), `spend`, and a rust "Open тЖТ" affordance. Whole row is a `next/link`. Props: `{ id, initial, name, meta, status: 'live'\|'setup', leadsPerWeek, spend, href }`. Re-export `ClientStatus` type. Will be reused on the future "all clients" admin list.

### `admin/hub/` тАФ single-client overview hub (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ Session 1b)

> The hub is admin sub-account `/dashboard` (Screen 20). It is **pure assembly** тАФ `_hub-content.tsx` composes these hub-specific components with reused ones (`WorkspaceContextBanner`, `RailCard`, `CalendarTodayPanel`, `ActivityFeed`, `StatCard`, `MiniTrendBars`, `FunnelPeriodToggle`, and the now-shared `FunnelConversionBars`). The client dashboard (Screen 1) is the parallel Cluster 7 build тАФ see `client/dashboard/` below.

- **`ClientHubHero`** (`hub/ClientHubHero.tsx`) тАФ the hub's ink hero. First consumer of the `lib/ink-hero.ts` recipe. Renders the rust status tag + client name + identity facts + composed management line + the big lead-focal block (count + breakdown + CTA) + a 4-tile 7-day stat strip. Takes `hero: HubHero`.
- **`OperatorActionBar`** (`hub/OperatorActionBar.tsx`) тАФ the `// OPERATOR ACTIONS` bar at the top of the hub. Operator-only chrome тАФ mono label + action chips (Edit page / Manage automations / Edit ad campaign / Billing / Impersonate) + a "viewing as operator" note. Each chip is an `OperatorAction` typed by `kind` (vision ┬з7). Takes `actions: OperatorAction[]`.
- **`HubInsightBand`** (`hub/HubInsightBand.tsx`) тАФ thin ink-bg insight strip at the foot of the hub. Composes its sentence from `FunnelInsight` parts (severity lead + reasoning + action). Built as a thin sibling rather than reusing `CampaignManagedBand` тАФ that component's 56px-icon-tile shape is chunkier than this one-line strip, so reuse would have fought (evaluate-at-build outcome). Takes `insight: FunnelInsight` + `cta`.

### `admin/integrations/` тАФ cross-client integrations matrix (Phase 5 session B)

Components for the operator's cross-client integrations matrix тАФ workspace-wide view across every client's *business* integrations (GBP / Meta / GA4 / Google Ads). The matrix has **no standalone route**: it renders inside `/settings/integrations` agency mode (`app/settings/integrations/_admin-content.tsx` тЖТ `AgencyIntegrationsView`) as the cross-client overview + the two nudge cards + the agency connection-policy section (the former `/settings/integration-defaults`, folded in here). Integrations is no longer a sidebar item тАФ it is reached via the Settings tab. Platform plumbing (Stripe / Resend / Twilio / Anthropic / Vercel) is NOT here тАФ it lives on `/settings/api`.

- **`IntegrationMatrixHero`** (`integrations/IntegrationMatrixHero.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg hero with rust-tagged pill + 28px headline + subtitle + N right-aligned stat tiles. Props: `tag` (mono string), `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust), `subtitle` (ReactNode), `stats: MatrixHeroStat[]` where each stat is `{ num: ReactNode, label: string, tone?: 'good' | 'warn' | 'bad' | 'neutral' }`. `num` is a ReactNode so callers can pass `<em>14</em>` to colour-key the number against the tone. Different shape from the client-side `IntegrationProgressHero` (stat tiles vs single fraction) тАФ kept as a sibling component on purpose.
- **`IntegrationMatrix`** (`integrations/IntegrationMatrix.tsx`) тАФ the table itself. Header bar with title + filter chips, then a `220px + repeat(N, 1fr) + 100px` grid of column headers and per-client rows. Each cell is a coloured circle (`connected` = good check, `warning` = warn `!`, `missing` = dashed-border `├Ч`). The Setup column holds a mini fraction + progress bar tinted by progress level (good = full, warn = тЙе50%, bad = <50%). Avatars use `MatrixClientAvatarTone` (`voltline`/`freshhome`/`keyhero`/`flowline`/`generic`) тАФ colours come from the prototype's per-client brand swatches. Re-exports `MatrixCellStatus`, `MatrixIntegrationColumn`, `MatrixClientRow`, `MatrixClientAvatarTone`, `MatrixFilter`.
- **`IntegrationMatrixActionCard`** (`integrations/IntegrationMatrixActionCard.tsx`) тАФ the right-rail action cards under the matrix ("Needs your attention", "Critical gaps"). Props: `heading`, `badge: { label, tone: 'warn' | 'info' }`, `description` (ReactNode), `items: ActionItem[]`, optional `tone: 'attention'` to flip to the warn-tinted gradient background. Each `ActionItem` is `{ id, clientInitial, clientTone?, text, cta }` тАФ `clientTone` is a Tailwind bg class (e.g. `'bg-rust'`) for the avatar tile. Re-exports `ActionItem`. `'use client'` тАФ each item's CTA fires a fire-and-forget client notification (reauth request / setup nudge); the stub tracks sent items in local state so the button settles into a disabled "Sent тЬУ" rather than staying inertly re-clickable.

### `admin/tickets/` тАФ admin-only ticket-inbox extras (Phase 5 session A)

> The admin inbox's client filter is the shared `FilterChips` (client chips derived from the tickets' own clients) + an `Input` search box, composed directly in `app/tickets/_admin-content.tsx` тАФ the same pattern as the admin leads inbox. The former decorative `AdminTicketsFilterBar` (non-functional `active`/`available` label chips) was deleted once real filtering landed.

### `shared/builder/` тАФ generic form primitives (Phase 5)

> **Architectural note тАФ generic by design.** Role-agnostic form-row primitives. Used by the website Q&A generation flow (`/website/new`) and the section-registry `Fields` components. Don't bake role-isms in. *(The 8-step onboarding wizard that originally used these тАФ and `BuilderLayout` / `PreviewPanelBar` тАФ was sunset; see the `clients/` create-client section below.)*

- **`BuilderStepHeader`** (`builder/BuilderStepHeader.tsx`) тАФ step header: rust mono `eyebrow` (string) + 40px Inter Tight `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust) + optional `subtitle` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = ink-bold). Same shape as `PageHeader`, spaced for sequential step rhythm (`mb-7`).
- **`BuilderFooterActions`** (`builder/BuilderFooterActions.tsx`) тАФ bottom-of-form Back/Continue row. Props: `progress` (mono uppercase label, ReactNode, `<strong>` = ink) + `actions` (ReactNode тАФ typically two `Button`s) + `bordered: boolean` (default `true` тАФ adds the `mt-9 border-t pt-5` rhythm; pass `false` when the footer sits outside a form panel).
- **`BuilderField`**, **`BuilderInput`**, **`BuilderTextarea`**, **`BuilderFormSection`**, **`BuilderFormRow`** (`builder/BuilderField.tsx`) тАФ the form-row toolkit. `BuilderField` wraps label + input + optional helper; supports an optional `hint` slot on the same line as the label (right-aligned, rule-coloured). `BuilderInput` / `BuilderTextarea` carry a `variant: 'default' | 'ai'` knob тАФ `'ai'` swaps to the rust-soft fill + rust border for AI-drafted fields. `BuilderFormSection` is a section block with a dotted-rule separator (auto-suppressed on last). `BuilderFormRow` is a `grid-cols-2 gap-3` pair-row for two side-by-side fields.
- **`AIPill`** (`builder/AIPill.tsx`) тАФ small `тЬж AI-DRAFTED` chip used inline inside `BuilderField` labels. Rust-on-rust-soft, mono `text-[9px]`, the тЬж glyph lives in the `::before` so the children slot is free for any label override.

### `admin/` тАФ create-client flow (Phase 6 ┬╖ post-cluster)

> **The canonical client-creation flow.** A new client business is created through `CreateClientModal` тАФ a seven-step modal (business тЖТ offer тЖТ brief тЖТ funnel-offer тЖТ design тЖТ build тЖТ review) that captures one brief, presents a final read-only summary, runs the website / funnel generators, persists the client + brand + website + funnel to Supabase (`lib/clients/create-client.ts`), and routes to `/clients/new/result` where the generated work renders as live previews with "Open in editor" links into `/website` and `/funnels`. The 8-step `/clients/new/<step>` onboarding wizard was sunset (it was a stub-era duplicate) тАФ `/clients/new` now just hosts the `CreateClientButton`. See `builder-design.md ┬з5` (SUPERSEDED banner).

- **`CreateClientButton`** (`admin/CreateClientButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` trigger pairing a `Button` with `CreateClientModal` open state (same pattern as `AddBookingButton`). Mounted on `/clients/new` and the sidebar `AdminClientPicker`'s "Add new client" entry.
- **`CreateClientModal`** (`admin/CreateClientModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` `Dialog`-based seven-step create flow (business тЖТ offer тЖТ brief тЖТ funnel-offer тЖТ design тЖТ build тЖТ **review** тЖТ generate). The brief is captured once; the website / funnel checkboxes on the build step decide which generators run. The design step captures **1тАУ3 brand colours** via a colour picker (`BrandObject.brandColors`; `accentColor` = the first) тАФ the generator themes sections from this palette. The brief step captures **funnel-specific inputs** тАФ `funnel_service` / `funnel_customer_pain` / `funnel_guarantee` (required text) + `funnel_testimonials` (gated behind a "Not yet / Yes, I have some" choice тАФ defaults to "Not yet" so the testimonial editor stays collapsed for the common case and only mounts when the user opts in; the funnel renders a "your reviews will appear here" placeholder when none are provided). The **funnel-offer** step runs the Sonnet-backed offer generator (`/api/generate-offer`) on click and renders the four resulting fields (`headline` / `promise` / `riskReversal` / `ctaText`) as editable inputs тАФ the user can regenerate, edit, or continue without an offer. The **review** step (UX polish pass) is a final read-only summary card-per-section with `Edit тЬО` affordances that jump back to the relevant step; the prominent "тЬж Generate my site тЖТ" CTA fires from here, not from build. **Polish chrome:** the header carries a segmented progress bar (one notch per step, rust-filled up to current) plus a `Step N of M ┬╖ {step name}` label; the body content is keyed on `phase` and runs `animate-in fade-in-0 duration-200` so steps fade between transitions; while generating, the form chrome (Cancel / Back / Continue) is unmounted and `GenerationSplash` (see next entry) takes the body. If generation fails the modal lands back on **review** with the error inline so the user sees their answers alongside the failure and can adjust before retrying. On success it calls `lib/clients/create-client.ts` (Supabase insert of `clients` + `brands` + `websites` + `funnels`) and routes to the result viewer.
- **`GenerationSplash`** (`admin/GenerationSplash.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` timed splash that replaces the previous single-spinner waiting state while `createClientWithGeneration` runs. Six hardcoded stages with per-stage `setTimeout` durations (~50s total before the final stage parks): Reading your brief тЖТ Selecting page layouts тЖТ Writing home page copy тЖТ Drafting about and services pages тЖТ Building your funnel тЖТ Almost ready. Final stage parks indefinitely тАФ the modal unmount on success/failure is what ends the splash, so the UI never claims done before the API call resolves. Visual: paper-cream bg, central spinner with rust тЬж glyph, mono `// Generating` eyebrow + the per-stage list as a checklist (done = good-tick struck-through, active = rust-soft pill + pulsing rust dot, pending = quiet). **Not** tied to real progress events тАФ real streaming is a separate later session; until then this is an honest reassurance pattern, not a fake progress bar (no percentage, no claim of "real progress"). Hardcoded timings approximate the real generator's latency; if the API resolves before/after a stage boundary the splash unmounts cleanly either way.
- **`lib/clients/create-client.ts`** тАФ the Supabase write path: resolves the signed-in operator via `supabase.auth.getUser()`, inserts the client + brand + website + funnel and their draft versions. The funnel insert now carries the four funnel-brief columns (`funnel_service` / `funnel_customer_pain` / `funnel_guarantee` / `funnel_testimonials`) тАФ required-when-`wantFunnel` guarded at the data layer so a direct API caller can't write a half-briefed funnel тАФ **plus `funnel_offer`** (jsonb, snake_case keys: `headline` / `promise` / `risk_reversal` / `cta_text`) when the wizard ran offer generation. **Generation:** the website is generated via `generateSiteStub` тЖТ the real Claude-backed `/api/generate-site` route (falls back to the deterministic generator when `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is unset or the call fails). The funnel is now also generated via Claude тАФ `generateFunnelStub` тЖТ the real `/api/generate-funnel` route (one Opus call for the seven-section landing step in the Sultanic / Suby shape, driven by the chosen offer + brief + testimonials), with the same `503` тЖТ deterministic-fallback pattern.
- **`lib/website/offer-generate.ts`** тАФ browser-side caller for `/api/generate-offer`. `generateFunnelOffer(input)` (`{ industry, serviceArea, funnelService, funnelCustomerPain, funnelGuarantee }`) тЖТ `FunnelOffer` (`{ headline, promise, riskReversal, ctaText }`). **Fallback policy diverges from `site-generation-stub.ts`:** `503` (key unset) **throws** `AppError.validation` rather than degrading to a deterministic stub тАФ a stub four-field offer would be misleading (the whole point of the step is a real Sonnet draft), and the user can edit any field after generation, so producing nothing is more honest than producing fake. `500` throws `AppError.unexpected` with the server's `{ name, status, detail }`. `offerToRow(offer)` maps the camelCase `FunnelOffer` to the snake_case shape persisted in `funnels.funnel_offer`. Also exports `enhanceFunnelOfferText` тАФ the offer-paragraph polish caller for `/api/enhance-offer`.
- **`lib/website/field-enhance.ts`** тАФ browser-side caller for `/api/enhance-field`. `enhanceField({ fieldName, currentValue, briefContext? })` тЖТ `string`. Same `AppError`-on-503 / `AppError`-on-500 contract as `enhanceFunnelOfferText`. Generic across freeform fields тАФ the route's framing is "draw out specificity", and the per-field call site passes `fieldName` as a label the prompt uses to orient (e.g. `funnel_customer_pain` тЖТ the model reads it as the urgency-moment field).
- **`components/shared/EnhanceableTextarea`** тАФ `'use client'`. Textarea + тЬж Enhance with AI button + accept/reject preview. Generic over the enhancer: caller passes `enhance: (current: string) => Promise<string>` (so the offer field can pass `enhanceFunnelOfferText` and other freeform fields can pass `enhanceField`). On click: shows inline preview card with the AI-enhanced text + "Use this тЖТ" (replaces the textarea value) / "Keep mine" (discards). `minLength` default 8 disables enhance on too-thin input. Errors surface inline beneath the textarea in the wizard's warn-tinted treatment. See the parked decision below тАФ accept/reject is deliberate, not auto-replace.
- **`lib/website/site-generation-stub.ts`** тАФ the brief тЖТ website/funnel generation the modal runs. `generateSiteStub` calls the **real Claude-backed `/api/generate-site` route** and falls back to the deterministic `generateSiteSync` when the route is unconfigured (no `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`) or fails тАФ so the flow works with or without a key. `generateSiteSync` (deterministic, no I/O) is the dev/test path. (Funnel generation тАФ `lib/funnel/generation-stub.ts` `generateFunnelStub` тАФ is **also Claude-backed now** via `/api/generate-funnel`; falls back to `generateFunnelSync` on `503` / network error.)
- **`app/api/generate-site/route.ts`** тАФ `POST` route, the real website generator. Takes a `ClientBrief` + optional `clientId`, mints one `generation_id` uuid per run + shares it across all four parallel `generatePageLive` calls, returns a `SiteGenerationResult`. Returns `503` when `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is unset (the client then falls back), `400` on bad body, `500` with `{ name, status, detail }` on a real Claude failure (read by `site-generation-stub.ts` and surfaced in the modal). **Writes `generation_log` rows** (one per ┬з4.4 fallback field, via the service-role client тАФ RLS write check accommodates this per migration 0011 comment) тАФ fire-and-forget so observability never blocks the response, and gated on `clientId` since dev preview surfaces may run without a created client. Server-only тАФ the API key never reaches the browser.
- **`lib/website/generate-live.ts`** тАФ server-only. `generatePageLive(ctx, generationId?)` тАФ the real Claude call: `composePrompt(ctx)` тЖТ `claude-opus-4-7` (adaptive thinking, streamed) тЖТ defensively-parsed JSON тЖТ `assembleResult` (the same ┬з4.4 validation pipeline the deterministic stub uses). The optional `generationId` lets the route share one uuid across all per-page calls of a site-generation run so `generation_log` rows group cleanly; defaults to a fresh uuid when called standalone. Imported only by the route, so `@anthropic-ai/sdk` stays out of the client bundle. The prompt-construction layer (`generation-prompt.ts`) and the validation pipeline are unchanged тАФ this only swaps the section source from "recipe" to "model".

### `lib/nav/` тАФ nav + sidebar data (single source of truth for nav)

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `NavItem` (`{ label, href, icon, badge? }`) + `NavSection` + `SettingsNavItem` (`{ label, href, icon }`, no badge тАФ settings tabs don't carry one in either prototype).
- **`client-nav.ts`** тАФ `clientNav` (sections + items), `clientWorkspace`, `clientSupport` (used as the `contact` prop on `ClientSupportCard`), `clientUser`.
- **`admin-nav.ts`** тАФ `adminOverviewNav`, `adminWorkspaceNav` (Workspace section тАФ Leads / Tickets / Websites / **Funnels** (Session 7) / Internal automations / Campaigns / Reviews / Calendar / Settings, in that order тАФ Integrations is not a sidebar item; the cross-client matrix lives inside `/settings/integrations` agency mode), `adminWorkspace`, `adminUser`.
- **`admin-clients.ts`** тАФ `adminClients` (stubbed client list of 4 clients: Voltline / FreshHome / KeyHero / NeatWorks). The previous `adminActiveClientId` const was removed тАФ active client now lives in the reactive `WorkspaceProvider` context, not a hardcoded module export. Replace `adminClients` with backend data when wired.
- **`client-settings-nav.ts`** тАФ `clientSettingsNav` тАФ 7 tabs (Integrations / Profile / **Team** / Notifications / Billing / Login + security / Help). The Team tab (Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite) is net-new тАФ the client prototype has no team surface; it mirrors the operator `/settings/team` for symmetry.
- **`admin-settings-nav.ts`** тАФ `adminSettingsNav` тАФ the operator's **agency-mode** (HQ) set, 10 tabs (Workspace / Team / Access / Integrations / Billing / Plans / Defaults / Default seat limit / API & services / Danger zone). Default seat limit (Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 3) and Plans (Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 2) are the agency-policy surfaces. Integrations holds the cross-client matrix + the agency connection policy (the former standalone "Integration defaults" tab, folded in); API & services holds the platform plumbing + API keys + webhooks.
- **`sub-account-settings-nav.ts`** тАФ `subAccountSettingsNav` тАФ the operator's **sub-account-mode** set (drilled into one client), 8 tabs (Profile / Access / Team / Integrations / Notifications / SMS / Billing / Danger zone). SMS (Phase 7 Twilio) is the per-client alphanumeric sender provisioning surface. Access appears here AND in `adminSettingsNav` тАФ the one genuinely bi-modal surface.
- **`use-settings-nav.ts`** тАФ `useSettingsNav()` тАФ resolves the settings nav for the current role + workspace mode (client тЖТ `clientSettingsNav`; operator + agency тЖТ `adminSettingsNav`; operator + sub-account тЖТ `subAccountSettingsNav`). `SettingsNav` consumes this; no tab page hard-codes a nav set.
