### `lib/dashboard/` тАФ per-role dashboard stub data

- **`admin-dashboard-types.ts`** тАФ operator-dashboard type shapes only: `DashboardStat`, `MidSetupClient`, `LiveClient`. `queries.tsx` maps live Supabase reads to them. (The former `dashboardGreeting` / `dashboardStats` / `midSetupClient` / `liveClients` data stubs were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)
- **`hub-types.ts`** тАФ the single-client overview hub's typed schema (admin Screen 20). Vision ┬з7 discipline: every field maps to a column or computed/templated value, nothing needs an LLM. Key shapes: `OperatorAction` (typed by `kind`), `ManagementState` (`{ primary, clientLastActiveDays, operatorName }` тАФ never composed prose), `HubHero` + `HubLeadFocal` + `HubHeroStat`, `HubContextCard`, `HubActivityEvent` (typed by `kind`), `HubWeeklyStat`, `HubFunnelConversion` + `HubFunnelStep`, `FunnelInsight` (`{ severity, target, suggestedAction, reasoning }`), and the top-level `ClientHub`. `schedule` reuses the calendar `CalendarTodayPanel` type.
- **`client-dashboard-types.ts`** тАФ the client dashboard's typed schema (client Screen 1). Same vision-┬з7 discipline as `hub-types.ts`. **Reuses `HubWeeklyStat` and `HubFunnelConversion` verbatim** тАФ the client "this week" trend + funnel bars are structurally identical to the hub's. New shapes for concepts that diverge structurally: `DashboardUrgentHero` (`{ count, threshold, label, callouts, cta }` тАФ `callouts: { name, age, note }[]`), `DashboardQueue` + `DashboardQueueItem` + `QueueItemTag`, `LandingSnapshot` + `LandingSnapshotStat`, `ClientFunnelSummary` (`{ weakPoint, operatorNote, healthNote, cta }` тАФ the client-framed sibling of `FunnelInsight`), and the top-level `ClientDashboard`.

### `lib/notifications/` тАФ notification feed data + types

> The client notification feed (client Screen 10). Distinct concern from `lib/settings/client-notifications.ts` тАФ that file is the per-channel notification *preferences*; this is the *feed* of fired events.

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `NotificationKind` (`lead | review | auto | booking | alert`), `NotificationTabId` (`all | unread | lead | booking | review`), `NotificationAction` (`{ label, href?, secondary? }`), `NotificationItem` (`{ id, kind, title: ReactNode, actions, time, read }`).
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ wired to live Supabase. `useNotifications()` reads the RLS-scoped `notifications` table + the `notification_reads` join; `useMarkNotificationsRead()` upserts read-state rows. Action chips are derived here from `kind` + `source_entity_*`, not stored.
- **Write path (Phase 9) тАФ DB triggers, not app code.** Nothing in the app inserts `notifications`; migration `0032_notification_write_path.sql` adds `AFTER INSERT` triggers on `leads` / `bookings` (one-off only) / `reviews` / `ticket_messages` (operator non-draft replies) that fan a notification to the client's users via the `private.notify_client_users` helper. All `SECURITY DEFINER` тАФ a fired notification is a system event, so it bypasses the operator-only `notifications_insert` RLS. Surface-agnostic: fires whatever inserts the row. `kind = 'auto'` has no honest source until Phase 8 (the messaging engine).

### `lib/realtime/` тАФ live query invalidation (Phase 9)

- **`RealtimeProvider`** (`realtime/RealtimeProvider.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'`. Mounted in the root layout (inside `WorkspaceProvider`). One Supabase Realtime channel per signed-in tab; `postgres_changes` events are RLS-scoped, so each subscription only delivers rows the user may see. On an event the matching React Query key is invalidated тАФ the surface refetches without a poll. Covers `notifications` (тЖТ `['notifications','feed']`), `tickets` + `ticket_messages` (тЖТ `['tickets']`). **Builder approval lanes** тАФ `website_approval_submissions` / `funnel_approval_submissions` / `website_versions` / `funnel_versions` changes fan a `BUILDER_EVENT` via `notifyBuilder()`, so every builder query refetches: a submitter's editor-lock banner clears when an operator resolves, and a freshly-published version surfaces on the detail / roster surfaces (editor-side + publication-side liveness). The website-approval surfaces here (the operator approvals queue, publish-state, pending-submission тАФ the surfaces B1 originally wired with targeted query-key invalidations, now unified under the event bus) all read through `useBuilderQuery`, so they already subscribe to `BUILDER_EVENT` тАФ the broad fan subsumes B1's per-key targeting. Holds no context тАФ runs the effect, passes children through. `notifications` / `tickets` / `ticket_messages` joined the `supabase_realtime` publication in migration `0032`; the four builder tables in migration `0046`.

### `lib/settings/` тАФ per-tab stub data for `/settings/*`

- **`client-profile.ts`** тАФ `clientProfileBusiness` + `clientProfileManagedByWebnua` field-row lists for the client Profile tab.
- **`admin-workspace.ts`** тАФ `adminWorkspaceFields` + `adminWorkspacePlanFields` for the admin Workspace tab (the Workspace ID row carries `mono: true` so the value renders in JetBrains Mono).
- **`client-integrations.tsx`** тАФ `clientIntegrationsHero` (props for `IntegrationProgressHero`) + `clientIntegrations` (the 5 integration cards Voltline sees on `/settings/integrations`). `.tsx` because description / meta / hero copy carry inline `<em>` / `<strong>` JSX.
- **`platform-services.tsx`** тАФ `adminPlatformServices` тАФ the 5 platform-plumbing services the agency runs (Stripe, Resend, Twilio, Anthropic, Vercel), rendered as `IntegrationCard`s on `/settings/api` ("API & services"). Distinct from the *business* integrations each client connects per sub-account. `.tsx` for the JSX-in-description reason.
- **`client-notifications.ts`** тАФ `clientNotifications: NotificationGroup[]` (Leads / Bookings / Reviews / Summary emails тАФ each with channel set + per-row default state) + `clientQuietHours` (enabled flag + window string).
- **`client-billing.tsx`** + **`admin-billing.tsx`** тАФ plan card props + payment method + invoice list per role. Client billing has `clientBillingIncluded` (the "what's included" grid); admin doesn't. `.tsx` because plan headlines carry `<em>` highlights.
- **`client-security.ts`** тАФ `clientSecurityCredentials`, `clientSecurityTwoFactor`, `clientSecuritySessions` for the Login + security tab.
- **`client-help.tsx`** тАФ `clientHelpFaqs` (7 FAQ entries, only the first carries an answer + `defaultOpen: true` by default, matching the prototype) + `clientHelpRecentSupport`.
- **`admin-team.ts`** тАФ `adminTeamMembers` + `adminTeamPermissions` for the Team tab.
- **`admin-defaults.ts`** тАФ `adminDefaultsAutomations` (4 toggleable defaults) + `adminDefaultsBranding` + `adminDefaultsPricing` for the Defaults tab.
- **`admin-api.tsx`** тАФ `adminApiKeys`, `adminWebhookEndpoint`, `adminWebhookEvents` for the API & services tab (alongside the `platform-services.tsx` platform-plumbing list).
- **`admin-danger.tsx`** тАФ `adminDangerWorkspace` (4 entries) + `adminDangerClient` (1 entry) for the Danger zone tab.

### `lib/integrations/` тАФ cross-client integrations matrix data

- **`admin-matrix.tsx`** тАФ `adminMatrixHero`, `adminMatrixFilters`, `adminMatrixColumns` (the 5 integration column defs: GBP / Meta / GA4 / G.Ads / Stripe), `adminMatrixRows` (4 client rows ├Ч per-integration status cells + per-client progress), `adminMatrixAttention` + `adminMatrixGaps` (action-card items). `.tsx` because hero stats and action-item text carry inline JSX. Reshape into Supabase reads when the backend lands.

### `lib/env.ts` + `lib/integrations/_shared/` тАФ Phase 7 integration foundation

> The shared spine every Phase 7 integration is built on. Two integration architectures exist тАФ **platform-level** (Webnua owns the account: Stripe / Twilio / Resend / Vercel; one API key in env, per-customer state is "which sub-identity is assigned" тАФ Session 1) and **per-tenant OAuth** (the customer owns the account: GBP / Meta; Webnua OAuths in and stores per-tenant tokens тАФ Session 2). Google Ads is NOT built (operator decision). Full status: `reference/integration-foundation-audit.md`. Everything here is SERVER-ONLY (reads server secrets / the service-role client) тАФ the one client-safe exception is `lib/integrations/connections.ts`.

- **`lib/env.ts`** тАФ typed, zod-validated, boot-validated env module. Exports `env` тАФ a lazy `Proxy` that validates on first property access (lazy so `next build` doesn't trip; a missing *required* key throws a clear, actionable boot error), `validateEnv()` (called by `src/instrumentation.ts`'s `register()` hook to force validation at server boot), and `getAppBaseUrl()` (resolves `APP_BASE_URL` тЖТ `VERCEL_URL` тЖТ `https://{APP_HOST}`). The schema has a slot for every Phase 7 provider; integration keys are `.optional()` (a feature degrades gracefully when unset). **New server code reads `env.X` instead of `process.env.X`** тАФ existing accesses were deliberately not refactored, this just sets the pattern. `zod` is the one dependency Phase 7 adds (utility tier тАФ not a stack expansion).
- **`integrations/_shared/call.ts`** тАФ **`callExternal()`**, the single wrapper for every outbound integration call. Timeout (30s default), retry on 5xx + network errors with exponential backoff (3 attempts default), structured logging of every attempt to `integration_call_log`, error classification (`retryable` / `non_retryable` / `auth_failed` / `rate_limited`), returns a typed `IntegrationResult<T>` discriminated union (`{ ok, data, status } | { ok:false, error: IntegrationError }`). JSON-in/JSON-out by default; `rawBody` / `parseResponse` escape hatches for the non-JSON 20%. Request *headers* are never logged (auth tokens); body shapes are redacted (secret-looking keys blanked).
- **`integrations/_shared/retry.ts`** тАФ exponential-backoff helper. `computeBackoffDelay` + `sleep` (consumed by `callExternal`'s own loop), `withRetry` (the ad-hoc throwing-fn wrapper), `DEFAULT_RETRY_CONFIG` (3 attempts / 500ms base / 10s cap / full jitter).
- **`integrations/_shared/jobs.ts`** тАФ the async-jobs API over `integration_jobs`. `enqueueJob` (insert, returns id), `enqueueJobImmediate` (enqueue + fire-and-forget self-POST to the executor for near-instant runs; `pg_cron` is the safety net if that POST fails), `registerJobHandler` (an integration registers what processes a `job_type`), `runJob` (the executor body тАФ atomic claim `UPDATE тАж WHERE status='pending'` тЖТ handler тЖТ terminal status; requeues with backoff while attempts remain).
- **`integrations/_shared/db-types.ts`** тАФ hand-written row/insert types for the integration tables (`0047`тАУ`0055` are not yet in the generated `Database` type) + `getIntegrationDb()` (an untyped view of the service-role client). Includes `IntegrationConnectionRow`/`Insert` (Session 2). Drop once `src/lib/types/database.ts` is regenerated post-deploy.
- **`integrations/job-handler-manifest.ts`** тАФ side-effect manifest the executor route imports so handler registrations land in its module graph. Each integration adds one `import` line; Session 2 added the first тАФ `_shared/job-handlers.ts` (the `token_refresh_check` handler).
- **`app/api/internal/job-executor/route.ts`** тАФ `POST` route running one job by id. Internal-only: verifies the `x-webnua-internal-secret` header against `INTERNAL_JOB_SECRET` (constant-time compare); `503` when the secret is unset. Called by the `pg_cron` poller (migration `0049`) and by `enqueueJobImmediate`.
- **`lib/website/vercel.ts`** тАФ refactored in Session 1 to route every Vercel call through `callExternal()` (the foundation's first validation against a real integration). Reads creds via `env`; public behaviour (domain provisioning, 409/404 idempotency, `{ configured:false }` degradation) unchanged.

#### Per-tenant OAuth foundation (Phase 7 ┬╖ Session 2)

> The scaffolding both the GBP and Meta business sessions build on тАФ no business logic, just the OAuth layer. Two registered providers: `google_business_profile` (refresh_access token model) and `meta_ads` (long_lived model тАФ written but unverified against a live Meta app, `TODO(meta)` flagged). Migrations `0054`тАУ`0056`. **`callWithToken()` is the call path for every per-tenant API call.**

- **`lib/integrations/connections.ts`** тАФ the ONE client-safe module: `OAuthProviderId` (`google_business_profile` | `meta_ads`), `TokenModel`, `IntegrationConnectionStatus`, `isOAuthProviderId`, and `OAUTH_PROVIDER_DISPLAY` (operator-facing name / blurb / logo tone per provider). Imported by both the operator UI and the server registry.
- **`integrations/_shared/oauth-providers.ts`** тАФ server-only provider registry. Each provider declares its endpoints + `exchangeCode` / `refreshToken` / `revoke` / `fetchAccountId` (all through `callExternal()`). `getOAuthProvider(id)`, `isOAuthProviderConfigured(id)`.
- **`integrations/_shared/oauth.ts`** тАФ generic helpers: `generateAuthorizationUrl`, `exchangeCodeForTokens`, `buildRedirectUri`, and the HMAC-signed `state` token (`signOAuthState` / `verifyOAuthState` тАФ 15-min TTL; the OAuth CSRF defence + the only authenticated context carried into the callback).
- **`integrations/_shared/tokens.ts`** тАФ token management. Vault RPC wrappers; `storeConnection` (Vault-encrypt then write the row тАФ **Vault failure is fatal, no plaintext fallback**), `getAccessToken` (on-demand refresh, forked on `token_model` тАФ `refresh_access` re-mints from the Vault refresh token, `long_lived` extends the Vault secret in place), `revokeConnection`, `notifyTokenRefreshFailure` (throttled operator alert). Typed errors: `VaultUnavailableError` / `ConnectionNotFoundError` / `TokenExpiredError` / `TokenRefreshFailedError` / `TokenRevokedError`.
- **`integrations/_shared/api-call-with-token.ts`** тАФ **`callWithToken(clientId, provider, fetchFn)`** тАФ every per-tenant API call goes through this: fresh access token in, 401 тЖТ refresh-and-retry-once, marks the connection `refresh_failed` + throws `TokenRefreshFailedError` on a dead token. `fetchFn` itself uses `callExternal()`.
- **`integrations/_shared/operator-auth.ts`** тАФ two helpers. `requireOperatorForClient(request, clientId)`: bearer-token тЖТ operator role + accessible-client check (token-scoped client so the `clients` RLS scopes a junior operator); integration management as operator governance. **`requireClientAccess(request, clientId)`** (Phase 7 GBP UI consolidation): the looser variant тАФ accepts EITHER an operator path (same check) OR a client-role user whose `client_id` matches. **Used for every per-tenant OAuth provider** (both GBP and Meta Ads тАФ the third-party account belongs to the customer, so the customer may connect / disconnect / pick the working entity themselves OR the operator may do it on their behalf). `meta_ads/campaigns` is the only Meta route that still gates on `requireOperatorForClient` тАФ launching campaigns + flipping their status is operator governance under the managed-service model, distinct from owning the connection.
- **`integrations/_shared/job-handlers.ts`** тАФ registers `token_refresh_check` (daily cron, migration `0056`): proactively refreshes `long_lived` connections within 14 days of expiry; `refresh_access` connections need none (on-demand re-mint).
- **`integrations/use-connections.ts`** тАФ `'use client'` operator-UI data layer: `useClientConnections` (reads `integration_connections`, RLS-scoped), `connectIntegration` (POST connect тЖТ navigate to consent), `useDisconnectIntegration`.
- **`app/api/integrations/[provider]/connect|callback|disconnect/route.ts`** тАФ `connect` (POST, returns `{ authorizationUrl }` JSON тАФ not a 302, since it is `fetch`-ed with a bearer token; auth is `requireClientAccess` for every per-tenant OAuth provider so the customer may connect their own account OR the operator may connect on their behalf), `callback` (GET, verified by the signed state тАФ a provider redirect carries no auth header), `disconnect` (POST, same auth shape, revokes).
- **`components/shared/settings/IntegrationConnectionsSection.tsx`** тАФ operator "Connected accounts" panel on sub-account `/settings/integrations` тАФ per-provider status + Connect / Disconnect / Reconnect.

#### Per-tenant OAuth тАФ Google Business Profile setup

> Operator steps to make GBP connect work in a deployment. Meta setup is deferred to the Meta business session (no Meta app exists yet).

1. Create a Google Cloud project (or reuse one) at console.cloud.google.com.
2. Enable the **Google My Business / Business Profile APIs** (Account Management API + Business Information API) for the project.
3. Create an **OAuth 2.0 Client ID** (type: Web application). Register the authorized redirect URI: `{app origin}/api/integrations/google_business_profile/callback` (e.g. `https://app.webnua.com/api/integrations/google_business_profile/callback`) тАФ it must match byte-for-byte.
4. Apply for **OAuth app verification** тАФ the `business.manage` scope is a sensitive/restricted scope; production OAuth with it requires Google's verified-app review (configure the OAuth consent screen, submit for verification; allow weeks). Until verified, the app works only for test users added on the consent screen.
5. Set `GOOGLE_OAUTH_CLIENT_ID` / `GOOGLE_OAUTH_CLIENT_SECRET` in the deployment env (and `.env.local` for dev). `GOOGLE_OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI_BASE` is optional (defaults to `{app origin}/api/integrations`); `OAUTH_STATE_SECRET` is optional (falls back to the service-role key).
6. Meta: deferred тАФ leave the `META_*` env slots blank.

#### Stripe billing (Phase 7)

> Subscription billing for Webnua clients тАФ тВм299/month, charged monthly via
> Stripe. Built on the Session 1 platform-integration spine: every Stripe call
> goes through `callExternal()`, the payment-failed operator alert runs on the
> `integration_jobs` queue, posture is mirrored onto `client_stripe_customers`
> (extended by migration `0057`). Stripe owns the account (standard scope, no
> Connect). The marketing framing тАФ "тВм99 platform fee + тВм200 Meta ad credit" in
> month 1 тАФ is UI copy only; Stripe charges a flat тВм299 every month, and the ad
> credit is handled OUTSIDE Stripe by the Meta ads integration. Everything here
> is SERVER-ONLY except `use-billing.ts` (the `'use client'` UI data layer).

- **`lib/integrations/stripe/client.ts`** тАФ the typed Stripe API wrapper. `isStripeConfigured()`, `createCustomer` / `createCheckoutSession` / `createSubscription` / `cancelSubscription` / `getSubscription` / `createPortalSession`. Every call routes through `callExternal()` (timeout / retry / `integration_call_log`). Stripe takes `application/x-www-form-urlencoded` bodies (bracket-nested) and returns JSON тАФ the form encoder + `callExternal`'s `rawBody` escape hatch carry it. Every POST sends an `Idempotency-Key` header so `callExternal`'s 5xx/network retry cannot double-create. **PRODUCTION SWAP** flagged inline: test vs live is purely which keys are in the env тАФ no code change.
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/types.ts`** тАФ Stripe API object slices (typed defensively тАФ most fields optional) + the extended `client_stripe_customers` row type + `StripeBillingStatus` (`incomplete | active | past_due | cancelled | paused`).
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/customers.ts`** тАФ `client_stripe_customers` data access (read by client / by Stripe customer id, insert) + the webhook appliers (`applySubscriptionEvent` / `applyInvoicePaid` / `applyInvoiceFailed`) + the StripeтЖТour-schema mappers (`mapStripeStatus` total, `extractPeriodEnd` тАФ reads `current_period_end` from both the legacy top-level field and the per-item field, since Stripe API 2025-03-31+ moved it onto subscription items).
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/webhook-verify.ts`** тАФ `verifyStripeWebhook(rawBody, header, secret)` тАФ Stripe's signing scheme (`HMAC-SHA256` over `{t}.{body}`, v1-signature match, timestamp tolerance) implemented with `node:crypto`. Pure, no SDK.
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/billing-status.ts`** тАФ `isClientBillingActive(clientId)` (active or past_due) + `shouldGateClientAccess(clientId)` (cancelled, or past_due past the 7-day grace window). The contract the future access-control layer builds against. A client with no `client_stripe_customers` row is neither active nor gated тАФ "billing not set up" is not a cancellation.
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/plan-info.ts`** тАФ `getPlanInfo()` тАФ the plan's name / price / currency / interval resolved LIVE from the Stripe Price object (`STRIPE_PRICE_ID_STANDARD`, product expanded), via `callExternal()`, cached 5 minutes. **Stripe is the single source of truth for plan details тАФ the UI never hardcodes the price.** The optional "what's included" feature list is read from the Price's `features` metadata key (a JSON array of strings). Returns null when Stripe is unconfigured/unreachable тАФ callers must handle null, never substitute a fixed price. Server-only.
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/notify.ts`** тАФ `sendOperatorEmail` тАФ a MINIMAL inline Resend send (via `callExternal`) + a `notifications_outbound` write. Degrades to `'skipped'` (no fake row) when `RESEND_API_KEY` is unset. The full Resend integration is a separate session; route this through it when that lands.
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/job-types.ts`** + **`job-handlers.ts`** тАФ `STRIPE_PAYMENT_FAILED_JOB` (`stripe_payment_failed_notify`); the handler resolves the client name + every operator email and sends the payment-failed alert. Registered via the `job-handler-manifest.ts` side-effect import.
- **`lib/integrations/stripe/use-billing.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`. `useStripeBilling(clientId)` reads `client_stripe_customers` (RLS-scoped browser client, untyped cast) + `startStripeCheckout` / `openStripePortal` (POST the operator routes, navigate to the Stripe-hosted page) + `usePlanInfo()` (the live plan details, via the plan-info route) + `formatPlanPrice()` (a `PlanInfo` тЖТ "тВм299.00/month" label).
- **`app/api/integrations/stripe/plan-info/route.ts`** тАФ `GET`, unauthenticated (plan pricing is public тАФ shown at Checkout). The browser bridge to `getPlanInfo()`. Returns the live `PlanInfo`, or `503` when Stripe is unconfigured/unreachable. `Cache-Control: public, max-age=300` mirrors the server cache.
- **`app/api/integrations/stripe/checkout/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, operator-only (`requireOperatorForClient`). Resolves/creates the Stripe Customer + the `client_stripe_customers` row, creates a subscription Checkout Session, returns the Checkout URL. `409` when the client is already on an active/past_due subscription. Billing email resolves from `clients.primary_contact_email`, falling back to the client's owner user.
- **`app/api/integrations/stripe/portal/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, operator-only. Mints a Stripe Customer Portal session (update card / view invoices / cancel) and returns the portal URL. *(Not a separately-enumerated task deliverable тАФ required by the "Manage billing" affordance.)*
- **`app/api/integrations/stripe/webhook/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, signature-authenticated. Handles `customer.subscription.{created,updated,deleted}`, `invoice.payment_{succeeded,failed}`; `payment_failed` enqueues the operator alert. Every verified event + every rejected delivery logs to `integration_call_log` `direction='inbound'`. Returns 200 once verified+applied (including the untracked-customer no-op), 400 on a bad signature, 500 on a genuine processing error (Stripe retries тЖТ self-heal).
- **`components/shared/settings/StripeSubscriptionSection.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`. The "Subscription & payment" panel тАФ the ONLY section on sub-account `/settings/billing` (Stripe is the real billing). Shows status / next renewal / last payment; "Set up billing тЖТ" (тЖТ Checkout) for no-subscription, "Manage billing тЖТ" (тЖТ Portal) for a live one. The plan price is read live via `usePlanInfo()` тАФ never hardcoded; loading тЖТ "LoadingтАж", Stripe-unreachable тЖТ "Pricing unavailable" (never a stale fixed price). Renders the `PlanInfo.features` list when the Stripe Price carries a `features` metadata key.
- **`integration-tests/stripe.test.mjs`** (`npm run test:stripe`) тАФ gated integration test: a webhookтЖТDB round-trip against a running app, and live TEST-mode Stripe API calls. Skips cleanly (exit 0) when the relevant env is unset.

#### Stripe billing тАФ operator setup

> One-time steps to make Stripe billing work in a deployment. Development uses
> Stripe TEST mode; production swaps the keys for LIVE mode (no code change).

1. Create a Stripe account and complete business verification (required before live charges).
2. Create the product: Stripe dashboard тЖТ **Products** тЖТ add a product тЖТ a **recurring price, тВм299 / month**. Copy the Price id (`price_тАж`).
3. Set the env vars (`.env.local` for dev, the deployment env for production): `STRIPE_SECRET_KEY`, `STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`, `STRIPE_PRICE_ID_STANDARD` (the Price id from step 2). Use `sk_test_тАж` + a test-mode Price id for development.
4. Activate the **Customer Portal**: dashboard тЖТ Settings тЖТ Billing тЖТ **Customer portal** тЖТ activate (and allow payment-method updates + cancellation). The "Manage billing" button fails until this is done.
5. Create a webhook endpoint: dashboard тЖТ **Developers тЖТ Webhooks** тЖТ add endpoint `{app origin}/api/integrations/stripe/webhook`, subscribed to `customer.subscription.created`, `customer.subscription.updated`, `customer.subscription.deleted`, `invoice.payment_succeeded`, `invoice.payment_failed`.
6. Copy the webhook **signing secret** (`whsec_тАж`) into `STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`.
7. Recommended Stripe config: set a **statement descriptor** ("WEBNUA"), enable **automatic retries / Smart Retries** for failed payments, and set the invoice **subscription behaviour** to email the customer on a failed payment.
8. The operator-payment-failed email needs `RESEND_API_KEY` set (the Resend integration is a later session); until then the alert job records `skipped` and the operator sees nothing тАФ set the key, or watch the Stripe dashboard.

#### Twilio SMS (Phase 7)

> One-way alphanumeric SMS for Webnua clients. Each client is assigned ONE
> alphanumeric sender id (their brand name, тЙд11 chars) that appears as the
> "From" on every outbound SMS тАФ lead acknowledgments, job confirmations,
> arrival notifications, review requests. Alphanumeric senders are one-way (the
> recipient cannot reply тАФ two-way is WhatsApp / a direct call, deferred). Built
> on the Session 1 platform-integration spine: every Twilio call goes through
> `callExternal()`, sends run on the `integration_jobs` queue, the send log is
> `sms_messages` (migration `0059`). Webnua owns the Twilio account тАФ customers
> do NOT connect their own. Everything is SERVER-ONLY except `use-sms.ts` (the
> `'use client'` UI data layer).
>
> **Two character-encoding pitfalls the editor exists to catch:** an SMS is
> GSM-7 (160 chars/segment) until one non-GSM character (a curly quote, em-dash,
> emoji, accented letter outside GSM 03.38) flips it to UCS-2 (70 chars/segment)
> тАФ silently doubling cost. And a message over one segment is billed per
> segment. The template editor surfaces both live.

- **`lib/sms/character-validator.ts`** тАФ pure. `validateTemplate(string)` тЖТ `{ isGSMCompatible, nonGSMCharacters[], length, segments, segmentEncoding, warnings[] }`. The GSM 03.38 basic + extension alphabets are encoded verbatim; segment maths is the standard split (GSM 160/153, UCS-2 70/67). Warnings name the common culprits (curly quote / em-dash / ellipsis / non-breaking space / emoji / other non-GSM / multi-segment). Also exports `countSegments`, `gsmSeptets`, `fixSmartCharacters` (the one-click smart-punctuation тЖТ ASCII fix) + `hasFixableSmartCharacters`.
- **`lib/sms/template-renderer.ts`** тАФ pure. `render(template, context)` substitutes `{{group.name}}` placeholders тЖТ `{ text, variablesUsed[], missingVariables[] }`. A referenced-but-missing variable renders empty (never the literal `{{тАж}}` тАФ a customer must not receive an un-substituted placeholder) and is reported.
- **`lib/sms/template-variables.ts`** тАФ pure. `TEMPLATE_VARIABLES` тАФ the closed catalogue of `{{placeholders}}` (`client.shortName/businessName/phone/responseTime`, `lead.firstName/service`, `job.date/time/address/eta`, `review.link`), each with a typical + a longest-realistic sample value. `buildSampleContext('typical' | 'long')` builds a render context for the editor preview / cost estimator.
- **`lib/sms/template-cost-estimator.ts`** тАФ pure. `estimateCost(template)` renders the template with typical sample data, validates the RENDERED output, returns `{ length, segments, encoding, costEur, тАж }`; `estimateWorstCase(template)` does the same with every variable at its longest value. The raw template length is misleading (`{{lead.firstName}}` is 18 chars, renders to 5тАУ11) тАФ the estimate is what the operator should trust.
- **`lib/sms/pricing.ts`** тАФ `SMS_SEGMENT_COST_EUR` (тВм0.05, a representative IE/UK transactional rate тАФ a code constant, not a real per-country rate table; see the parked decision) + `segmentCost` + `formatSmsCost`.
- **`lib/sms/default-templates.ts`** тАФ `SMS_TEMPLATE_KEYS` (the closed 4) + `SmsTemplateKey` + `SMS_TEMPLATE_META` (label/description) + `DEFAULT_SMS_TEMPLATES` (the 4 default bodies тАФ **must stay in lockstep with the seed bodies in migration `0060`**; the constant is the send_sms job's runtime fallback) + `MAX_TEMPLATE_LENGTH` (320 = 2 GSM segments, the hard save limit).
- **`lib/sms/phone.ts`** тАФ pure. `normalizePhone(raw, defaultCountry)` тАФ best-effort coercion of a freeform phone number to E.164 (handles already-E.164, `00`-international, leading-`0` national). A heuristic, not libphonenumber; a number it cannot normalise is returned as-is and Twilio rejects it (an honest failed `sms_messages` row).
- **`lib/integrations/twilio/client.ts`** тАФ the typed Twilio API wrapper, every call through `callExternal()`. `isTwilioConfigured()` / `isSenderRegistrationConfigured()`; `registerSenderID(clientId, senderId)` (adds the alphanumeric string to the Messaging Service as an AlphaSender resource тАФ the resource SID is the "registration id"); `getSenderIDStatus(registrationId)`; `sendSMS(senderId, to, body, opts)`; `mapTwilioMessageStatus`. HTTP Basic auth (Account SID / Auth Token). PRODUCTION SWAP flagged тАФ test vs live is purely which credentials are set.
- **`lib/integrations/twilio/types.ts`** тАФ Twilio API object slices + the three SMS-table row shapes (`ClientSmsSenderRow`, `SmsMessageRow`/`Insert`, `SmsTemplateRow`) hand-written until the generated `Database` type is regenerated.
- **`lib/integrations/twilio/senders.ts`** / **`messages.ts`** / **`templates.ts`** тАФ service-role data access for `client_sms_senders` / `sms_messages` / `sms_templates` via `getIntegrationDb()`. `templates.ts` exposes only the read (`getTemplate`) the `send_sms` job calls; an editor would expose more, but template editing is deferred to the Automations feature, so the write helpers don't exist yet.
- **`lib/integrations/twilio/webhook-verify.ts`** тАФ `verifyTwilioSignature(url, params, signature, authToken)` тАФ Twilio's HMAC-SHA1-over-(URL + sorted params) scheme, `node:crypto` only, no SDK.
- **`lib/integrations/twilio/job-types.ts`** + **`job-handlers.ts`** тАФ `SEND_SMS_JOB` (`send_sms`); the handler loads the client's template, builds the render context (client + lead facts) and validates length, sends via Twilio, records the `sms_messages` row. Retry discipline: a retryable Twilio failure with job attempts left re-throws (the job requeues, no row); a terminal failure records a `failed` row тАФ so a retried send never double-records. Skips honestly (no row) when Twilio is unconfigured / the client has no approved sender. Registered via the `job-handler-manifest.ts` side-effect import.
- **`lib/integrations/twilio/use-sms.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`. `useClientSmsSender` (RLS-scoped browser read) + `useRegisterSmsSender` / `useRefreshSmsSender` (POST the operator-only sender route).
- **`app/api/integrations/twilio/sender/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, operator-only (`requireOperatorForClient`). `action: 'register'` registers the alphanumeric sender + inserts the `client_sms_senders` row (`pending_approval`); `action: 'refresh'` polls Twilio and flips the row to `approved` once Twilio confirms the AlphaSender resource.
- **`app/api/integrations/twilio/webhook/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, signature-authenticated (X-Twilio-Signature). Twilio's delivery status callback тАФ updates `sms_messages.status` by Twilio message SID as queued тЖТ sent тЖТ delivered (or failed / undelivered). Every delivery + every rejected delivery logs to `integration_call_log` `direction='inbound'`.
- **`components/shared/settings/SmsSenderSection.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`. The sender provisioning panel on sub-account `/settings/sms` тАФ submit a sender id, or see the current one + its registration status + a "Refresh status" poll.
- **`app/settings/sms/page.tsx`** тАФ the SMS settings surface (sub-account mode, operator-only тАФ a new `/settings/sms` tab in `subAccountSettingsNav` + the `SUB_ACCOUNT_ONLY` layout guard). Composes `SmsSenderSection` only. **Template editing lives with the Automations feature** тАФ the message bodies are tied to the automations that fire them, so an isolated template editor here would be misleading. The four per-client templates are still seeded by migration `0060` so the `send_sms` job has a body to render; an operator-facing editor mounts once Automations is fully built.
- **Lead-acknowledgment trigger** тАФ `app/api/forms/submit/route.ts` enqueues a `send_sms` job (`enqueueJobImmediate`, the `lead_acknowledgment` template) the moment a public lead-capture form creates a lead, when the lead carries a phone number. Best-effort тАФ a job-enqueue failure never fails the lead capture.

#### Twilio SMS тАФ operator setup

> One-time steps to make SMS work in a deployment. Development uses Twilio TEST
> credentials; production swaps to live credentials (no code change).

1. Create a Twilio account and complete business verification (a US business or an international one тАФ an Ireland sole trader is fine).
2. Create a **Messaging Service** (Twilio Console тЖТ Messaging тЖТ Services). Copy its SID (`MGтАж`) into `TWILIO_MESSAGING_SERVICE_SID` тАФ alphanumeric senders are registered against it.
3. Enable the **alphanumeric Sender ID** feature for the account. In most of Europe / Ireland it is available by default; some accounts / destination countries require a Twilio support ticket or a regulated-country Sender ID registration (Twilio Console тЖТ Messaging тЖТ Sender IDs) тАФ that registration is the "1тАУ3 business days" the UI mentions. `registerSenderID()` adds the sender to the Messaging Service immediately; the regulated-country registration, where required, is completed in the Console.
4. Configure the **status callback URL**: `{app origin}/api/integrations/twilio/webhook` тАФ either on the Messaging Service, or it is sent per-message automatically when `APP_BASE_URL` (or `VERCEL_URL` / `APP_HOST`) resolves.
5. Set the env vars (`.env.local` for dev, the deployment env for production): `TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID`, `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN`, `TWILIO_MESSAGING_SERVICE_SID`, and optionally `TWILIO_DEFAULT_COUNTRY` (ISO-3166 alpha-2, default `IE`). Use `ACтАж` test credentials + a test Messaging Service for development.
6. Per client: an operator submits the client's alphanumeric sender id on sub-account `/settings/sms`, then completes any regulated-country registration in the Twilio Console, and uses "Refresh status" to confirm the sender is approved. SMS only sends once the sender is `approved`.

#### Resend email (Phase 7)

> Transactional email + an inbound-reply pipeline for Webnua clients. The same
> two-way conversation surface as SMS, but unlike one-way alphanumeric senders
> the customer can reply by email; replies route back to the Webnua lead
> inbox via plus-addressed thread tokens (`{clientSlug}+lead-{token}@mail.
> webnua.com`) that an HMAC binds to the lead so addresses are unforgeable.
> Built on the Session 1 platform-integration spine: every Resend call goes
> through `callExternal()`, every transactional send runs on the
> `integration_jobs` queue (so retries + observability are automatic), the
> message log is `email_messages` (migration 0061). Webnua owns the Resend
> account тАФ customers do NOT connect their own. SERVER-ONLY for the lib;
> `use-email.ts` is the one `'use client'` UI layer.
>
> **Three flow paths from one integration:**
> 1. **Customer-facing email** (lead_followup / review_request /
>    quote_followup) тАФ fired by the public form-submit route and by future
>    automations. The thread carries a Reply-To with a plus-addressed token
>    so any reply lands in the inbox.
> 2. **Operator notification** (lead_notification / lead_digest) тАФ fanned
>    automatically by a DB trigger on `leads` (migration 0063). The
>    `send_lead_notification` job resolves the configured operator recipients
>    on `notification_preferences`, runs the 5-minute throttle, and either
>    dispatches immediately OR defers the lead to the hourly digest worker.
> 3. **Operator-typed reply** (the lead inbox "Reply" button) тАФ POSTs the
>    body to `/api/leads/[id]/reply`, which sends through Resend, threads
>    via `In-Reply-To`, and writes the `email_messages` row + `email_out`
>    `lead_events` entry.

- **`lib/integrations/resend/client.ts`** тАФ typed Resend wrapper.
  `isResendConfigured()`, `isInboundWebhookConfigured()`, `sendEmail`,
  `getMessage`, `mapResendEventToStatus`. Every call routes through
  `callExternal()` (timeout / retry / `integration_call_log`). HTTP Bearer
  auth on `RESEND_API_KEY`. Resend takes JSON, returns JSON.
- **`lib/integrations/resend/types.ts`** тАФ slices of the Resend API objects
  this integration reads + the four row shapes (`client_email_senders` 0051
  via this session, `email_messages` 0061, `email_templates` 0062,
  `notification_preferences` 0063). Hand-written until the generated
  `Database` type is regenerated.
- **`lib/integrations/resend/webhook-verify.ts`** тАФ Svix-style signature
  verification (`HMAC-SHA256` over `{id}.{timestamp}.{rawBody}`, 5-minute
  timestamp tolerance). Pure node:crypto, no Svix SDK. Used by both the
  inbound webhook (whole emails) and the delivery webhook (status events) тАФ
  same signing secret, route discriminates on the JSON `type` field.
- **`lib/integrations/resend/{senders,messages,templates,preferences}.ts`**
  тАФ typed data access against the four new tables. `senders.ts` includes
  the global-unique `slug` check + `getSenderBySlug` / `findSenderByClientSlug`
  the inbound webhook uses to resolve the plus-addressed recipient back to a
  client. `messages.ts` carries `findOutboundByResendId` for In-Reply-To
  fallback. `preferences.ts` exposes the throttle query
  `lastSentAtForRecipient` against `notifications_outbound`.
- **`lib/email/threading.ts`** тАФ `generateThreadToken(leadId)` /
  `parseThreadToken` (HMAC-SHA256 base64url-encoded payload with version +
  leadId + iat); `composeReplyToAddress(clientSlug, token)` /
  `parseInboundAddress(addr)`. HMAC key resolves `OAUTH_STATE_SECRET` тЖТ
  `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` тАФ same fallback chain as the OAuth state token.
  `looksLikeAutoResponder(email)` тАФ RFC 3834 `Auto-Submitted` + the older
  `X-Autoreply` family + subject-pattern fallback (Out of Office /
  Auto-Reply / On Vacation / On Holiday).
- **`lib/email/templates.ts`** тАФ pure renderer (`renderEmail({subject,
  body_html, body_text}, context) тЖТ {subject, html, text, variablesUsed[],
  missingVariables[]}`). `{{placeholder}}` substitution; a missing variable
  renders empty (never the literal `{{тАж}}` тАФ a customer must not receive an
  un-substituted placeholder) and is reported. Plus the HTMLтЖФplain helpers
  `wrapPlainAsHtml(plain)` and `htmlToPlain(html)` the operator-reply path
  uses to fill in whichever body the operator did not type.
- **`lib/email/default-templates.ts`** тАФ `DEFAULT_EMAIL_TEMPLATES` тАФ the five
  default bodies. **Must stay in lockstep with the seed bodies in migration
  0062** (the constant is the send_email job's runtime fallback when a
  template row is somehow absent; the migration is the source of truth an
  operator edits).
- **`lib/email/template-variables.ts`** тАФ closed catalogue of
  `{{placeholders}}` extending the SMS set with `{{review.link}}`,
  `{{platform.inboxLink}}`, `{{lead.email}}` / `phone` / `fullName` /
  `lastNameSuffix` / `preview`, and the digest variables. Drives a future
  editor's variable picker (deferred, same precedent as SMS).
- **`lib/integrations/resend/job-types.ts`** + **`job-handlers.ts`** тАФ four
  registered handlers via `job-handler-manifest.ts`:
  - **`send_email`** тАФ the workhorse. Loads the template (db row, falling
    back to `DEFAULT_EMAIL_TEMPLATES`), renders against a context built from
    the client + the related lead, sends via Resend, writes the
    `email_messages` row. Customer-facing templates carry a Reply-To with
    a freshly-minted thread token; operator-facing templates do not.
    Retryable failures with attempts left re-throw so the job requeues;
    terminal failures record a `failed` row (no duplicate per-retry rows тАФ
    same discipline as `send_sms`).
  - **`send_lead_notification`** тАФ fan-out triggered by the AFTER INSERT
    trigger on `leads` (0063). Looks up recipients via
    `listNewLeadRecipients`, checks each against the 5-minute throttle on
    `notifications_outbound`, then dispatches `send_email` for immediates
    or sets `leads.notification_pending_at` for everyone throttled / on the
    hourly+daily frequency tiers.
  - **`batch_notification_digest`** тАФ hourly worker (scheduled by `pg_cron`
    in 0063). Finds leads with `notification_pending_at` set, groups by
    client, sends one `lead_digest` send_email per (client, recipient),
    clears the flags.
  - **`send_test_notification`** тАФ operator-triggered test send from the
    settings UI; renders a synthetic lead_notification.
- **`lib/integrations/resend/use-email.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`. Browser
  hooks: `useClientEmailSender(clientId)`, `useNotificationPreferences`,
  plus the matching `useRegisterEmailSender` /
  `useUpdateEmailSender` / `useCreateNotificationPreference` /
  `useUpdateNotificationPreference` / `useDeleteNotificationPreference` /
  `useTestNotification` mutation hooks.
- **`app/api/integrations/resend/sender/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, operator-only.
  `action: 'register'` provisions the per-client slug + display name (the
  slug is globally unique тАФ a pre-check returns a friendlier 409 than the
  constraint violation); `action: 'update'` edits the display name or
  toggles `status` between `active` / `suspended`.
- **`app/api/integrations/resend/preferences/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  operator-only. `create` / `update` / `delete` against
  `notification_preferences` (per-client recipient configuration).
- **`app/api/integrations/resend/test-notification/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  operator-only. Enqueues `send_test_notification` for the "Test send"
  button on the settings UI.
- **`app/api/integrations/resend/inbound/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  signature-authenticated (Svix). Resend POSTs every inbound email here.
  Parses the plus-addressing back to (clientSlug, token); verifies the
  thread token's HMAC; cross-tenant guards that the lead belongs to the
  resolved client; detects auto-responders; re-uploads attachments to the
  email-attachments Storage bucket (0064); inserts the inbound
  `email_messages` row + an `email_in` `lead_events` event (skipped for
  auto-responders). Returns 200 once verified (even on a routing failure тАФ
  returning non-200 would make Resend retry indefinitely; an inbound to a
  bad address is operator-debug territory, logged to `integration_call_log`
  with `operation='rejected_inbound'`).
- **`app/api/integrations/resend/webhook/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  signature-authenticated. Resend's delivery status callback тАФ
  updates outbound rows' status by `resend_message_id` as Resend reports
  `email.sent` тЖТ `delivered` (or `bounced` / `complained` / `failed`).
- **`app/api/leads/[id]/reply/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`, lead-access-gated. The
  body of the lead inbox's reply composer POSTs here. Resolves the most-
  recent outbound to set `In-Reply-To` (so mail clients thread the
  conversation), sends through Resend with a freshly-minted thread token
  (so the next inbound from the customer reaches the right lead), writes
  the `email_messages` row + the `email_out` `lead_event`.
- **`components/shared/leads/LeadConversationComposer.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`.
  Wraps the visual `ConversationComposer` and wires the **Email** channel
  to `useReplyToLead`. The SMS channel stays inert ("sending SMS from the
  inbox is a Phase 8 concern" тАФ the automation execution engine, see the
  "Automation overlap / anti-spam suppression rules" parked decision below).
  Channel availability follows what's on file: a lead with no email locks
  the composer to SMS, a lead with no phone locks to email, both available
  defaults to Email.
- **`components/shared/settings/EmailSenderSection.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`.
  The slug + display-name provisioning panel on sub-account `/settings/email`,
  with the address preview `{slug}@mail.webnua.com` + a pause/resume affordance.
- **`components/shared/settings/NotificationPreferencesSection.tsx`** тАФ
  `'use client'`. The operator-recipient list on sub-account
  `/settings/notifications`. Add / remove recipients, per-event toggles
  (`notify_on_new_lead` / `_payment_failure` / `_review_received`), the
  digest-frequency select (immediate / hourly / daily), and a Test send
  button.
- **`app/settings/email/page.tsx`** тАФ the new sub-account-only settings
  tab (added to `subAccountSettingsNav` + the layout's `SUB_ACCOUNT_ONLY`
  guard). Composes `EmailSenderSection` only тАФ template editing is deferred
  to a future Automations editor session.
- **`app/settings/notifications/page.tsx`** тАФ now a `'use client'` role
  dispatcher. Operator + sub-account тЖТ `NotificationPreferencesSection`;
  client-role тЖТ the existing channel-preferences stub (preserved). The
  layout's `SUB_ACCOUNT_ONLY` guard keeps an operator in agency mode away.
- **Lead-followup email trigger** тАФ `app/api/forms/submit/route.ts`
  enqueues a `send_email` (`lead_followup`) job alongside the SMS-acknowledgment
  enqueue, when the public form captured a customer email. Best-effort тАФ
  a job-enqueue failure never fails the lead capture. The operator
  **new-lead notification** is fanned by a DB trigger on `leads`
  (migration 0063), so the public route stays minimal.

#### Resend email тАФ operator setup

> One-time steps to make email work in a deployment.

1. Create a Resend account (resend.com).
2. Add and verify the **sending domain** (default: `mail.webnua.com`). Resend's
   dashboard issues DNS records тАФ add the **DKIM** CNAMEs, the **SPF**
   `include`/`v=spf1` TXT, and a **DMARC** TXT (`v=DMARC1; p=quarantine; тАж`)
   at the registrar. Resend's dashboard shows verification status; do not
   send until all three are green.
3. Set up **inbound email**: in the Resend dashboard, configure inbound
   routing on the same domain (or a subdomain) to POST every inbound message
   to `{app origin}/api/integrations/resend/inbound`. This requires MX
   records pointing to Resend.
4. Create a **delivery-status webhook** in the Resend dashboard pointing at
   `{app origin}/api/integrations/resend/webhook`, subscribed to `email.sent`,
   `email.delivered`, `email.bounced`, `email.complained`, `email.failed`.
   Copy its signing secret (`whsec_тАж`) into `RESEND_WEBHOOK_SECRET`.
4b. Create a **separate inbound webhook** in the Resend dashboard pointing at
   `{app origin}/api/integrations/resend/inbound`, subscribed to
   `email.received`. Copy its signing secret (`whsec_тАж`) into
   `RESEND_INBOUND_WEBHOOK_SECRET`. **Each Resend webhook has its own signing
   secret** тАФ using only `RESEND_WEBHOOK_SECRET` for both webhooks produces
   a 400 + `{"error":"invalid-signature"}` on every `email.received`
   delivery (which is silently dropped: nothing arrives in the lead inbox).
   `RESEND_INBOUND_WEBHOOK_SECRET` falls back to `RESEND_WEBHOOK_SECRET` only
   in the rare single-webhook setup (one Resend webhook URL covers both
   types тАФ not possible today, since the two routes live at different URLs).
5. Set the env vars (`.env.local` for dev, the deployment env for production):
   `RESEND_API_KEY`, `RESEND_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, `RESEND_INBOUND_WEBHOOK_SECRET`,
   optionally `EMAIL_SENDING_DOMAIN` (default `mail.webnua.com`). The
   threading HMAC reads `OAUTH_STATE_SECRET` if set, falling back to
   `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY`.
6. Per client: an operator provisions a sender slug on sub-account
   `/settings/email`. The sending address becomes `{slug}@mail.webnua.com`.
   Adds notification recipients on `/settings/notifications` (sub-account
   mode) тАФ typically the operator's own email + the client's own.

#### Google Business Profile (Phase 7)

> Per-tenant integration with each customer's own GBP listing. Reviews drive
> local SEO rankings, so this is one of the highest-leverage automations in
> the acquisition machine. Three end-to-end flows:
>
> 1. **Connect + pick location.** GBP belongs to the customer's own
>    business, so the **client** can connect their own listing directly
>    (the "Connect Google Business тЖТ" CTA on `/reviews` when no location
>    is wired up yet) тАФ the operator can also do it on their behalf from
>    sub-account `/settings/integrations`. On callback return, the
>    `GbpLocationPickerModal` auto-opens so they pick WHICH location to
>    manage. The selection lands in `client_gbp_locations` (one row per
>    client, migration `0066`). The connect/disconnect routes accept
>    EITHER role for GBP via `requireClientAccess` (Meta Ads stays
>    operator-only тАФ different governance axis).
> 2. **Review-request automation.** When a booking transitions to
>    `completed`, the migration `0069` `AFTER UPDATE` trigger enqueues a
>    `gbp_send_review_request` job with a **2-hour delay**. The handler
>    resolves the GBP review link, picks SMS or email (SMS preferred when
>    the customer has a phone AND the client has an approved alphanumeric
>    sender; email fallback), and enqueues the underlying `send_sms` /
>    `send_email` job. The audit row lands on `gbp_review_requests`.
> 3. **Daily review pull.** `pg_cron` fires `gbp_sync_reviews` daily (06:00
>    UTC) for every connected location. The handler calls Google's
>    `listReviews` via `callWithToken()`, upserts `gbp_reviews` rows
>    preserving each row's `is_new_since_last_view` state, marks
>    Google-removed reviews as deleted, attributes recent requests to the
>    review they led to (7-day window), and refreshes the cached headline
>    metrics on the location row. Polling rather than push because GBP
>    review notifications aren't reliable.
>
> SERVER-ONLY for the lib; `use-gbp.ts` is the one `'use client'` UI layer.
> V1 ships: location data, reviews list, review reply, review-request
> automation. V1.1: GBP posts + insights (stubbed as fast-fail
> `IntegrationResult` in `client.ts`).

- **`lib/integrations/gbp/client.ts`** тАФ the typed GBP API wrapper.
  `isGbpConfigured()`, `listAccounts`, `listLocations`, `getLocation`,
  `listReviews`, `replyToReview`. Posts + insights are V1.1 stubs that
  return a fast-fail `non_retryable` `IntegrationResult` so any call site
  fails loudly when those V1.1 paths get wired. Every call routes through
  `callWithToken()` so token refresh + 401 retry are handled per-call.
  Google's APIs are split across three hostnames (Account Management,
  Business Information, the legacy v4 surface that still owns reviews);
  the wrapper hides that split behind the function-level interface.
  Helpers: `composeLocationPath(accountId, locationId)` (builds the full
  `accounts/.../locations/...` path the v4 API requires from the two stored
  halves), `buildReviewLink(location)` (prefers
  `metadata.newReviewUri`, falls back to a `placeId`-based
  `search.google.com/local/writereview?placeid=тАж` URL), and
  `formatLocationAddress(location)` (single-line string from Google's
  structured `storefrontAddress`).
- **`lib/integrations/gbp/types.ts`** тАФ Google API slices (`GbpAccount` /
  `GbpLocation` / `GbpReview` / `GbpStarRating` and the wrappers) +
  `starRatingToInt()` (Google's enum-string тЖТ 1-5 integer) + hand-written
  row types for the three new tables (`ClientGbpLocationRow`,
  `GbpReviewRow`, `GbpReviewRequestRow`) until the generated `Database`
  type is regenerated.
- **`lib/integrations/gbp/locations.ts`** тАФ `client_gbp_locations` data
  access (`findLocationByClientId`, `upsertLocation`,
  `updateLocationSyncState`, `deleteLocationByClientId`). Crucially exports
  **`getReviewLinkForClient(clientId)`** тАФ the helper the SMS + email
  `buildRenderContext` calls to substitute `{{review.link}}` to the real
  Google "leave a review" URL. Pre-GBP, both handlers either left it empty
  (Twilio) or used a `/reviews` placeholder (Resend); both now resolve
  through this.
- **`lib/integrations/gbp/reviews.ts`** тАФ `gbp_reviews` data access:
  `listKnownReviewIds()` (pre-query set the sync uses to preserve seen
  state), `upsertReviews()`, `markReviewsDeleted()` (`NOT IN` sweep so
  Google-removed rows drop out of the visible list but stay for audit),
  `markReviewsSeen()` (badge-clear on operator open), `recordReviewReply()`
  (post-reply cache so the inbox shows the reply without waiting for
  tomorrow's sync), `findReviewById()`.
- **`lib/integrations/gbp/review-requests.ts`** тАФ `gbp_review_requests`
  data access: `insertReviewRequest()`, `findAttributableRequest(clientId,
  reviewCreatedAt)` (the 7-day attribution window тАФ a fresh review may
  link back to the request that caused it),
  `attributeRequestToReview()`. The 7-day window is a practical heuristic:
  reviews left more than a week after a prompt are nearly always
  unprompted, and a wider attribution window would mislead the conversion
  dashboard.
- **`lib/integrations/gbp/job-types.ts`** + **`job-handlers.ts`** тАФ two
  registered handlers (manifest-imported via
  `job-handler-manifest.ts`):
  - **`gbp_sync_reviews`** тАФ pull recent reviews + upsert. **Two-pass
    upsert strategy** to preserve seen state: pre-query existing
    `gbp_review_id`s, then INSERT-as-upsert fresh rows with
    `is_new_since_last_view=true` and UPSERT known rows WITHOUT touching
    the seen flag (Supabase upsert leaves columns absent from the payload
    alone on conflict). Optional `refreshLocation: true` flag re-fetches
    location detail too (used post-connect + on operator "Sync now");
    daily cron leaves it off to keep API quota cheap.
  - **`gbp_send_review_request`** тАФ payload normalisation (handles the
    trigger's `jsonb_build_object` shape via `normalizeSendReviewRequestPayload`),
    channel selection (SMS preferred тЖТ email fallback, with sender +
    integration-configured gates), then enqueues `send_sms` or
    `send_email` with a `contextOverrides: { 'review.link': тАж }` so the
    underlying handler doesn't re-resolve. The `gbp_review_requests`
    audit row is the high-level "we asked" log; per-channel detail
    (delivery / segments / Resend id) lives on `sms_messages` /
    `email_messages`.
- **`lib/integrations/gbp/use-gbp.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`. Operator-UI data
  layer: `useClientGbpLocation` / `useClientGbpReviews` /
  `useClientGbpReviewRequests` (RLS-scoped browser reads),
  `useListGbpLocations` / `useSelectGbpLocation` / `useSyncGbpReviews` /
  `useReplyToGbpReview` / `useMarkGbpReviewsSeen` /
  `useSendGbpReviewRequest` (POST the operator routes), plus the cheap
  derived `useNewGbpReviewsCount(clientId)` used by the dashboard widget.
- **`app/api/integrations/google_business_profile/locations/route.ts`** тАФ
  `POST`, client-or-operator (the customer's own listing). Two actions: `list` calls
  `listAccounts` + `listLocations` for every account in parallel,
  returning a bucketed list the picker UI groups under the parent Google
  account; `select` upserts the chosen location, fetches its detail to
  cache title / address / `review_link`, and fires an initial
  `gbp_sync_reviews` job with `refreshLocation=true`. Returns 503 when GBP
  isn't configured so the consent error is meaningful.
- **`app/api/integrations/google_business_profile/sync/route.ts`** тАФ
  `POST`, client-or-operator (the customer's own listing). Manual "Sync now" тАФ enqueues a sync with
  `refreshLocation=true` so the location detail + reviews refresh together.
- **`app/api/integrations/google_business_profile/reply/route.ts`** тАФ
  `POST`, client-or-operator (the customer's own listing). Validates the reply (тЙд 4096 chars), resolves the
  `gbp_review_id` (the API path) from the DB row id, calls `replyToReview`
  via `callWithToken`, then caches the reply locally via
  `recordReviewReply` so the inbox refresh shows the reply immediately
  (the next daily sync would otherwise be the source of truth).
- **`app/api/integrations/google_business_profile/review-request/route.ts`** тАФ
  `POST`, client-or-operator (the customer's own listing). Manual review-request send (off-platform jobs,
  re-sends). Same job handler the trigger uses тАФ `gbp_send_review_request`.
- **`app/api/integrations/google_business_profile/mark-seen/route.ts`** тАФ
  `POST`, client-or-operator (the customer's own listing). Clears `is_new_since_last_view` for every unseen
  review for a client (badge-clear).
- **`components/shared/settings/GbpLocationPickerModal.tsx`** тАФ
  `'use client'`. Post-OAuth location picker. Calls the `list` action on
  mount, buckets locations under their parent Google account header, and
  lands the selection through `useSelectGbpLocation`. Triggered
  contextually: auto-opens from `IntegrationConnectionsSection` when the
  OAuth callback redirects back with the GBP success URL; also opened
  manually from the GBP connection row's "Change location" button.
- **`components/shared/settings/IntegrationConnectionsSection.tsx`**
  *(extended)* тАФ the existing operator OAuth connections panel on
  sub-account `/settings/integrations`. Phase 7 GBP UI consolidation
  added: (1) auto-open `GbpLocationPickerModal` on the GBP success URL
  (an effect on `useLocationSearch()` flips the picker open the first
  time the URL carries the matching params); (2) an inline
  `GbpConnectionFooter` block on the GBP connection row only тАФ surfaces
  the connected location title + rating + last-sync time + "Sync now" +
  "Change location" buttons, OR a "pick a location" prompt when GBP is
  OAuth-connected but no location row exists yet. No dedicated GBP tab тАФ
  connection management AND operational state live on the same surface.
- **`components/shared/reviews/ReviewItem.tsx`** *(extended)* тАФ
  `'use client'`. The existing reviews-list row (used by `/reviews` in
  both operator + client contexts) now carries an inline reply UI gated
  on `review.clientId`. Reply state is read off the row (`review.reply`
  when GBP has a published reply); when absent, an inline composer opens
  via `useReplyToGbpReview(clientId)`. Operator + client reply through
  the same component; the operator just passes the per-card client id.
- **`components/shared/leads/LeadTimeline.tsx`** *(extended)* тАФ the
  existing lead-timeline component now styles the new `review-request`
  dot type (amber star тАФ the GBP echo). Review-request sends fold into
  the same chronological timeline as the other lead events; no separate
  audit section.
- **`components/shared/gbp/GbpConnectPanel.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`.
  Empty-state "Connect Google Business Profile тЖТ" CTA mounted on
  `/reviews` (client view) when the client has no GBP location
  connected. Fires the OAuth flow via the shared `connectIntegration`
  helper; the underlying `/connect` route accepts a client-role user
  for GBP. Self-hides once a location is connected. Also offers an
  "Already connected? Pick a location" link that opens
  `GbpLocationPickerModal` directly тАФ for the case the operator
  pre-OAuth'd on behalf and the client just needs to pick.
- **`components/shared/gbp/GbpSendRequestButton.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`.
  The manual review-request affordance. Three render variants:
  `'button'` (default; outline button), `'action-row'` (full-width
  ghost row with leading icon, for in-rail mounting), `'ghost'`
  (ghost button for hero-actions rows). Owns its own modal тАФ pre-filled
  with the recipient context the parent passes (lead or booking). Posts
  through `useSendGbpReviewRequest(clientId)` which enqueues the
  `gbp_send_review_request` job; the modal closes on success.
- **`components/shared/GbpReviewsWidget.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'`. The
  dashboard widget: rating + total reviews + new-since-last-view counter
  + an "Open reviews тЖТ" link. Mounted on the operator hub (sub-account
  `/dashboard`) and the client `/dashboard`; both default the link to
  `/reviews` (the dedicated GBP tab is gone тАФ `/reviews` IS the
  destination). Self-hides when the client has no connected GBP location,
  so a freshly-onboarded dashboard doesn't show an empty placeholder.

#### Google Business Profile тАФ operator setup

> Builds on the OAuth-app config above ("Per-tenant OAuth тАФ Google
> Business Profile setup"). These are the in-Webnua steps per-customer.

1. Ensure the OAuth consent screen lists the
   `https://www.googleapis.com/auth/business.manage` scope, and (for
   production use) the OAuth app has passed Google's verified-app review.
   Until verified, only test users added to the consent screen can connect.
2. Either path is supported: (a) the **client** signs into their own
   Webnua account and clicks **"Connect Google Business тЖТ"** on `/reviews`
   (the empty-state CTA when no GBP location is connected), OR (b) with
   the customer present, the operator navigates to sub-account
   `/settings/integrations` and clicks **Connect** on the GBP row. Either
   way the customer signs in to their own Google account + grants consent.
3. The callback redirects to `/settings/integrations?integration=google_business_profile&integration_status=connected`.
   The `GbpLocationPickerModal` opens automatically on landing тАФ pick the
   Business Profile location Webnua should manage; the modal stores the
   selection and fires an initial sync.
4. An initial sync runs in the background. The headline rating + review
   count populate within seconds; the next daily cron continues from
   there. The GBP connection row on the same `/settings/integrations`
   page surfaces the connected location + a "Sync now" button + a
   "Change location" affordance for later changes.
5. Once a booking is marked **completed** in Webnua, the booking-
   completion trigger queues a review-request SMS or email two hours
   later automatically. For off-platform jobs / re-sends, use the
   **тШЕ Send review request** button on the lead detail (under QUICK
   ACTIONS) or on the booking detail (under AFTER THE JOB / in the hero
   actions for operators).
6. Reviews + replies live on `/reviews` for both operator (cross-client
   grid) and client (single-business) views; reply inline on any row.

#### Meta Ads (Phase 7 тАФ FINAL Phase 7 session)

> Per-tenant Meta Ads integration тАФ Webnua manages each customer's
> Facebook / Instagram lead-generation campaigns end to end. Five flows:
>
> 1. **Connect + pick ad account + capture customer agreement.** Either
>    the client themselves OR the operator initiates the connect from
>    `/settings/integrations` (Meta sits behind `requireClientAccess`,
>    same governance shape as GBP тАФ the third-party account belongs to
>    the customer). The post-OAuth callback redirects back to the
>    integrations page, the `MetaAdAccountPickerModal` auto-opens (mirror
>    of `GbpLocationPickerModal`), and the operator (or the customer)
>    picks WHICH ad account + records the customer's email as the audit
>    trail for two consents: (a) Meta billing the customer's card
>    directly for ad spend, (b) Webnua managing campaigns on their
>    behalf. Selection lands on `client_meta_ad_accounts` (one row per
>    client, migration `0070`).
> 2. **Manage campaigns directly in Meta Ads Manager.** The operator opens
>    the admin `/campaigns` page, picks a client from the sidebar
>    (sub-account mode), clicks **Open Meta Ads Manager тЖТ** тАФ
>    `LaunchMetaCampaignButton` deep-links to
>    `business.facebook.com/adsmanager/manage/campaigns?act={id}` for the
>    customer's connected ad account (the OAuth grant gives Webnua
>    business-manager access). All campaign creation + editing happens in
>    Meta's own UI; Webnua doesn't build campaigns in-app. Webnua's
>    `/campaigns` surface lists what Meta says is live + carries the
>    in-app pause / resume affordance.
> 3. **Hourly campaign discovery.** `pg_cron` at minute 7 of every hour
>    fires `meta_sync_campaigns` per client with a wired ad account
>    (migration `0075`). The handler calls Meta's
>    `/act_{id}/campaigns` via `callWithToken()` and upserts both
>    `public.campaigns` and `meta_campaigns` rows for every campaign on
>    the ad account тАФ idempotent on `meta_campaign_id`, so re-running
>    refreshes existing rows + picks up anything newly launched in Ads
>    Manager. **Auto-fires immediately** after a fresh ad-account pick
>    (`/api/integrations/meta_ads/ad-accounts` `select` action) so a
>    newly-connected customer sees their campaigns within seconds. The
>    operator `/campaigns` page also carries a "тЖ╗ Sync campaigns"
>    button (`SyncCampaignsButton`) that fires the same job manually.
>    V1 fills `meta_ad_set_id` / `meta_ad_id` / `meta_creative_id` /
>    `meta_lead_form_id` as null on ingest тАФ the existing
>    `meta_sync_insights` job (#4) attaches to the discovered rows; the
>    `meta_sync_leads` job (#5) does NOT yet attach (lead-form
>    discovery requires walking the campaign тЖТ ad-set тЖТ ad тЖТ creative
>    chain, deferred to a follow-up).
> 4. **Daily insights sync.** `pg_cron` at 04:00 UTC fires
>    `meta_sync_insights` per active campaign (migration `0074`). The
>    handler calls Meta's `/insights` endpoint via `callWithToken()`,
>    upserts a row per day on `meta_ads_insights` (unique on
>    `(meta_campaign_id, date_recorded)`), and refreshes the local
>    campaign status from Meta's `effective_status` so a Meta-side pause
>    / disapproval surfaces without waiting for next manual fetch.
> 5. **Every-15-min lead pull.** `pg_cron` `*/15 * * * *` fires
>    `meta_sync_leads` per active lead-form-attached campaign. The
>    handler pulls leads created since the last sync via Meta's
>    `/{form_id}/leads`, dedupes on `meta_lead_id` (stored on
>    `lead_events.payload`), and for each new lead inserts a `customers`
>    + `leads` (`source_kind='meta'`) + `lead_events` (`form_submitted`)
>    row triple, then enqueues the lead-acknowledgment SMS if the lead
>    has a phone. Same downstream as the public form-submit flow тАФ the
>    Meta lead is indistinguishable at every surface (inbox, dashboard,
>    automation triggers, operator new-lead notification).
> 6. **Performance display lights up `/campaigns`.** The existing
>    `lib/campaigns/queries.tsx` was extended to join `meta_campaigns` +
>    sum the last 7 days of `meta_ads_insights` per campaign; the per-row
>    `тАФ` LEADS / SPEND / CPL placeholders become real numbers when an
>    inner row exists. The 4-week trend chart on the client deep-dive
>    (`CampaignTrendChart`) now renders real per-week leads + spend.
>    Campaigns with no Meta linkage continue to render placeholders
>    honestly.
>
> **Month-1 ad-credit accounting**: each `meta_campaigns` row carries
> `created_via` (`webnua_month_1` / `webnua_ongoing` / `external`). The
> `meta_sync_campaigns` ingest tags every Ads-Manager-discovered
> campaign as `external` (Webnua did not launch them); the previous
> launch-route Stripe-anchor logic is gone with the in-app builder. The
> month-1 ad-credit envelope is now a manual operator concept тАФ the
> actual тВм200 funding transfer from Webnua to the customer's ad
> account is an out-of-band operator process for V1 (Meta has funding
> APIs but they are not wired here тАФ defer to V2).
>
> SERVER-ONLY for the lib; `use-meta-ads.ts` is the one `'use client'`
> UI layer.

- **`lib/integrations/meta-ads/client.ts`** тАФ the typed Meta Marketing
  API wrapper. `isMetaConfigured()`, `listAdAccounts` / `getAdAccount` /
  `listPages` (discovery for the picker), `createCampaign` /
  `createAdSet` / `createLeadForm` / `createAdCreative` / `createAd`
  (launch orchestration), `pauseCampaign` / `activateCampaign` /
  `pauseAd` / `activateAd`, `getCampaign` (refresh status), `getCampaignInsights`
  (daily metrics), `getLeads` (15-min lead pull). Every call routes
  through `callWithToken()` so the per-tenant long-lived token is
  fresh + a 401 triggers exactly one refresh-and-retry. Meta's POST
  endpoints use `application/x-www-form-urlencoded` (with complex
  values serialised as JSON strings) тАФ same `callExternal` `rawBody`
  escape hatch Stripe uses.
- **`lib/integrations/meta-ads/types.ts`** тАФ Meta API slices
  (`MetaAdAccount` / `MetaPage` / `MetaCampaign` / `MetaInsightsRow` /
  `MetaLeadRow` / etc., all defensively `?` since Meta omits liberally)
  + the four row types (`ClientMetaAdAccountRow` /
  `MetaCampaignRow` / `MetaAdsInsightsRow` / `MetaLeadFormRow`) +
  `mapMetaStatusToLocal()` (Meta `effective_status` тЖТ
  `MetaCampaignDbStatus`) + `describeMetaAccountStatus()` (numeric тЖТ
  human label).
- **`lib/integrations/meta-ads/{ad-accounts,campaigns,insights,lead-forms}.ts`** тАФ
  service-role data access against the four new tables.
- **`lib/integrations/meta-ads/lead-sync.ts`** тАФ bridge from Meta's
  `/leads` endpoint to `public.leads` + `public.lead_events`. Dedupes
  on `meta_lead_id` (stored on `lead_events.payload.meta_lead_id`) so
  overlapping cron + manual syncs are idempotent. Mirrors the
  `/api/forms/submit` insert shape so a Meta lead is structurally
  identical to a website / funnel / test-submit lead at every
  downstream surface.
- **`lib/integrations/meta-ads/job-types.ts`** + **`job-handlers.ts`** тАФ
  three registered handlers via the `job-handler-manifest.ts` side-effect
  import:
  - **`meta_sync_campaigns`** тАФ hourly + on-demand whole-account ingest.
    Reads `client_meta_ad_accounts` for the client, calls
    `listCampaignsForAdAccount`, and runs `upsertCampaignFromMeta` per
    campaign (in `meta-ads/campaigns.ts`) тАФ idempotent on
    `meta_campaign_id`, writes BOTH `public.campaigns` (the operator-
    facing row the `/campaigns` reader joins to) AND `meta_campaigns`
    (the Meta-side companion). Sets `created_via='external'` since
    Webnua didn't launch the campaign. Auto-fires post-pick from the
    ad-accounts route + the `/api/integrations/meta_ads/sync` route
    when called without `metaCampaignDbId` (the "тЖ╗ Sync campaigns"
    button). One bad row in the sweep logs + skips; the rest still
    upsert.
  - **`meta_sync_insights`** тАФ daily per-campaign insights pull. Two-step:
    (1) refresh local status from `getCampaign().effective_status`;
    (2) pull `/insights` for the date range (default yesterday-only;
    manual sync widens to 7 days for backfill), upsert rows on
    `meta_ads_insights`. Lead counts are extracted from Meta's `actions`
    array (Meta returns leads under one of `lead` /
    `leadgen_grouped` / `onsite_conversion.lead_grouped` depending on
    the campaign objective тАФ the handler sums the candidate set).
  - **`meta_sync_leads`** тАФ quarter-hour per-form lead pull. Default
    lookback 1 hour (the dedupe-on-meta_lead_id makes a 1-hour overlap
    with the prior cron tick safe); manual sync widens to 24 hours.
    Per-lead errors swallow + log so one malformed payload doesn't
    fail the whole batch.
- **`lib/integrations/meta-ads/use-meta-ads.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`.
  Operator + customer UI data layer: `useClientMetaAdAccount` /
  `useClientMetaCampaigns` / `useClientMetaInsights` (RLS-scoped
  browser reads, untyped cast тАФ same pattern as `use-gbp.ts` /
  `use-sms.ts`), `useListMetaAdAccounts` / `useSelectMetaAdAccount` /
  `useLaunchMetaCampaign` / `useSetMetaCampaignStatus` /
  `useSyncMetaCampaign` (POST the operator routes). Exports
  `AdAccountPickerOption` / `PagePickerOption` /
  `AdAccountPickerResponse` (the route response shapes the picker UI
  consumes тАФ distinct from the raw `MetaAdAccount` so the picker
  doesn't have to know Meta's snake_case + nullables) +
  `summariseInsights()` for the dashboard widget.
- **`app/api/integrations/meta_ads/ad-accounts/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  client-or-operator (`requireClientAccess` тАФ the Meta ad account
  belongs to the customer). `action: 'list'` returns the ad accounts
  the connected user can manage + the FB Pages they own (lead-gen ads
  need a Page); `action: 'select'` persists the chosen ad account +
  captures `customer_agreed_by_email` for audit AND fires an immediate
  `meta_sync_campaigns` job so the customer sees their campaigns on
  `/campaigns` within seconds. Returns 503 when Meta is unconfigured.
- **`app/api/integrations/meta_ads/campaigns/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  operator-only (`requireOperatorForClient`). `action: 'pause' |
  'activate'` flips a campaign on Meta + updates the local row.
  Operator-only тАФ flipping campaign status is governance under the
  managed-service model, distinct from owning the underlying Meta
  connection. The previous `launch` action was removed when V1 moved
  campaign building to Meta Ads Manager (`LaunchMetaCampaignButton`
  deep-links there).
- **`app/api/integrations/meta_ads/sync/route.ts`** тАФ `POST`,
  client-or-operator (`requireClientAccess` тАФ refreshing data for
  the caller's own client is a read action, same as GBP's "Sync now").
  Two shapes: `{ clientId }` fires `meta_sync_campaigns` for the
  whole ad account (campaign discovery тАФ what the "тЖ╗ Sync campaigns"
  button on `/campaigns` calls); `{ clientId, metaCampaignDbId }`
  fires per-campaign `meta_sync_insights` + `meta_sync_leads` for one
  row with widened windows (7d insights, 24h leads).
- **`components/shared/settings/MetaAdAccountPickerModal.tsx`** тАФ
  `'use client'`. Post-OAuth ad-account picker. Auto-opens from
  `IntegrationConnectionsSection` on the Meta success URL. Picks an
  account + collects the customer agreement email + the
  acknowledgement checkbox. Sibling of `GbpLocationPickerModal`.
- **`components/shared/settings/MetaAdAccountFooter.tsx`** тАФ
  `'use client'`. The in-row summary block below the Meta connection
  row on sub-account `/settings/integrations` тАФ ad-account name +
  currency + status + balance + Change ad account. Sibling of the
  GBP `GbpConnectionFooter`. Self-prompts to pick an account when
  OAuth-connected but no account is wired yet.
- **`components/admin/campaigns/LaunchMetaCampaignButton.tsx`** тАФ
  `'use client'`. The admin `/campaigns` action row тАФ two buttons
  side by side: **тЖ╗ Sync campaigns** (fires `useSyncMetaAccountCampaigns`,
  the whole-account ingest; settles into a "Queued тЬУ" 3-second
  confirmation) and **Open Meta Ads Manager тЖТ** (opens
  `business.facebook.com/adsmanager/manage/campaigns?act={id}` in a
  new tab, with `&business_id=` when present, scoping to the
  customer's Business Manager). Disabled in agency mode (pick a
  client) and when no ad account is wired (link to
  `/settings/integrations` first). The in-app launch wizard was
  removed тАФ V1 manages campaigns directly in Meta Ads Manager.
- **`lib/campaigns/queries.tsx`** *(extended)* тАФ added
  `fetchMetaMetricsByCampaignId()` and `fetchMetaWeeklyTrend()`. The
  admin roster's per-row cells (LEADS / SPEND / CPL) now show real
  7-day numbers when a `meta_campaigns` row exists; the workspace
  `LEADS ┬╖ 7D` stat tile sums across all Meta-linked campaigns. The
  client deep-dive's metrics + 4-week trend chart light up from the
  same data. Campaigns with no Meta linkage continue to render the
  honest `тАФ` + "Awaiting Meta Ads" placeholders.

#### Meta Ads тАФ operator setup

> One-time + per-customer steps. The Meta side is the longest setup of
> any Phase 7 integration тАФ App Review can take weeks.

1. Create a Meta App at developers.facebook.com (Meta for Developers
   account required тАФ allow ~1 day for developer account verification
   if you don't have one).
2. Complete **Meta business verification** for Webnua (the developer
   dashboard surfaces the flow). Allow 3-10 business days.
3. Submit **App Review** for the sensitive permissions Webnua needs:
   `ads_management`, `ads_read`, `business_management`, `pages_show_list`,
   `pages_manage_ads`, `leads_retrieval`. Each typically takes 1-3 weeks
   per submission and may bounce on first attempt тАФ Meta's reviewers
   need clear demo screencasts showing the operator flow. Apply for
   **Advanced Access** on each approved permission (a separate review).
4. While App Review is in progress, you can test with **test users**
   added on the Developer dashboard тАФ they can grant the sensitive
   permissions without review.
5. Register the OAuth redirect URI on the App's Facebook Login product:
   `{app origin}/api/integrations/meta_ads/callback` тАФ must match byte
   for byte.
6. Set the env vars (`.env.local` for dev, the deployment env for
   production): `META_APP_ID`, `META_APP_SECRET`. Optional:
   `META_API_VERSION` (defaults to `v21.0`; bump periodically as Meta
   deprecates older versions), `META_OAUTH_REDIRECT_URI_BASE` (defaults
   to `{app origin}/api/integrations`).
7. Per client: either the customer themselves OR the operator initiates
   Meta connect on `/settings/integrations` тЖТ customer signs into their
   own Facebook account тЖТ grants permissions on their Business Manager
   + ad account + the Page that will host ads тЖТ callback redirects back
   to Webnua and `MetaAdAccountPickerModal` auto-opens to pick the ad
   account + capture the customer's agreement email.
8. Operator builds the customer's first campaign **directly in Meta
   Ads Manager**. From admin `/campaigns` (sub-account mode), the
   **Open Meta Ads Manager тЖТ** button deep-links to the connected
   ad account in Ads Manager (`business.facebook.com/adsmanager`). The
   operator's business-manager access (granted by the customer's
   OAuth consent) lets them create campaigns / ad sets / lead forms /
   creatives / ads in Meta's own UI. Webnua's `/campaigns` surface is
   for cross-client performance rollup + the in-app pause/resume
   affordance, not campaign building.
9. **Manual тВм200 funding (month 1, V1 only)**: Webnua transfers тВм200
   to the customer's ad account out-of-band before the campaign
   publishes. The exact mechanism depends on how the customer's ad
   account is funded тАФ if prepaid (most common), Webnua sends them
   тВм200 via Stripe Transfer / SEPA / similar and the customer tops up
   their Meta funding source manually. Document the per-customer
   process in the operator playbook. **V2** will automate via Meta's
   funding APIs.
10. Meta bills the customer's card directly for ad spend тАФ Webnua
    manages the campaign in Ads Manager (creative, targeting, budget,
    scaling).

### `shared/website/` тАФ website hub + section editor shell (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 3 тЖТ 3.5)
