> **Architectural note тАФ `/website` is shared between roles.** Lives at top-level `app/website/` (moved out of `(client)/` in Session 3) with its own `layout.tsx` ('use client', reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`). The hub page (`app/website/page.tsx`) renders header/footer/nav cards + page grid for the active workspace's website. The page editor lives at `app/website/[pageId]/page.tsx`; two reserved sibling routes `app/website/header/page.tsx` and `app/website/footer/page.tsx` take precedence over `[pageId]` and mount the editor in singleton mode (design doc ┬з2.6). The agency-level cross-client matrix lives separately at `app/(admin)/websites/` (admin-only).

> **Architectural note тАФ `Website` тЙа `Funnel`.** Per design doc ┬з2.0, a website (multi-page, shared chrome) and a funnel (linear sequence, no chrome) are independent artefacts that share the section registry and the client's brand but nothing else. A client's home page is **not** their funnel's landing page. Session 3.5 pinned the website page types to `'home' | 'about' | 'services' | 'contact' | 'generic'` and added website-level singletons (`header`, `footer`) plus a flat `nav: NavLink[]` capped at 6 items. Funnel types (`Funnel`, `FunnelStep`, `FunnelStepType`) live shape-only in `lib/funnel/types.ts` until Session 7 wires the funnel editor.

- **`PageGridCard`** (`website/PageGridCard.tsx`) тАФ single page card on the website hub. Prototype-aligned shape: per-page-type wireframe thumbnail (`PageThumbnail`, paper-2 surface) with a green-dot LIVE pill in the top-right when the website has a published version; rust mono URL line (domain ┬╖ slug) with a leading good-dot; bold page title; a 2-up stat row keyed by page type (`// VISITS 30D` + a variant cell тАФ V1 ships AVG TIME for every page type; BOUNCE / SUBMITS / FUNNEL CTR are Session B once `analytics_funnel_daily` gets the `page_ref` PK extension, see audit ┬з2.2); EDITED-Nd-AGO meta with `BY YOU` (rust) / `BY WEBNUA` (info); paper-2 footer with split View (live page in a new tab, inert + tooltip when unpublished) + Edit (`/website/[pageId]`) buttons. Per-page totals come from `fetchPageTotalsByRef`, fetched once at the hub level and passed down keyed by slug.
- **`PageThumbnail`** (`website/PageThumbnail.tsx`) тАФ small CSS "wireframe gist" of a page's visual structure, used by `PageGridCard`. Per-page-type silhouettes: `home` = hero band + 3 service chips + text bars; `about` = image block + text bars; `services` = list rows with rust + good dots + a "+ NEW SERVICE" pill; `contact` = form bars + map placeholder with a rust pin; `generic` = simple text bars. Pure CSS тАФ no SVG, no real screenshots. A real-screenshot pipeline is V2 (CLAUDE.md "Public site rendering" gap).
- **`SingletonStrip`** (`website/SingletonStrip.tsx`) тАФ full-width Header / Footer card on `/website`. Replaces the previous 3-up `SingletonCard` row (Header / Footer / Nav as equal-width cards) тАФ the strips now sit ABOVE and BELOW the page grid to mirror the rendered website's visual position. Header strip folds in the nav-link list (no separate Nav card anymore); the link count appears in the strip's meta line. Each strip is a `next/link` to its editor + carries a wireframe gist (header: logo + nav-link mono labels + rust CTA pill; footer: 3-col ink bg with paper-tinted link bars + legal line).
- **`WebsiteHero`** (`website/WebsiteHero.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg hero at the top of `/website`, built on the `inkHeroSurface` recipe (`lib/ink-hero.ts`). Left side: rust LIVE pill carrying the live domain + a good-dot prefix, "Your website + funnel" headline (rust `<em>`), explainer copy that flags funnel pages as Webnua-managed, primary "+ Request a change" CTA (routes to `/tickets/new?from=request-change&category=website`) + secondary "тЖЧ Preview live site" (`href=https://{domain}`, inert "Not published yet" placeholder when unpublished). Right side: translucent stat card with `// SITE PERFORMANCE ┬╖ 30 DAYS ┬╖ LIVE` header, MONTHLY VISITS + PAGE SPEED in a 2-up grid, and a 30-day visit-trend sparkline rendered as an inline SVG polyline with a soft rust area fill. Reads via `fetchSurfacePageTotals` + the new `fetchPageVisitsDaily` (analytics queries).
- **`WebsiteActivityCard`** (`website/WebsiteActivityCard.tsx`) тАФ "Recent website activity" panel on `/website`. Thin adapter over the shared `ActivityFeed` primitive тАФ maps `useWebsiteVersions` results into `ActivityRowData[]` with rust tone for the signed-in user's edits, info tone for Webnua's, good tone + тЖС glyph for publish events. V1 sources from version metadata only; per-section / per-field edit attribution is the same backend follow-up flagged alongside the per-page analytics gap (audit ┬з2.2 / Session B).
- **`OpenRequestsCard`** (`website/OpenRequestsCard.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg "Open requests" panel on the right of `/website`'s bottom row. Reads via `useClientTicketsInbox` filtered to `website` + `website-approval` categories with `status !== 'done'`; surfaces the most recent awaiting-reply ticket as a deep-linked inner card (`// AWAITING YOUR REPLY` + title + age + `TAP TO ANSWER тЖТ`) above a primary "+ Request a change" CTA. All-caught-up state mounts a paper/[0.04] placeholder when no open tickets match.
- **`WebsiteEngagementCard`** (`website/WebsiteEngagementCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` visitor-engagement insights card mounted above the page grid on `/website`. Three panels in one card (analytics-audit ┬з3 / ┬з4): **Scroll depth** (% of visitors reaching 25 / 50 / 75 / 90 тАФ pre-migration-0041 only the 50% slice surfaced, as the canonical `engaged` stage), **Top CTAs by clicks** (per-`element_label` rollup from migration 0041, top-5 by count, fed by `fetchSurfaceClickBreakdown`), and **Form completion** (Started / Abandoned / Submitted minus failed, with a warn note when failed > 0). Window-bounded by `ANALYTICS_WINDOW_DAYS` (7d). Loading + empty states render the card chrome so the layout doesn't jump once data lands. Takes `surfaceId: string` (the website id).
- **`VersionHistoryCard`** (`website/VersionHistoryCard.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg list of recent versions for a website. Same visual chrome as `client/funnels/FunnelHistoryCard` (rust radial-gradient flourish, dotted-bottom-bordered rows) but reads the Session 2 `Version` model. Each row: status pill (LIVE = rust fill for the currently-live one; DRAFT = paper/12 on ink; PENDING = warn-soft; archived = rust/18 on rust-light) + notes + mono timestamp. Props: `title`, `subtitle`, `versions: Version[]`, `currentPublishedId: string | null` (drives which row shows the rust LIVE pill). **Session 8** added the rollback affordance: pass `websiteId` and every non-current published / archived row gets a "тЖ║ Restore" button calling `restoreVersionAsDraft` (behind a `window.confirm`). Restore is disabled while a pending submission is in flight (a warn banner explains). `allowRestore` (default true when `websiteId` is set) opts a read-only surface out.
- **`PagePreviewPane`** (`website/PagePreviewPane.tsx`) тАФ the editor's main pane (Phase 6 ┬╖ rail removal: there is no left section rail). Renders **every** section's `<Preview>` stacked тАФ disabled ones dimmed with a "Hidden" badge so they stay re-enableable. Clicking a section selects it; clicking an element inside the selected section selects that element. Per-section management is the `SectionHoverToolbar`; an `+ Add section` button sits at the foot. Management chrome shows only when the management callbacks are passed (omitted by the wizard walk / singleton mode). The `device` prop (`desktop` | `tablet` | `mobile`) constrains the canvas width so the sections' container queries render the matching responsive layout. Props: `sections`, `brand`, `device`, `selectedSectionId`/`onSelectSection`, `selectedElementId`/`onSelectElement`, and the optional `onToggleSectionEnabled`/`onRemoveSection`/`onMoveSection`/`onDuplicateSection`/`onRequestAddSection`.
- **`SectionHoverToolbar`** (`website/SectionHoverToolbar.tsx`) тАФ the floating per-section controls in the preview (replaces the old left-rail row). Move up/down + show/hide (`editLayout`-gated), duplicate + delete (`editSections`-gated). Appears on hover; pinned visible while the section is selected. Every handler stops propagation.
- **`EditorToolbar`** (`website/EditorToolbar.tsx`) тАФ top bar of the section editor. Discriminated `mode: { kind: 'tabs', tabs, activeTabId, backHref? } | { kind: 'breadcrumb', label, backHref? }`. **Tabs**: one pill per `EditorToolbarTab` (`{ id, label, href }`), ink-active for the current; `backHref` defaults to `/website` for website editing and is passed `/funnels/[id]` for funnel-step editing. **Breadcrumb**: static mono uppercase line (used by `/website/header` and `/website/footer`). Middle slot: `AutosaveIndicator` (when `autosave` prop is provided тАФ Session 5 (A) wired this against the real `useAutosave` hook; omitted in static demos). Right slot: View live тЖЧ + the publish action following design-doc ┬з3.3 (Publish тЖТ / Submit for review тЖТ / hidden). Session 5 props: `autosave?` (status/lastSavedAt/onRetry), `publishDisabled?` (hides both publish actions тАФ used by the Lane B editor lock AND by the funnel-step editor where publish isn't wired yet), `onPublish?` / `onSubmitForReview?` (real handlers replacing the visual-stub buttons from Session 3), `publishMenu?` (slot for the `ForcePublishMenu` chevron тАФ chunk F). **Session 7** swapped the `website: Website` prop for a plain `domain: string` so the toolbar can mount over either a website OR a funnel without coupling to either model.
- **`AutosaveIndicator`** (`website/AutosaveIndicator.tsx`) тАФ Session 5 (A). The mono pill in the toolbar middle slot. Five states from the `useAutosave` hook result: `idle` (no edits yet тАФ static good dot, "Autosaved"), `pending` (within the 500ms debounce window тАФ rust pulse, "EditingтАж"), `saving` (brief тАФ rust pulse, "SavingтАж"), `synced` (settled тАФ static good dot, "Saved Ns ago" with a 5s re-tick interval so the relative text stays current without parent rerenders), `failed` (button тАФ warn dot, "Save failed ┬╖ retry тЖ╗" calling `onRetry`).
- **`SectionEditor`** (`website/SectionEditor.tsx`) тАФ composes the toolbar + rail + preview pane + fields panel and owns the editor's local state (selected section id, locally-mutated section list). **Session 7** added a third mode discriminator and moved `website` from a top-level prop onto each website-bound mode entry, so the editor takes a single `mode` prop:
  - `{ kind: 'page', website, pages, page }` тАФ website page editor; page tabs in toolbar.
  - `{ kind: 'singleton', website, section, label }` тАФ website header / footer editor; breadcrumb in toolbar.
  - `{ kind: 'funnelStep', funnel, steps, step }` тАФ funnel-step editor; step tabs prefixed `01 ┬╖`, `02 ┬╖`, `03 ┬╖`. **Publish + Lane B are wired (A3)**: the toolbar routes through `/funnels/[id]/review` (`reviewHref`), the Lane B lock resolves via `useUserPendingFunnelSubmission`. Autosave wires through with a funnel-keyed `DraftSlot`.

  Brand resolves through the client either way: website mode reads `website.clientId`, funnel mode reads `funnel.clientId`, both via `getBrandForClient` (one brand per client, design doc ┬з2.3). Layout (Phase 6 ┬╖ rail removal) is **`[preview 1fr | fields 400px]`** when a section is selected, full-width preview otherwise тАФ no left rail; section management is the in-preview `SectionHoverToolbar`. Section state runs through `useUndoableState` (toolbar undo/redo). **Singleton mode auto-selects** the only section so the fields panel is visible immediately. The `+ Add section` button opens `AddSectionDialog` (the registry-driven section picker тАФ see below); picking a type appends a fresh section seeded from the registry's `defaultData()` and selects it. **Session 5 wiring:** the editor feeds every mutation through `useAutosave`, rehydrates initial state from `loadDraftSections`, and publish routes through a review surface (`reviewHref` тАФ `/website/review` for website modes, `/funnels/[id]/review` for funnel mode, A3). **Lane B lock**: `useUserPendingSubmission(websiteId, user.id)` (websites) **or** `useUserPendingFunnelSubmission(funnelId, user.id)` (funnels, A3) returns the submitter's pending submission if one exists; when present the `WebsiteEditorPendingBanner` mounts above the toolbar with `surface="website" | "funnel"`, the rail + preview opacity-65 + pointer-events:none, the fields panel hides, autosave pauses, and the `ForcePublishMenu` is hidden via `publishMenu hidden={locked}`. Operators never see the lock тАФ it only lights up for the user who submitted.
- **`AddSectionDialog`** (`website/AddSectionDialog.tsx`) тАФ the section picker behind the rail's `+ Add section` button. `Dialog size="default"` listing every implemented section type valid for the current `ContainerKind` (`getSectionsForContainer` тАФ `page` for page/funnel-step editors). Each row is the section's `// LABEL` + description; clicking one fires `onAdd(type)` and closes. `SectionEditor` owns the open state and the append logic.
- **`WebsiteEditorPendingBanner`** (`website/WebsiteEditorPendingBanner.tsx`) тАФ Session 5 (D). Warn-tinted top banner that mounts above the editor for a Lane B submitter while their submission is pending operator review. Renders the submitted-at timestamp + the fields-changed/sections-changed summary from `submission.diff` + two affordances: "Open ticket тЖТ" (deep-links to `/tickets`) and "Recall submission тЖй" (after a `window.confirm`; the submitter's draft slots are untouched so recall resumes editing exactly where they left off). **`surface: 'website' | 'funnel'`** (A3) discriminates the recall write тАФ `recallSubmission` vs `recallFunnelSubmission`; the banner reads only the shared `id`/`submittedAt`/`diff` fields, so one component serves both lanes. `reviewerName` defaults to `'Craig'` (the one admin stub user).
- **`ForcePublishMenu`** (`website/ForcePublishMenu.tsx`) тАФ Session 5 (F). Break-glass "skip approval" affordance тАФ chevron menu to the right of the rust "Publish тЖТ" button, admin-only via call-site `role === 'admin'` check (design doc ┬з2.4: NOT a separate capability). Two-stage confirm: (1) menu open, (2) reason-required dialog. The confirm dialog uses `Dialog size="default"` (560px), warn-tinted header, required `Textarea` reason, warn "Force publish тЪб" CTA stays disabled until the reason field has non-whitespace content. Confirm calls `publishDraft({ force: { reason } })` which both publishes AND writes a `ForcePublishEntry` to the audit overlay. `hidden` prop returns null when set (used by `SectionEditor` to drop the menu when the publish button itself is disabled тАФ Lane B lock).
- **`SeoPanel`** (`website/SeoPanel.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` site-wide SEO editor `Dialog`. Lists every page (website mode) or every funnel step (funnel mode) with its meta title + description, char counters, a per-row `тЬж Regen`, and a master `тЬж Auto-fill all` that drafts metadata for the whole site in one click. Generic over websites + funnels тАФ both pass `SeoPanelTarget[]` + an `onSave` (website тЖТ `saveSeoForPages`, funnel тЖТ `saveSeoForSteps`). Opened from the `EditorToolbar` `seo` slot тАФ a `тЬж SEO` button `SectionEditor` renders when `editSEO` is held and the mode is not singleton/locked. Title + description only (the preflight blockers); ogImage deferred. AI generation runs through `lib/website/seo-generate.ts` (`generateSeo` тЖТ the Claude route, deterministic fallback). SEO writes straight to the draft version snapshot (not the `content_drafts` section buffer тАФ `mergeDraftsIntoSnapshot` preserves `page.seo`).
- **`SectionFieldsPanel`** (`website/SectionFieldsPanel.tsx`) тАФ third column of the editor, only visible when a section is selected. Header shows the section type's label + description + a Close ├Ч button; body scrolls and mounts the registry's `Fields` component for the selected section. Per-field capability gating happens INSIDE the Fields component (every section's Fields uses `CopyField`/`MediaField`, both of which wrap inputs in `<CapabilityGate mode="request">` so view-only users see the request-change affordance on hover). The panel itself is just chrome. `hideClose` prop suppresses the Close ├Ч in singleton mode (no other section to deselect to). Force-remounts when the selected section changes (`key={section.id}`) so per-field state like `CopyField`'s AI-variant index resets cleanly.
### `shared/website/` (cont'd) тАФ preflight + review surface (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 8)

> **Architectural note тАФ the review surface is the publish gate.** Session 8 (design doc ┬з7) makes the review surface the single place a website publishes from; **A3 extends the same pattern to funnels** (`/funnels/[id]/review`). The editor's `EditorToolbar` never publishes directly: when its `reviewHref` prop is set the two lane buttons collapse into one **"Review & publish тЖТ"** link (`SectionEditor` passes `/website/review` for website modes, `/funnels/[id]/review` for funnel mode). The review surface runs preflight, blocks publish on hard fails, and owns the actual `publishDraft` / `submitForApproval` (websites) or `publishFunnelDraft` / `submitFunnelForApproval` (funnels) calls following the ┬з3.3 capability lane. `/website/review` joins `header` / `footer` as a reserved static sibling; `/funnels/[id]/review` is a reserved sibling of `/funnels/[id]/edit`. **The `ForcePublishMenu` break-glass path is website-only** тАФ funnels have no force-publish (see the A3 divergences in the parked decisions): `force_publish_audit_log` is website-keyed, and a funnel preflight blocker is the operator's own content to fix.

- **`DomainStatusIndicator`** (`website/DomainStatusIndicator.tsx`) тАФ Session 8. Small status pill for a website's primary domain + SSL state. UI ONLY тАФ DNS / cert work is a backend concern (design doc ┬з8: domain management is V2). `sslStatus` drives the dot colour: `live` = good, `pending` = warn pulse, `error` = warn. Renders the primary domain in mono + an alias count when `domain.aliases` is non-empty. Mounted on the `/website` hub and the `/website/review` surface.
- **`ConnectDomainButton`** (`website/ConnectDomainButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'`. Operator affordance on the `/website` hub (mounted next to `DomainStatusIndicator`, behind a `role === 'admin'` check) to point a client's own domain at their site. Opens a `Dialog`: enter a domain тЖТ registers it with the Vercel project via `POST /api/domains` (so HTTPS provisions) AND saves it as the website's `domain_primary` via `setCustomDomain` (`lib/website/mutations.ts` тАФ demotes the old `{slug}.webnua.dev` host to an alias so it keeps resolving). Shows the A / CNAME record to add at the registrar + any Vercel verification records; a "Disconnect" reverts to the `.webnua.dev` host (`clearCustomDomain`). The middleware + `resolveSite` already serve any host тАФ this is the capture/registration UI. Vercel calls go through `lib/website/vercel.ts` (server-only, reads `VERCEL_TOKEN` / `VERCEL_PROJECT_ID` / `VERCEL_TEAM_ID`); unset env тЖТ the domain is still saved, an operator finishes it in the Vercel dashboard. Domain parsing/DNS-record helpers live in `lib/website/domain.ts`.
- **`PreflightChecklist`** (`website/PreflightChecklist.tsx`) тАФ Session 8. Renders a `PreflightReport`: a summary row of pass / warn / fail count chips + the list of warn + fail result rows (passing rules collapse to the green count). Each issue row carries the rule title + message + an optional rust "Fix тЖТ" deep-link to the offending editor. `allClear` reports render a green "all clear" banner instead of the list. Presentation only тАФ publish gating lives on the review surface.
- **`PageReviewCard`** (`website/PageReviewCard.tsx`) тАФ Session 8. One card per page on the review surface. Page-type pill + slug + section count + a lightweight section-stack glyph "thumbnail" (rust bars for enabled sections, paper-2 for disabled) + a per-page preflight roll-up footer (worst status of that page's results). Whole card is a `next/link` to the page editor. Real visual thumbnails wait for a render-to-image backend.

> **Architectural note тАФ funnels are top-level AND shared between roles** (Session 7 relocation). The prototype framed funnels as client-only (Screen 23) and admin interactions via a different page-builder flow, but the platform converged on a single funnel editor that both roles use тАФ admins drive funnel changes day-to-day for clients on managed plans, and the editor's per-field capability layer covers per-user gating. `/funnels` therefore lives at the **top level** (`app/funnels/`) alongside `/website`, `/tickets`, `/leads`, etc., NOT inside `(client)/`. Routes: `/funnels` (context-aware list тАФ agency mode renders the cross-client roster; sub-account / client renders that client's funnels), `/funnels/[id]` (analytics detail with an operator-facing `Edit funnel тЖТ` CTA), `/funnels/[id]/edit/[stepId]` (funnel-step editor тАФ Session 7), `/funnels/[id]/review` (the pre-publish review surface тАФ A3, a reserved static sibling of `edit`). The funnel detail's back link reads "тЖР back to funnels" and points to `/funnels`. **Sidebar:** both the client nav (`lib/nav/client-nav.ts`) AND the admin nav (`lib/nav/admin-nav.ts`) carry a top-level `Funnels` item alongside `Website` / `Websites`. The website hub itself lives at the shared route `app/website/` (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 3); see the `shared/website/` inventory above.

- **`FunnelHero`** (`funnels/FunnelHero.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg banner with rust radial-gradient flourish + a paired `FunnelAggCard` on the right. Props: `back: { label, href }` (renders as `тЖР {label}` mono link), `tag` (rust-light mono pill with ЁЯФТ glyph), `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust-light), `subtitle` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = paper-bold), `meta: FunnelHeroMeta[]` (mono `LABEL` + paper-bold value pairs, e.g. `BUILT 14d ago`), `versionLabel` (optional rust-light pill), `actions: { viewLiveLabel, viewLiveHref, requestChangeLabel, requestChangeHref, editFunnelLabel?, editFunnelHref? }` (ghost View live + primary Request-change + optional Session 7 `Edit funnel тЖТ` button rendered when caller passes both `editFunnel*` strings тАФ gate upstream on edit caps), `agg: FunnelAggCardProps`. Grid is `1.4fr 1fr`. **Standalone тАФ not extracted into a shared `InkHero` primitive (see parked decisions; this is the 4th ink-hero data point).**
- **`FunnelAggCard`** (`funnels/FunnelAggCard.tsx`) тАФ translucent-on-ink metric tile used inside `FunnelHero`. Props: `label` (mono eyebrow), `live` (renders the pulsing good-dot LIVE indicator), `metrics: [FunnelAggMetric, FunnelAggMetric]` (2-up grid; `num` is ReactNode so `<em>412</em>` highlights rust-light, plus mono label + optional trend in good-green), `bottom?: { left, right }` (border-topped revenue row).
- **`FunnelFlow`** (`funnels/FunnelFlow.tsx`) тАФ white card containing the 3-step row + 2 arrows + period toggle in its header. Props: `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust), `steps: FunnelStep[]`, `arrows: FunnelArrow[]` (rendered between consecutive steps via `flatMap`; arrow `n` sits between step `n` and `n+1`), `periods: FunnelPeriod[]`, `defaultPeriod?: FunnelPeriod`. Grid is `1fr 100px 1fr 100px 1fr` тАФ widened from the prototype's 40px so the pct pill + wrapped drop-off captions fit cleanly without overflowing into neighbouring step cards. Currently rendering 3 steps; the column template would need to extend for 4+ (out of scope for the stub layer).
- **`FunnelStepCard`** (`funnels/FunnelStepCard.tsx`) тАФ per-step paper-bg card. `step: FunnelStep` does all the work; the `tone` field (`'first' | 'middle' | 'last'`) drives the colour treatment: `first` = rust-soft gradient + rust accent; `last` = good-soft gradient + good accent; `middle` = plain paper + rust accent. Composes `FunnelStepThumbnail` for the visual gist. Hover lifts -translate-y-0.5 + shadow-card.
- **`FunnelStepThumbnail`** (`funnels/FunnelStepThumbnail.tsx`) тАФ small 64px-tall CSS "preview gist" of each step. `variant: 'landing' | 'schedule' | 'thanks'`. Pure visual, no business logic. Already used by both the detail view's step cards AND the funnels list row, so it's a real shared-within-funnels primitive тАФ kept in `client/funnels/` because both consumers are client-only.
- **`FunnelArrow`** (`funnels/FunnelArrow.tsx`) тАФ between-steps cell: rust-soft conversion-rate pill on top, line + `тЖТ` glyph in the middle, mono drop-off caption below (`<strong>` renders in warn-red for emphasis on the drop count).
- **`FunnelPeriodToggle`** (`funnels/FunnelPeriodToggle.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` pill toggle for time-range (7D / 14D / 30D / 90D). Local `useState` active state тАФ fine for the stub layer; lift to a callback or URL state when real period filtering wires up. Optional `onChange` is plumbed but the stub doesn't need it.
- **`FunnelInsightsCard`** (`funnels/FunnelInsightsCard.tsx`) тАФ white-surface "// Insights ┬╖ what we see" list. Props: `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust), optional `subtitle`, `items: FunnelInsight[]`. Sibling export **`FunnelInsightRow`** renders one row тАФ a 28px tone-tinted icon glyph + body (with `<em>` = rust, `<strong>` = ink-bold) + mono meta line. Severity tones: `warn` (warn-tinted), `good` (good-tinted), `info` (rust-soft).
- **`FunnelHistoryCard`** (`funnels/FunnelHistoryCard.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg version history list with a rust radial-gradient flourish. Props: `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust-light), optional `subtitle`, `items: FunnelVersion[]`, `ctaLabel`, `ctaHref` (rendered through `Button asChild` + `next/link`, full-width below the list). Sibling export **`FunnelHistoryItem`** renders one row тАФ version pill (`current` = rust-filled, others = rust-light on rust/18) + body text + mono meta line + right-aligned mono timestamp. **Not** a `RailCard` тАФ the heading rhythm and the version-pill column make it its own shape.

### `lib/funnels/` тАФ funnels stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for funnel shapes: `FunnelStepThumbVariant` (`landing` | `schedule` | `thanks`), `FunnelStepTone` (`first` | `middle` | `last`), `FunnelStep`, `FunnelArrow`, `FunnelPeriod` + `FUNNEL_PERIOD_LABEL`, `FunnelInsight` + `FunnelInsightTone`, `FunnelVersion`, `FunnelAggMetric` + `FunnelAggBottom`, `FunnelHeroMeta`, and the top-level `FunnelDetail` that ties it all together (back link, hero, agg, flow config, steps, arrows, insights, history).
- **`client-detail.tsx`** тАФ `voltlineFunnel`: the single canonical Voltline "$99 emergency call-out" funnel stub matching client Screen 23 (412 тЖТ 74 тЖТ 14, three insights, three versions). `.tsx` because titles / subtitles / metric numbers / insight bodies all carry inline `<em>` / `<strong>` JSX. Reshape into Supabase reads when the backend lands.

### `lib/tickets/` тАФ tickets stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for ticket shapes: `TicketStatus = 'open' | 'in_progress' | 'blocked' | 'done'` (admin's vocabulary is the stored one тАФ client's `Review` is derived view-time via `StatusPill reviewAware` when status is `in_progress` and `awaiting === 'client'`), `TicketUrgency`, `TicketCategory`, `TicketAwaiting` (`'operator' | 'client' | null` тАФ drives both the client row's attention pill and the derived `Review` label), `TicketTab`, plus the `CATEGORY_LABEL` / `STATUS_LABEL` / `URGENCY_LABEL` maps.
- **`client-tickets.tsx`** тАФ hero + tab config + the `ClientTicketRow` type: `clientTicketsHero` (props for `TicketsHero`), `clientTicketTabs` (Active / Needs your reply / Done / All), `ClientTicketRow`. `.tsx` because hero copy carries inline JSX. (The `clientTickets` row data stub was removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)
- **`admin-tickets.tsx`** тАФ hero + tab config + the row types: `adminTicketsHero` (props for `TicketsHero` with 4 stat tiles), `adminTicketTabs` (All / Open / In progress / Blocked / Done), `AdminTicketRow`, `AdminTicketHeroStat`, `AdminTicketClientTone` (`voltline` / `freshhome` / `keyhero` / `flowline` / `generic`). (The `adminTickets` row data stub was removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)
- **`client-detail.tsx`** тАФ the client-view detail **types** only: `ClientTicketDetail`, `TicketDetailMessage`, `TicketDetailProperty`, `TicketDetailAction` (the admin stub reuses the message/property/action shapes). (The `clientTicketDetail` data stub was removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup; `queries.tsx` maps live reads to these types.)
- **`admin-detail.tsx`** тАФ the `AdminTicketDetail` **type** only; imports the message/property/action shapes from `client-detail.tsx`. (The `adminTicketDetail` data stub was removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)
- **`request-change.ts`** тАФ `buildRequestChangeHref(params)` тАФ the single source of truth for the `/tickets/new` URL a request-change affordance routes to. Takes optional `{ capability, pageId, sectionId, fieldKey }`, returns `/tickets/new?from=request-change&category=website&тАж`. Consumed by `CapabilityGate`'s default `request`-mode behaviour; the `NewTicketForm` reads the params back to prefill + show its context banner.
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ **Phase 3 ┬╖ the whole tickets cluster (inbox + detail + `/tickets/new`) is wired to live Supabase data.** `useClientTicketsInbox()` / `useAdminTicketsInbox()` тАФ TanStack Query hooks over a shared `tickets` fetch (RLS bounds the rows; the dispatch only picks the row shape). `useClientTicketDetail(reference)` / `useAdminTicketDetail(reference)` тАФ one ticket by display `reference` + its full `ticket_messages` thread, composed into a `ClientTicketDetail` / `AdminTicketDetail` (the by-reference `.single()` resolves as `not_found` for a ticket outside the caller's tenant). `useCreateTicket()` тАФ a `useMutation` that inserts a `tickets` row + its opening `ticket_messages` row (allocating the next `TKT-NNNN` reference, retrying on the unique-constraint clash), then invalidates the inbox query. `useReplyToTicket()` тАФ a `useMutation` (backs the `TicketReply` composer in both roles) that resolves the ticket UUID from its display `reference`, inserts a non-draft `ticket_messages` row, and flips the ticket's `awaiting` to whichever party did not just reply. Presentation-only stub fields (`preview`, `statusLabel` / `statusHeadline` / `metaLine`, `statusDescription`, `properties` rows, the `meta` blurb) are derived/composed here from `tickets` / `ticket_messages` / `users` / `clients` per design ┬з5 #3 тАФ hence `.tsx`. The action affordances (`actions`, `statusOptions`, reply `chips`) are static UI composed here, not data. The `client-tickets.tsx` / `admin-tickets.tsx` files supply **only** hero copy + tab config (`*TicketsHero`, `*TicketTabs`) + the row **types** (`ClientTicketRow`, `AdminTicketRow`); `client-detail.tsx` / `admin-detail.tsx` hold **only** the detail **types** (`ClientTicketDetail`, `AdminTicketDetail`, `TicketDetailMessage`/`Property`/`Action`). The dead row + detail data stubs were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup; `queries.tsx` maps live reads to the surviving types.
- **RLS note (migration `0020_ticket_cluster_rls_fixes`).** Wiring this cluster surfaced two RLS gaps, fixed by migration 0020: (1) `users_select` hid operator (admin) rows from clients тАФ but the client must see the named operator replying on the thread, so operator rows are now visible to every authenticated user; (2) `ticket_messages_select` leaked operator *draft* replies (`is_draft = true`) to clients тАФ drafts are now operator-only, so the same ticket query serves both roles (RLS drops drafts for a client viewer, keeps them for the operator).

### `shared/leads/` тАФ lead inbox + detail + conversation (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 1)

> **Architectural note тАФ leads lives outside the role route groups**, same reason as settings / tickets / dashboard. Routes: `/leads` (inbox), `/leads/[id]` (detail), `/leads/[id]/conversation` (conversation). `app/leads/layout.tsx` (`'use client'`, reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`). Each page is a `'use client'` dispatcher with `_client-content.tsx` / `_admin-content.tsx` siblings. The detail + conversation pages reuse `TicketDetailLayout` directly (same `1fr 320px` shape). For the stub layer, the `[id]` slug is decorative тАФ both roles render their single canonical Sarah Davies stub regardless of the actual id.

- **`LeadsHero`** (`leads/LeadsHero.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg rust-tagged hero used by the admin inbox. Props: `tag` (mono pill string), `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust), `subtitle` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = paper-bold), optional `right` slot. Visually same chrome as `TicketsHero` (the 5th ink-hero data point тАФ see parked decisions; still hold-pattern, no extraction).
- **`LeadTabsBar`** (`leads/LeadTabsBar.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` pill-tab strip with counts. Same shape as `TicketTabsBar` тАФ supports uncontrolled (`defaultActiveId`) or controlled (`value` + `onChange`) use; the `/leads` content files run it controlled and filter their row list + recompute tab counts from the active tab. Takes the leads-typed `LeadTab[]`. Kept separate from `TicketTabsBar` to keep type boundaries clean тАФ if a third surface needs the same pattern, extract to a generic `TabsBar` primitive.
- **`LeadRow`** (`leads/LeadRow.tsx`) тАФ single canonical row, discriminated by `variant: 'client' | 'admin'`. Both variants share the `unread` тЖТ left rust rail + faint rust bg attention treatment. Client variant: `44px + 1fr + auto + auto + 70px` grid тАФ avatar + name+preview (with suburb prefix in mono) + `LeadStatusPill` + optional `LeadUrgencyPill` + age. Admin variant: `36px + 180px + 1fr + 110px + 90px + 100px` grid тАФ tone-tinted avatar + name+`LeadClientPill` + preview + `LeadStatusPill` + age + tone-coloured activity meta (`good`/`rust`/`quiet`).
- **`LeadDetailHeader`** (`leads/LeadDetailHeader.tsx`) тАФ top-of-detail row: 48px avatar + name + comma-joined meta parts (phone bolded via `<strong>`, suburb, email) + optional `clientPillLabel` (admin uses this for the "FreshHome" pill). `rightActions` slot is open for future per-role overflow.
- **`LeadStatusSwitcher`** (`leads/LeadStatusSwitcher.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` mono-uppercase segmented control: `// STATUS` label + 5 status buttons (New / Contacted / Booked / Completed / Lost). Active = ink-bg paper-text. Local `useState` тАФ lift when status mutation wires to backend.
- **`LeadTimeline`** + **`LeadTimelineEventRow`** (`leads/LeadTimeline.tsx`) тАФ activity-timeline list: heading + `N EVENTS ┬╖ NEWEST FIRST` mono meta on the right + vertically-stacked events. Each `LeadTimelineEvent` carries a `dot` type (`sms-in` / `sms-out` / `form` / `status` / `email` / `scheduled-sms` / `scheduled-email`), `meta` (ReactNode), optional `body` + `snippet` (rendered in a tinted bordered block matching dot type), optional right-aligned `rightTime`, and `pending: true` for opacity-dimmed scheduled future events. `auto: true` adds the inline `тд┐ AUTO` pill in the meta row.
- The leads side-rail uses the shared **`RailCard`** (with the `rows` shorthand) + **`RailPropertyRow`** тАФ see the `shared/` rail-primitives entry below. (The former `LeadRailCard` / `LeadRailRowItem` were merged into `RailCard` in Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6.)
- **`LeadQuickActions`** + **`LeadQuickActionItem`** (`leads/LeadQuickActions.tsx`) тАФ vertical button stack used inside the `// QUICK ACTIONS` rail card. Each `LeadQuickAction` is `{ icon, label, primary?, href? }` тАФ `primary: true` renders rust-filled (used by Call Sarah back now / Open conversation); others render bordered ghost. When `href` is set the item is a `next/link`; otherwise a `<button>`.
- **`LeadStatusPill`** / **`LeadUrgencyPill`** / **`LeadClientPill`** (`leads/pills.tsx`) тАФ three small pills exported together. `LeadStatusPill` tones: `new` (rust) / `contacted` (info) / `booked` (good) / `completed` (ink) / `lost` (quiet); optional `label` override. `LeadUrgencyPill` tones: `asap`/`today` (warn) / `soon` (quiet); `none` renders nothing. `LeadClientPill` is a colour-tinted client-name pill driven by `LeadClientTone` (`voltline` / `freshhome` / `keyhero` / `neatworks` / `flowline` / `generic`) тАФ used in the admin row to attribute leads to their client.
- **`ConversationHeader`** (`leads/ConversationHeader.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` top-of-conversation row: avatar + name + meta + optional channel-tabs (All / SMS / Email) + optional `actions` (call / chevron / overflow glyphs). Local `useState` for active channel тАФ visual stub for the stub layer.
- **`ConversationThread`** + **`ConversationMessageRow`** + **`ConversationDayDivider`** (`leads/ConversationThread.tsx`) тАФ message-thread wrapper. Days are rendered with a centred mono day-divider pill; each `ConversationMessage` is rendered with a kind-discriminated bubble: `incoming` (paper card on left), `outgoing` (ink on right), `auto` (rust-tinted on right with inline `тд┐ AUTO` meta), `system` (centred paper-2 mono pill). Bubble metadata (channel / timestamp / `DELIVERED` flag / `metaPrefix` like "SARAH" / "LISA") is rendered in mono uppercase below the bubble. **Not** built on `TicketThreadMessage` because the meta-row vocabulary (AUTO tag, DELIVERED, channel) diverges enough that composition wouldn't simplify the call site.
- **`ConversationComposer`** (`leads/ConversationComposer.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` reply composer at the bottom of the conversation card. Two channel-control modes: `channels: ['SMS', 'Email']` renders a top pill-tab strip (client variant); `channelToggle: 'SMS тЖХ'` renders an inline pill button to the left of the textarea (admin variant тАФ single-line, matches the prototype's compact admin row). Optional `helpers` row beneath the textarea renders rust-light affordance chips with a right-aligned `Spell check тЬУ`. Send button is rust-filled.

### `lib/leads/` тАФ leads stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for lead shapes: `LeadStatus` (`new | contacted | booked | completed | lost`), `LeadUrgency`, `LeadClientTone`, `LEAD_STATUS_LABEL` + `LEAD_URGENCY_LABEL` maps, `LeadTab`, `LeadFilterChip`, inbox-row shapes (`ClientLeadRow`, `AdminLeadRow`), `LeadTimelineEvent` + `LeadTimelineDot`, `LeadRailRow` + `LeadRailCard` + `LeadQuickAction`, the top-level `LeadDetail`, and the conversation shapes (`ConversationBubbleKind`, `ConversationMessage`, `ConversationDay`, `ConversationChannelTab`, `ConversationQuickReply`, `LeadConversation`).
- **`client-leads.tsx`** тАФ hero + tab config only: `clientLeadsHero` (props for `PageHeader`), `clientLeadsTabs` (5 tabs ┬╖ New / Contacted / Booked / Lost / All). `.tsx` because hero copy carries inline `<em>` / `<strong>` JSX. (The `clientLeads` / `voltlineLeadDetail` / `voltlineConversation` data stubs were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)
- **`admin-leads.tsx`** тАФ hero + tab/filter config only: `adminLeadsHero` (props for `LeadsHero`), `adminLeadsClientFilters` (5 chips ┬╖ All clients + 4 clients), `adminLeadsTabs` (6 tabs ┬╖ New / Contacted / Booked / Completed / Lost / Spam). `.tsx` for the same JSX reason. (The `adminLeads` / `freshhomeLeadDetail` / `freshhomeConversation` data stubs were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ **Phase 3 ┬╖ the whole leads cluster (inbox + detail + conversation) is wired to live Supabase data.** `useClientLeadsInbox()` / `useAdminLeadsInbox()` тАФ TanStack Query hooks over a shared `leads` fetch (RLS bounds the rows; the dispatch only picks the row shape). `useLeadDetail(id)` тАФ one lead + its full `lead_events` timeline composed into a `LeadDetail`. `useLeadConversation(id)` тАФ the message-kind `lead_events` (sms/email in/out) grouped into `ConversationDay`s, with status/form events folded in as `system` bubbles. `useUpdateLeadStatus()` тАФ a `useMutation` (backs the `LeadStatusSwitcher`) that updates `leads.status` and logs a `status_changed` `lead_events` row carrying the from/to status labels so the move surfaces on the timeline + conversation. Every by-id `.single()` fetch resolves as `not_found` for a lead outside the caller's tenant. Presentation-only stub fields (`preview`, the admin activity blurb, `unread`, timeline `meta`/`body`/`snippet`, conversation bubbles, `title`/`subtitle`/`metaParts`, rail cards, quick actions) are derived/composed here from `leads` / `lead_events` / `customers` / `lead_reads` per design doc ┬з5 тАФ hence `.tsx` (the mappers build JSX). **B12 тАФ `submission_id` reconciliation.** `useLeadDetail` selects `leads.submission_id` and `buildLeadDetail` appends a "Submission ID" row to the `// LEAD DETAILS` rail card (only when present тАФ a manual / imported lead has no submission to reconcile). The value renders through `CopyableId` (`components/shared/CopyableId.tsx` тАФ monospace, click-to-copy) so an operator can copy the exact id and reconcile the lead back to the public-form submission that created it. The `admin-leads.tsx` / `client-leads.tsx` files supply **only** hero copy + tab/filter config (`*LeadsHero`, `*LeadsTabs`, `adminLeadsClientFilters`); their row + `*LeadDetail` / `*Conversation` data stubs were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.

### `shared/calendar/` + `admin/calendar/` тАФ week calendar (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 2 ┬╖ Session 1)

> **Architectural note тАФ calendar lives outside the role route groups**, same reason as settings / tickets / leads / dashboard. Single shared route `app/calendar/` with `'use client'` layout (reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`) + `'use client'` dispatcher `page.tsx` + `_client-content.tsx` / `_admin-content.tsx` siblings. The grid itself is identical in both roles; the admin variant adds a client-filter row, a colour legend, and a today-summary panel.

- **`CalendarGrid`** (`shared/calendar/CalendarGrid.tsx`) тАФ the week-grid surface. White card with a `70px + repeat(6, 1fr)` header (day labels) and body (time column + 6 day columns). Each day is 12 hour-slots tall, 50px per hour (= 600px). Renders `BookingPill`s positioned by `top`/`height` px from the booking data, plus an optional `CalendarNowLine` on the today column. Takes `week: CalendarWeek` and renders. Tone of the booking pills comes from the data (`tone?: CalendarClientTone`) тАФ client view leaves it unset (defaults to rust); admin view passes `freshhome` / `keyhero` / `voltline` / `neatworks` and gets per-client tinting.
- **`BookingPill`** (`shared/calendar/BookingPill.tsx`) тАФ single positioned booking. Absolute-positioned inside its day column (`top: Npx; height: Npx`). Renders mono time / Inter Tight title / customer line, all paper-on-tone. Renders as a `next/link` when `href` is set; otherwise a click-target `<div>` (will lift to a real callback when the booking detail wires up in Session 2). `tone: CalendarClientTone` controls the background fill via `CLIENT_TONE_BG` from `lib/clients/tones.ts` тАФ `voltline` тЖТ `bg-rust`, the others use solid hex (`#4a7ba6` / `#8a5cb8` / `#2d8a4e`) matching the prototype.
- **`CalendarNowLine`** (`shared/calendar/CalendarNowLine.tsx`) тАФ the pulsing rust horizontal line + leading dot + "NOW ┬╖ 10:35" pill at a given `top` px inside the today column. Pointer-events disabled тАФ purely visual.
- **`CalendarToolbar`** (`shared/calendar/CalendarToolbar.tsx`) тАФ white-card control strip: prev/next nav buttons + period label (`Week of <em>May 11</em> тАФ May 16, 2026`, ReactNode so `<em>` segments render rust) on the left, `CalendarViewTabs` on the right.
- **`CalendarViewTabs`** (`shared/calendar/CalendarViewTabs.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Day/Week/Month pill toggle. Local `useState` active state; optional `onChange` (not wired for the stub тАФ Day/Month views ship in a later session).
- **`CalendarLegend`** (`admin/calendar/CalendarLegend.tsx`) тАФ admin-only horizontal legend row: per-client colour swatches in a paper-2 mono uppercase bar, with an optional right-aligned `meta` ReactNode (e.g. `28 bookings ┬╖ 11 today`). Tone тЖТ swatch colour mapping is the canonical `CLIENT_TONE_BG` from `lib/clients/tones.ts` тАФ same map `BookingPill` and `AutomationFlowMini` consume.
- **`CalendarTodayPanel`** (`admin/calendar/CalendarTodayPanel.tsx`) тАФ admin-only summary card below the grid. Heading + meta line (`<strong>` = rust) + list of `CalendarTodayJob` rows. Each row is a 5-column grid (`100px 36px 1fr auto auto`) with a colour-coded left border (per-client tone), mono time, single-letter client logo on ink, title + customer, status pill (`completed` тЖТ good-soft; `scheduled`/`in_progress` тЖТ rust-soft), and a rust "Open тЖТ" affordance. Renders as a `next/link` when `href` is set. **Cluster 6 ┬╖ 1b** added two optional props: `action` (header-right ReactNode, e.g. an "Open calendar тЖТ" link) and `hideClientLogo` (drops the logo column тЖТ 4-col grid тАФ used by the single-client overview hub, where a per-row client logo is redundant).

### `lib/calendar/` тАФ calendar stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for calendar shapes: `CalendarClientTone` (`voltline | freshhome | keyhero | neatworks | generic`), `CalendarBookingStatus` + `CALENDAR_BOOKING_STATUS_LABEL`, `CalendarBooking` (id / time / title / customer / `top` + `height` px / optional tone + href), `CalendarDay` (id / name / num / `isToday` / `bookings` / optional `nowTopPx` + `nowLabel`), `CalendarWeek` (corner label / period label ReactNode / time slots / days), plus admin extras (`CalendarClientFilter`, `CalendarLegendItem`, `CalendarTodayJob`, `CalendarTodayPanel`) and the top-level `ClientCalendar` + `AdminCalendar`.
- **`client-calendar.tsx`** тАФ `voltlineCalendar`: trimmed to **only** `{ hero }` (the client-calendar hero copy for client Screen 4). `.tsx` because hero copy carries inline `<em>` / `<strong>` JSX. (The full week/booking data stub was removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup тАФ `queries.tsx` is the live source.)
- **`admin-calendar.tsx`** тАФ `adminCalendar`: trimmed to **only** `{ hero }` (the admin-calendar hero copy for admin Screen 13). `.tsx` for the same JSX reason. (The full week/filter/legend/today-panel data stub was removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.)

> **Phase 3 тАФ the calendar + booking detail are wired to live data.** The week grid and booking-detail hooks live in **`lib/bookings/queries.tsx`** (one module spans both `lib/` dirs since both read the `bookings` table). The `voltlineBooking` / `freshhomeBooking` stub files were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup; `voltlineCalendar` / `adminCalendar` were trimmed to **only** their `.hero` copy config (the leads/tickets precedent). The `lib/calendar/types.ts` + `lib/bookings/types.ts` shapes stay live; `queries.tsx` maps to them.

### `shared/bookings/` тАФ booking detail (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 2 ┬╖ Session 2)

> **Architectural note тАФ bookings live outside the role route groups**, same reason as calendar. Single shared route `app/bookings/[id]/` with `'use client'` layout (reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`) + `'use client'` dispatcher `page.tsx` + `_client-content.tsx` / `_admin-content.tsx` siblings. The `[id]` slug is decorative for the stub layer (both roles render their single canonical booking regardless of the actual id тАФ Voltline's "Ceiling fan + RCD replacement" on the client; FreshHome's "Fortnightly clean ┬╖ 3-bed" on the admin). Reached from any `BookingPill` with `href` set on the calendar grid. The nested route `app/bookings/[id]/complete/page.tsx` is the **job completion flow** (client Screen 11) тАФ a `'use client'` page reached from the booking detail's "Mark job complete" / "Mark complete" action (both roles); confirming logs the completion (stub) and routes to `/dashboard`.

- **`ClientBookingHero`** (`bookings/ClientBookingHero.tsx`) тАФ **ink-bg** hero for client Screen 8. `1fr auto` grid: left half carries the rust-light mono `tag` + 26px Inter Tight `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust-light) + meta line (`{ customer, suburb, price, duration }`, `┬╖`-separated; first segment renders ink-bold via the customer prop). Right half is a rust-bg paper-text dot pill rendering `statusLabel` (e.g. `Scheduled ┬╖ 2.5h away`). Inverse chrome to `AdminBookingHero` тАФ kept as a separate component because the structures invert (ink surface vs white card with tone left-border).
- **`AdminBookingHero`** (`bookings/AdminBookingHero.tsx`) тАФ **white-card** hero for admin Screen 18. `tone: CalendarClientTone` drives a 6px-wide left border tint matching the calendar booking pill colours. Renders mono `timeRow` (ReactNode, `<strong>` = ink) + 28px Inter Tight `jobTitle` + customer row (name strong + phone + suburb + rust-soft client pill) + an open `actions` slot (caller supplies the `Button` row тАФ typically Mark complete / Reschedule / Open lead / Cancel booking).
- **`BookingSection`** (`bookings/BookingSection.tsx`) тАФ section block with a mono `// HEADING`. `variant: 'card' | 'inline'`. **Card** (default, admin): standalone white card with its own border + padding (`px-6.5 py-5.5`). **Inline** (client): plain block separated from the next section by a paper-2 bottom rule (`border-b border-paper-2 pb-5.5 mb-5.5`), auto-suppressed on `:last-child`. Use inline when stacking sections inside an outer wrapper card.
- **`BookingJobGrid`** (`bookings/BookingJobGrid.tsx`) тАФ 2-column key/value grid. `cells: BookingJobCell[]` (`{ label, value }`, value is ReactNode so `<em>` renders rust). `surface: 'paper' | 'plain'`. **Paper** (client): each cell sits in its own paper-bg tile (`rounded-lg bg-paper px-3.5 py-3`). **Plain** (admin): cells are inline label/value pairs with no tile surface (`gap-x-6 gap-y-4`).
- **`BookingNotesBox`** (`bookings/BookingNotesBox.tsx`) тАФ paper-bg notes container with a rule-coloured 3px left border. Renders children at 14px ink-soft, with `<strong>` segments switching to bold ink. Identical chrome in both roles.
- **`BookingHistoryRow`** (`bookings/BookingHistoryRow.tsx`) тАФ discriminated by `variant: 'compact' | 'grid'`. **Compact** (client): a single-line paper-bg pill with `<strong>{date}</strong> ┬╖ {body}`; `body` is ReactNode so the price + review meta inline. **Grid** (admin): `100px 1fr 80px auto` grid with mono date / title / price / status (`done` = good-green; optional `statusLabel` override for star ratings).
- **`BookingActionBtn`** (`bookings/BookingActionBtn.tsx`) тАФ client-rail stacked icon+label button. `tone: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'danger'`. **Primary** = rust-filled paper-text (Mark job complete). **Secondary** = paper bg + rule border, hovers to ink-fill (Call / Reschedule / etc.). **Danger** = warn text on paper, hovers to warn-fill (Cancel booking). Renders as `next/link` when `href` is set, else a `<button>`. `mb-2 last:mb-0` auto-spaces within a stack.

### `lib/bookings/` тАФ booking detail stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for booking shapes: `BookingJobCell` (label/value), `BookingRailRow` (label/value/`accent`), `BookingHistoryItemCompact` (date + ReactNode body), `BookingHistoryItemGrid` (date / title / price / `status: 'done'|'scheduled'` / optional `statusLabel`), `ClientBookingActionTone` (`primary | secondary | danger`), `ClientBookingAction` + `ClientBookingActionGroup`, plus the top-level `ClientBookingDetail` and `AdminBookingDetail` (the latter carries `tone: CalendarClientTone` so the hero border tint pairs with the calendar pill colour).
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ **Phase 3 ┬╖ the bookings + calendar read surfaces are wired to live Supabase data** (one module for both `lib/` dirs тАФ both read the `bookings` table). `useClientCalendar()` / `useAdminCalendar()` тАФ TanStack Query hooks over a week-range-bounded `bookings` fetch; RLS bounds the rows, the role hook builds the role's shape (the admin hook also derives the client-filter chips, legend, `legendMeta` and the today panel). `useClientBookingDetail(id)` / `useAdminBookingDetail(id)` тАФ one booking by id + the customer's other bookings (job history + the customer-value rail aggregates), composed into a `ClientBookingDetail` / `AdminBookingDetail` (the by-id `.single()` resolves as `not_found` for a booking outside the caller's tenant). Pixel layout (`top` / `height` / `nowTopPx`) is computed from `starts_at` / `ends_at` per design ┬з5 #11 тАФ never stored; the seed's wall-clock times are read with the UTC accessors so no local-zone shift creeps in. The `job` / `details` cells, the `actions` groups, the `automations` rail and the booking `tag` / `timeRow` are composed here; cancelled bookings are filtered off the grid. `useUpdateBookingStatus()` тАФ a `useMutation` that moves a booking to a terminal lifecycle status (`completed` from the `/bookings/[id]/complete` flow; `cancelled` from the booking-detail "Cancel booking" `ConfirmDialog`) and invalidates the bookings queries (a cancelled booking drops off the grid). **Phase 3b тАФ the booking-write flows are wired:** `useRescheduleBooking()` (`UPDATE starts_at/ends_at`), `useCreateBooking()` (resolve customer тЖТ INSERT `bookings`), and `useCreateRecurringSchedule()` (INSERT `recurring_booking_schedules` + a rolling window of `bookings`) тАФ plus the pure `computeOccurrences()` projector and the `checkRecurringConflicts()` overlap query. `resolveCustomer` (shared internal helper) inserts a `customers` row for a quick-add customer. Stub fields with no backing column (bedrooms / bathrooms / assigned cleaner / products) are dropped тАФ the schema doesn't carry them. `lib/calendar/{client,admin}-calendar.tsx` are trimmed to **only** `.hero` copy config; `lib/bookings/{client,admin}-booking.tsx` were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup.
- **`time.ts`** тАФ wall-clock-in-UTC timestamp helpers shared by the booking-write forms: `composeTimestamp(date, time)` (a `YYYY-MM-DD` + `HH:MM` тЖТ an ISO timestamp read as UTC, matching the calendar's UTC accessors), `isoToDateValue` / `isoToTimeValue` (decompose for native inputs), `formatTimeRange` / `formatDayLabel` / `formatShortDate`, `durationMinutes`, `addMinutes`, `addDays`.
- **`client-booking.tsx`** тАФ `voltlineBooking`: Liam Reilly's "Ceiling fan + RCD replacement" stub from client Screen 8. Customer block + 4 job-grid cells + notes paragraph + 2-row history + 2 action groups (On arrival / Manage, 3 buttons each) + the "// NEXT" tail explainer. `.tsx` because titles / values / notes / next-note all carry inline `<em>` / `<strong>` JSX.
- **`admin-booking.tsx`** тАФ `freshhomeBooking`: Anna Larsen's "Fortnightly clean ┬╖ 3-bed" stub from admin Screen 18. Hero (eyebrow / title / subtitle) + FreshHome tone + time row + 8 job-grid cells + customer notes + 4-row history (last carries 5тШЕ rating) + 3 rail data sets (customer value 4 rows, location address, automations 2 rows). `.tsx` for the same JSX-in-fields reason.
- **`recurring-setup.tsx`** тАФ `recurringSetup`: the static copy for `/recurring/new` тАФ hero copy, the 3 frequency options (`fortnightly` default), 7 day options (`thu` default), and the footnote. The form's time / duration / service / price / customer / preview are all live state on the page now (Phase 3b). Re-exports `RecurringSetup`, `RecurringFrequencyOption`, `RecurringDayOption`, `RecurringPreviewRow`. `.tsx` for the JSX hero copy.
- **`conflict-modal.tsx`** тАФ types only (Phase 3b): `ConflictModalData`, `ConflictCardSide`, `ConflictOption`. The recurring page builds a `ConflictModalData` from the real `checkRecurringConflicts` result; the old `voltlineConflict` stub was removed.
- **`job-completion.tsx`** тАФ `voltlineJobCompletion`: the job-completion-flow stub (client Screen 11) тАФ tag/title/subtitle + тЬУ-hero + job-summary rows + payment options + review-request trigger card. Backs `app/bookings/[id]/complete`. Re-exports `JobCompletion`, `JobCompletionSummaryRow`, `JobCompletionPaymentOption`. `.tsx` for inline `<em>`/`<strong>` JSX.
- **`reschedule-modal.tsx`** тАФ the reschedule modal's static copy: **`freshhomeReschedule`** (admin) and **`voltlineReschedule`** (client) тАФ rust tag + title (em=rust) + subtitle, 6 reason chips, SMS preview tokens, 2 toggles, footer info, save label. The `was`/`now` compare data is computed by the modal from the real booking + the form (Phase 3b тАФ no longer stub strings). Re-exports `RescheduleModalData`, `RescheduleReasonOption`, `ReschedulePreviewToken`, `RescheduleToggleField`.

### `shared/bookings/` тАФ recurring setup + new-booking modal (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 2 ┬╖ Session 3)

> **Architectural note тАФ these two screens have different home shapes.** Client Screen 16 (recurring setup) is a **full page**, not a modal тАФ lives at `app/(client)/recurring/new/page.tsx` since it's client-only (no admin equivalent in the prototype). Admin Screen 21 (new booking) is a **Dialog-based modal** invoked from a "+ New booking" button on the admin calendar тАФ no route of its own. The shared primitive that unifies both surfaces is `ChipSelector` (extracted to `shared/`) тАФ used by the recurring day picker (`mono` variant), the modal service chips (`pill` variant), and any future single-select pill row.

- **`CustomerPicker`** (`bookings/CustomerPicker.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` search-and-pick / quick-add customer control (Phase 3b). Props: `clientId` (UUID тАФ scopes the search), `value: SelectedCustomer | null`, `onChange`. Searches existing customers via `useCustomerSearch`; the "+ Add a new customer" path collects name + phone and hands back a `{ kind: 'new' }` `SelectedCustomer` the write flow inserts. Used by `NewBookingModal` and the `/recurring/new` page.
- **`FrequencyGrid`** (`bookings/FrequencyGrid.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` 4-column option grid for the recurring frequency picker. Each card carries `{ id, name, meta }`; selected state = rust border + rust-soft bg + rust meta line; hover = rust border only. Local `useState` active state тАФ lift to `value`/`onChange` when real persistence wires up.
- **`RecurringPreviewList`** (`bookings/RecurringPreviewList.tsx`) тАФ paper-bg card listing the next-N visits. Mono eyebrow at the top (`<strong>` = rust) + `120px 1fr 90px` rows (mono date / time + visit sub / rust right-aligned price). Dotted bottom rules between rows, auto-suppressed on the last.
- **`RecurringSummaryBar`** (`bookings/RecurringSummaryBar.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg summary footer with the configured frequency on the left (line 1 тАФ `<strong>` = paper-bold) + secondary detail line + 22px rust-light `totalLabel` line, and a rust CTA button on the right. Renders the CTA as `next/link` when `ctaHref` is set, else as a click button.
- **`NewBookingModal`** (`bookings/NewBookingModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` controlled-form booking modal (Phase 3b тАФ wired to `useCreateBooking`). Built on the canonical `Dialog`/`DialogContent` (size `lg`) with a custom header / scrollable body / footer rhythm. **Viewport-safe**: `max-h-[calc(100vh-4rem)]` + `overflow-y-auto`. Props: `open`, `onOpenChange`, `clientId` (UUID the booking is created against). Body: job-title `Input` + `CustomerPicker` + native date/start/end inputs + service `ChipSelector` + price `Input` + notes `Textarea`. Save validates (title, customer, a valid time range) then inserts the booking and routes to `/bookings/[id]`.
- **`AddBookingButton`** (`bookings/AddBookingButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` button that opens `NewBookingModal`. Resolves the target client itself: a client-role user books their own client; an operator books `useWorkspace().activeClientId` тАФ so in agency mode the button is disabled with a "pick a client first" hint. Resolves the client slug тЖТ UUID via `useClientId`. Mounted on both calendars. Replaces the earlier admin-only `admin/calendar/AddBookingButton.tsx`.

### `shared/` тАФ new generic primitive added in Session 3

- **`ChipSelector`** (`shared/ChipSelector.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` generic single-select pill row. `options: ChipOption<T>[]` (`{ id: T, label }`) + `defaultId`/controlled `value`/`onChange`. `variant: 'pill' | 'mono'`. **Pill** (default) тАФ Inter Tight 13px pill chip, ink-active on white card bg, hover-rust border. Used by the new-booking modal's service-chip row. **Mono** тАФ small mono uppercase pill stretched flush via `flex-1`, ink-active on paper bg, hover-rust border. Used by the recurring day-picker row. Different from `shared/FilterChips`, which is a **multi-toggle filter** chip row (rust-active with count badges); `ChipSelector` is a single-select pick (ink-active, no badges). The two patterns share visual chrome but are semantically distinct тАФ both intentionally kept separate.

### `shared/bookings/` тАФ conflict + reschedule modals (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 2 ┬╖ Session 4)

Two Dialog-based modals that complete the booking-edit flows. Both reuse the same body+footer rhythm pattern as `NewBookingModal` (custom `p-0 gap-0` on `DialogContent` + manual header/body/footer sections with paper footer + paper-2 dividers + custom paper-2 close button). Both are entry-pointed by a small `'use client'` trigger component that owns the modal `open` state.

- **`ConflictCard`** (`bookings/ConflictCard.tsx`) тАФ single comparison card inside the conflict modal. `tone: 'attempted' | 'existing'` drives the colour: attempted = rust-soft bg + rust border + rust tag; existing = warn-soft bg + warn border + warn tag. Body is mono tag + 15px ink-bold `time` + 12px ink-soft `detail` line.
- **`ConflictOptionRow`** (`bookings/ConflictOptionRow.tsx`) тАФ numbered option row in the conflict modal's option list. 28px col + 1fr text grid. 22px ink-bg/rust-light digit circle + (`<strong>` title block + 11px sub line). `selected` OR `recommended` flips the row to rust-soft bg + rust border. Stub layer: `onClick` swaps the selected row.
- **`ConflictModal`** (`bookings/ConflictModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Dialog (size `default` = 560px), data-driven (Phase 3b). Header: warn-coloured tag + 22px rust-em title + subtitle. Body: 56px warn-soft тЪа icon + 2-up `ConflictCard` grid + explainer + N `ConflictOptionRow`s with local `useState` selection. Footer: Cancel + a primary action. Props: `data: ConflictModalData`, `onConfirm(optionId)`, `confirmPending?`. The `/recurring/new` page builds the `data` from the real `checkRecurringConflicts` result and `onConfirm` either books the non-clashing visits (`skip`) or cancels.
- **`RescheduleCompareCard`** (`bookings/RescheduleCompareCard.tsx`) тАФ single compare card inside the reschedule modal. `tone: 'was' | 'now'`: was = paper-bg + rule border + `opacity-65` (dim previous state); now = rust-soft bg + rust border + rust tag (highlighted new state). Body is mono tag + 22px ink time + 14px ink-soft day line. Larger time font than `ConflictCard` per prototype.
- **`RescheduleSmsPreview`** (`bookings/RescheduleSmsPreview.tsx`) тАФ SMS preview card: white card surface with a rust-mono eyebrow (leading rust dot) + a paper-bg/left-good-border SMS body. Body is rendered from `tokens: ReschedulePreviewToken[]` тАФ each `type: 'text'` is plain copy, each `type: 'var'` renders the rust-tinted mono-styled variable highlight. Token-array shape lets the data declare which spans are variables without inline JSX.
- **`RescheduleModal`** (`bookings/RescheduleModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Dialog (size `lg`), wired to `useRescheduleBooking` (Phase 3b). Props: `open`, `onOpenChange`, `booking: { id, startsAt, endsAt }`, `data: RescheduleModalData`. Body: 2-up `RescheduleCompareCard` grid (was = the booking, now = live from the form), native date/start/end inputs, a reason `ChipSelector`, `RescheduleSmsPreview` (still a display stub тАФ no messaging backend), toggle row. Save validates the range, `UPDATE`s the booking, closes.
- **`EditJobNotesModal`** (`bookings/EditJobNotesModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` `Dialog` (`size="default"`) editing a booking's job notes тАФ a `Textarea` seeded from `ClientBookingDetail.notesText` + Save / Cancel. Stub: Save logs the next value and closes. The parent mounts it only while open so it opens with fresh state. Backs the client booking-detail "Edit job notes" action.
- **`RescheduleBookingButton`** (`bookings/RescheduleBookingButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` button + `RescheduleModal` pair. Takes `booking: { id, startsAt, endsAt }`, `data: RescheduleModalData`, and a `variant: 'button' | 'action-row'`. **`button`** (default, admin hero) renders a secondary `Button`. **`action-row`** (client booking rail) renders a `BookingActionBtn`-style ghost row with leading icon glyph тАФ drops in for the client's "Reschedule" entry in the MANAGE action group. Both variants share the same modal open state.

### `shared/automations/` + `admin/automations/` тАФ `/automations` list page (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 3 ┬╖ Session A)

> **Architectural note тАФ automations lives outside the role route groups**, same reason as settings / tickets / leads / calendar / dashboard. Single shared route `app/automations/` with `'use client'` layout (reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`) + `'use client'` dispatcher `page.tsx` + `_client-content.tsx` / `_admin-content.tsx` siblings. The two role bodies render **different shapes** (client = flat list of stats cards; admin = filter chips + workspace stats + grouped per-client mini-rows) тАФ intentionally not converged, because they're genuinely different surfaces (personal flows vs cross-client roster). Session B will add `app/automations/[id]/` for the admin-only editor; that page is admin-only by role-gate inside the dispatcher.
- **`AutomationStatTile`** (`shared/automations/AutomationStatTile.tsx`) тАФ single stat tile used inside `AutomationStatsCard`. Mono uppercase label + 22px Inter Tight value (ReactNode тАФ `<em>` renders rust). Paper-bg `rounded-lg` surface; designed to sit in a `grid grid-cols-4 gap-2.5` row.
- **`AutomationStatsCard`** (`shared/automations/AutomationStatsCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` client-Screen-5 card: header (tag + title + description) + `Switch` (ON/OFF label) + a 4-tile stats grid below. Disabled state hides the stats grid entirely (paper-2 bg + 65% opacity). Stats render via `AutomationStatTile`. Different shape than `AutomationCard` тАФ this card is **read-only with stats**, no expanded trigger/step body; the onboarding card is **structural with toggle**, no stats. Both coexist.
- **`AutomationInfoBanner`** (`shared/automations/AutomationInfoBanner.tsx`) тАФ rust-soft tinted info banner with a rust `i` glyph + ReactNode body (`<strong>` = ink-bold). Used at the top of the client `/automations` page to explain "Webnua writes and manages these automations for you." New small primitive; if a second "this surface is managed by your operator" banner lands elsewhere on the client side, reuse this rather than re-inlining the chrome.
- **`AutomationFlowMini`** (`admin/automations/AutomationFlowMini.tsx`) тАФ admin-Screen-10 compact per-client row inside a group. 6-column grid (`36px logo + 1fr name+flow + 3├Ч 90px metric + 56px toggle`). Tinted logo from `AutomationClientTone` (`voltline`/`freshhome`/`keyhero`/`neatworks`/`flowline`/`generic`), coloured via the canonical `CLIENT_TONE_BG` from `lib/clients/tones.ts` тАФ the same map `BookingPill` consumes. When `flow.href` is set AND the flow is enabled, renders as `next/link` (whole row clicks through to the editor at `/automations/[id]`). The `Switch` is wrapped in a `stopPropagation` div so toggling doesn't trigger navigation. Disabled rows render with `paper-2` background + opacity and don't click through.
- **`AutomationGroup`** (`admin/automations/AutomationGroup.tsx`) тАФ admin-Screen-10 group container. White card with a paper-2 header (title + ink/8 count badge + `<strong>`-bolded meta) + a stack of `AutomationFlowMini` rows separated by paper-2 borders. Driven by `AutomationGroup` data (`title`, `countBadge`, `meta`, `flows[]`).

### `lib/automations/` тАФ automations stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for automation shapes. List page (Session A): `AutomationClientTone` (mirrors calendar tones + adds `flowline`), `AutomationStat`, `AutomationStatsCard` (client card), `AutomationFlowMini` (admin mini-row), `AutomationGroup` (admin group container), `AutomationsHero`, `AutomationsWorkspaceStat`, `ClientAutomations`, `AdminAutomations`. Editor (Session B): `AutomationEditorChannel`, `AutomationEditorTrigger`, `AutomationEditorStep` (id / number / channel / delay / name / optional subject / body ReactNode with `[data-slot=var]` highlights / footerMeta / variables[] / `isEditing`), `AutomationVariable`, `AutomationPerformanceMetric` (with `tone: 'default' | 'accent' | 'good'`), `AutomationTestSendData`, and the top-level `AutomationEditor`.
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ **Phase 3 ┬╖ the automations cluster is wired to live Supabase data.** `useClientAutomations()` / `useAdminAutomations()` тАФ TanStack Query hooks over a shared `automations` + `automation_steps` fetch (RLS-bounded); the client hook builds the toggle-card list, the admin hook the type-grouped cross-client roster. `useAutomationEditor(id)` тАФ one automation + its steps composed into an `AutomationEditor` (the by-id `.single()` resolves as `not_found` outside the tenant). `useToggleAutomation()` тАФ a real `useMutation` enabling/disabling a flow; it persists and invalidates the automations queries. The **automation library is seeded by migrations `0021_seed_automations` + `0022_seed_automation_types`** тАФ 21 automations (one per type per client) across the four clients, with their step templates, so every automation the UI shows is a real editable row. **Six trigger types** in the library тАФ `lead_created` / `lead_stale_24h` / `booking_upcoming` / `job_completed` / `booking_no_show` / `customer_dormant` (Instant confirm / 24-hour follow-up / Appointment reminder / Review request loop / No-show recovery / Win-back re-engagement). Adding a 7th type means a seed migration + amending the `TYPE_ORDER` / `TYPE_LABEL` / `TYPE_TAG` / `TRIGGER_NAME` / `TYPE_DESCRIPTION` maps in `queries.tsx`. Step `body` is a plain-text template with `{placeholder}` tokens (design ┬з5 #6); `highlightVars` wraps the tokens in the editor's `data-slot="var"` highlight span at render. **Metrics gap (same as campaigns):** automation *performance* counts (sent / delivered / replied) have no schema home тАФ no send-log table тАФ so the stat tiles + the editor performance rail render honest placeholders; the *definitions* (name, trigger, steps, copy, enabled) are fully live and editable. The `client-automations.tsx` / `admin-automations.tsx` / `admin-editor.tsx` stub files were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup; `types.ts` shapes stay live.
- **Editable status (Phase 3):** the enable/disable toggle is a real persisted mutation across the client cards, the admin roster rows, and the editor's footer. The editor's per-step **copy save** is also wired тАФ `AutomationEditorStep` is a controlled component (name / email subject / message body are editable fields, body is a textarea over the raw `{placeholder}` template); the editor page's `EditorBody` owns the step state and the footer Save calls `useUpdateAutomationSteps` to persist. **Still not wired:** step *timing* (the delay pill is display-only) and step add/remove/reorder тАФ those need a delay picker + a step insert/delete/position mutation (a later increment).

---

### `admin/automations/` тАФ automation editor + test-send (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 3 ┬╖ Session B)

> **Architectural note тАФ the editor lives at `/automations/[id]`** inside the shared `/automations` route tree (Next won't allow it inside `(admin)` simultaneously). The page is a `'use client'` dispatcher that role-gates internally: admin renders the editor; client falls back through `router.replace('/automations')` since there's no client editor. The `[id]` slug is decorative for the stub layer тАФ the single canonical FreshHome 24h follow-up renders regardless of id. Admin Screen 10's `AutomationFlowMini` rows already carry `href` values pointing here from Session A.

- **`AutomationEditorLayout`** (`automations/AutomationEditorLayout.tsx`) тАФ `1fr 340px` two-column wizard shell (canvas + sticky right rail). Canvas is wrapped in a white card surface (`rounded-xl border border-rule bg-card px-7 py-6.5`); the rail is a plain `sticky top-[100px]` flex-col. **3rd `1fr + fixed-rail` detail layout** alongside `TicketDetailLayout` + the inline lead-detail shape тАФ see parked decisions for layout-shell consolidation.
- **`AutomationTriggerBox`** (`automations/AutomationTriggerBox.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg trigger row with the rust тЪб icon + `// TRIGGER` mono label + the trigger name + a rust-light "Change trigger тЖТ" affordance. `1fr` middle column holds the trigger summary.
- **`AutomationStepConnector`** (`automations/AutomationStepConnector.tsx`) тАФ small 2px rule-coloured vertical line, centred between the trigger and each step. Pure decorative, `aria-hidden`.
- **`AutomationEditorStep`** (`automations/AutomationEditorStep.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` editable step. Header is a 6-col grid: numbered ink circle (rust-light digit) + channel pill (`sms` = good, `email` = info) + delay pill (mono with тЧ╖ glyph) + editable name input + тЖХ reorder + ├Ч delete (icon buttons via the inner `StepIconBtn`). Body: optional subject input (email only) + the message body in a tinted card with `[data-slot=var]` highlighting. `isEditing: true` flips the header bg to rust-soft, the body border to rust + rust-glow shadow, and tints the footerMeta rust. Footer: the meta string + the variable chip row (always leads with a "+ Insert variable" rust-soft chip). Inputs are local state тАФ wire to backend when real save lands.
- **`AutomationAddStep`** (`automations/AutomationAddStep.tsx`) тАФ dashed-border `+ Add another step (SMS / Email / Wait)` affordance. Hover-flips to rust border + rust-soft fill.
- **`AutomationVariableList`** (`automations/AutomationVariableList.tsx`) тАФ right-rail card listing the 7 available variables. Each row: mono rust `{code}` + ink-quiet description + rust "+" affordance. Hover-tinted rust-soft.
- **`AutomationTestSendCard`** (`automations/AutomationTestSendCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` right-rail card that owns the modal `open` state. Heading + description + full-width ink button (hover-flips to rust). Mounts `AutomationTestSendModal` underneath.
- **`AutomationPerformanceCard`** (`automations/AutomationPerformanceCard.tsx`) тАФ right-rail card with N rows of `label : value`. Per-row value tint: `accent` = rust, `good` = good-green, `default` = ink-bold. Dotted bottom rules between rows.

### `shared/automations/` тАФ test-send modal (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 3 ┬╖ Session B)

- **`AutomationTestSendModal`** (`automations/AutomationTestSendModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Dialog (size `default` = 560px) for admin Screen 22. Same viewport-safe header / scrollable body / footer rhythm as `NewBookingModal` (`p-0 gap-0` on `DialogContent`, custom paper-2 close button, paper footer with paper-2 top border). Body: "Send to" readonly Input + SMS preview card (blue-tinted phone-frame surface with the white SMS bubble + the variables-filled mono line below) + paper test-options row (info text + Switch-to-email secondary button). Footer: Twilio Twilio-credit info text (`<strong>` = ink) + Cancel / Send buttons (both close the modal тАФ wire to real send when backend lands).

### `shared/` тАФ editor-mode footer actions (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 3 ┬╖ Session B)

- **`EditorFooterActions`** (`EditorFooterActions.tsx`) тАФ sibling to `BuilderFooterActions` (the wizard footer). Built separately because the interaction model differs: editor footers carry an "auto-saved" mono progress indicator + a 3-button action set (Back / Disable / Save) rather than the wizard's 2-button Back/Continue. No top border by default тАФ the canvas above already carries its own card border; centred `mt-7` gap separates the rows. Used by the automation editor today; future editors (e.g. page builder) should reuse it. See parked decisions for the "revisit when a third footer-actions variant appears" rule.

### `shared/search/` тАФ global search (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ Session 2)

> **Architectural note тАФ `/search` is a shared route.** `app/search/` has its own `layout.tsx` ('use client', `useRole()`, picks sidebar, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`). `page.tsx` is a `'use client'` dispatcher that picks the role-scoped stub and renders the shared `SearchResultsView` тАФ no `_admin-content` / `_client-content` siblings, because the two role bodies are structurally identical (same view, different data). Operators search across every client (admin Screen 35); a client searches their own account. `page.tsx` wraps the body in `<Suspense>` because it reads `?q=` via `useSearchParams`.

- **`GlobalSearchInput`** (`search/GlobalSearchInput.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` rounded-pill search field (тМХ icon + input + decorative `тМШK` hint). Enter routes to `/search?q=тАж`. As of Session 7 the `Topbar` auto-renders it for every operator-role page (the rollout is complete тАФ see the `Topbar` entry); pages pass it explicitly only to seed a value (`/search` seeds the current query), or set `hideSearch` to suppress it (admin leads + tickets inboxes, which carry their own in-body search).
- **`SearchResultRow`** (`search/SearchResultRow.tsx`) тАФ single result row, a `next/link`: kind-tinted 40px avatar tile (initials for people, glyph otherwise) + title + meta (both run through `highlightMatch`) + `тЖТ`. `KIND_TILE` maps the six `SearchResultKind`s to tone classes.
- **`SearchResultGroup`** (`search/SearchResultGroup.tsx`) тАФ one per-kind group: mono label + ink count chip header, then a bordered card of `SearchResultRow`s.
- **`SearchResultsView`** (`search/SearchResultsView.tsx`) тАФ the shared `/search` body: an ink result-count summary strip + the per-kind groups. Role-agnostic тАФ operator and client pass their own `SearchResults`.

### `lib/search/` тАФ global search data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `SearchResultKind` (`lead | booking | review | conversation | customer | client`), `SearchResult` (`{ id, kind, avatar, title, meta, href }` тАФ each result a typed entity with a real detail `href`), `SearchResultGroup`, `SearchResults`.
- **`highlight.tsx`** тАФ `highlightMatch(text, query)` тЖТ ReactNode, wrapping case-insensitive query matches in a rust `<mark>`.

### `shared/` тАФ rail-card primitives (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6)

> The canonical white-card side-rail pattern. Extracted in Cluster 6 (mechanical rename) from the previously-separate `TicketSideCard` / `TicketPropertyRow` (tickets + bookings) and `LeadRailCard` / `LeadRailRowItem` (leads) тАФ all four deleted, no re-export shims. Used by the tickets, leads, and bookings detail rails, and the single-client overview hub.

- **`RailCard`** (`RailCard.tsx`) тАФ right-rail card wrapper. Props: `heading` (mono uppercase string, e.g. `// Status`), `tone: 'light' | 'dark'` (default light = white card with `border-ink/8`; dark = ink-bg paper-text тАФ used by `TicketStatusCard`), optional `rows: RailRow[]` shorthand (each row renders as a mono-labelled `RailPropertyRow`), `children` (for bespoke bodies тАФ status pickers, action lists). `rounded-[14px] px-5 py-[18px]`. `RailRow` (`{ label, value, accent?, tone? }`) is structurally compatible with `lib/leads/types.ts` `LeadRailRow` тАФ feature types stay put (same pattern as `FilterChips`).
- **`RailPropertyRow`** (`RailPropertyRow.tsx`) тАФ single label/value row inside a `RailCard`.
