Props: `label` (string) + `value` (ReactNode) + `editable` (boolean тАФ appends a mono `тЬО` glyph) + `tone: 'good' | 'quiet' | 'default'` (value colour) + `accent` (boolean тАФ rust value, overrides `tone`) + `labelStyle: 'plain' | 'mono'` (default `plain` тАФ quiet sentence-case label for tickets/bookings; `mono` тАФ mono uppercase label, used by the leads rail rows). `space-between` flex, dotted bottom rule between rows, suppressed on the last. Tighter than `SettingsFieldRow` because the 320px side panel can't carry settings' 220px label column.

### `shared/` тАФ activity feed (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ Session 1a)

> The canonical flat activity-log card. Extracted at the third-surface trigger (the single-client overview hub) from the previously-sibling `CampaignActivityCard`. **`LeadTimeline` is deliberately NOT consolidated here** тАФ a timeline (dot-spine, scheduled-future pending events, tinted snippet quotes, gapped rows) is a different structural concern from a flat feed; folding it in would re-create the optional-slot grab-bag. The two coexist by design.

- **`ActivityRow`** (`ActivityRow.tsx`) тАФ one feed row. `row: ActivityRowData` does the work; `ActivityRowData` is **event-shaped** per vision ┬з7 тАФ `{ id, icon, tone, actor?, body, detail?, time, href? }`, a typed attributable event, not rendered prose. `tone: ActivityTone` is a colour-keyed vocabulary (`info | amber | good | rust`) тАФ consumers map their own domain categories onto these slots. `grid-cols-[32px_1fr_auto]`: tone-tinted 32px icon tile + body (rust-bold `actor` + `body` + quiet `detail` block) + right-aligned mono `time`. Dotted bottom rule between rows. Renders as a `next/link` when `href` is set.
- **`ActivityFeed`** (`ActivityFeed.tsx`) тАФ white-card wrapper: `title` (ReactNode, `<em>` = rust) + optional `sub` (`<strong>` = ink-bold) + optional `action` (header-right ReactNode, e.g. an "All тЖТ" link тАФ added Cluster 6 ┬╖ 1b) + a stack of `ActivityRow`s from `items: ActivityRowData[]`. `rounded-xl border border-rule bg-card px-6 py-5.5`. Used by client `/campaigns` (via the `CampaignActivityCard` adapter) and the single-client overview hub.

### `shared/reviews/` + `client/reviews/` тАФ `/reviews` page (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 4 ┬╖ Session A)

> **Architectural note тАФ reviews lives outside the role route groups**, same reason as settings / tickets / leads / calendar / automations / dashboard. Single shared route `app/reviews/` with `'use client'` layout (reads `useRole()`, picks `ClientSidebar` vs `AdminSidebar`, mounts `DevRoleSwitcher`) + `'use client'` dispatcher `page.tsx` + `_client-content.tsx` / `_admin-content.tsx` siblings. Client renders a single-business reviews surface (client Screen 6) + the negative-review intercept modal (prototype admin Screen 24 тАФ relocated to client side, see prototype-disagreement note below); admin renders a cross-client per-client-card grid (admin Screen 12). The two role bodies share `ReviewSummaryHeader` (sized down inside the per-client card) and `ReviewItem` (with `variant: 'full' | 'compact'`) тАФ single canonical components, no role-specific duplicates.
>
> **Prototype-disagreement note тАФ negative-review alert is client-side, not admin.** The platform prototype mounts the 2тШЕ alert modal on admin Screen 24 ("Call Jamie immediately to apologise" framed as the operator's action). In practice the business owner is the one with the customer relationship and the one who'd actually call back; the operator's role here is to be informed and to adjust ad copy if a pattern emerges. The modal lives in `shared/reviews/` (reusable shape) but its only mount today is on client `/reviews` via `client/reviews/NegativeReviewAlertButton`. If a future operator-facing "FreshHome just got a 2тШЕ" surfacing lands in Cluster 6, build that as a sibling тАФ don't shoehorn it into this modal.

- **`ReviewSummaryHeader`** (`reviews/ReviewSummaryHeader.tsx`) тАФ big rating block (Inter Tight rating value with `<em>` rust on the тШЕ glyph + stars-row + mono meta line). `size: 'lg' | 'sm'` controls scale (56px headline on client Screen 6; 26px headline inside admin per-client cards). `align: 'left' | 'right'` so the same component can sit left-aligned in the client summary and right-aligned in the admin per-client card header. Single canonical тАФ don't sibling per-surface.
- **`ReviewDistributionBars`** (`reviews/ReviewDistributionBars.tsx`) тАФ 5тШЕтЖТ1тШЕ horizontal bar chart driven by `ReviewDistributionRow[]` (stars / count / pct). Rust-fill on paper-2 track, mono labels. Used by client `/reviews` today; lives in `shared/` so admin can reuse if a future single-client admin drill-down appears.
- **`ReviewCallout`** (`reviews/ReviewCallout.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg "Asked, not begged." motivational card on the right of the client summary row. ReactNode `headline` (`<em>` = rust-light on ink) + sub line + a rust-light mono link.
- **`ReviewItem`** (`reviews/ReviewItem.tsx`) тАФ single canonical Google review entry, discriminated by `variant`. **`full`** (client Screen 6) = `44px avatar + 1fr body + 100px stars + 80px age` grid with name + job + quote + filled-star row + mono age. **`compact`** (admin per-client cards) = `1fr text + auto right-aligned stars-and-age` with `<strong>Name</strong> ┬╖ "quote"` and right-aligned `тШЕтШЕтШЕ ┬╖ age`. Same data shape, two layouts.
- **`ReviewMiniStat`** (`reviews/ReviewMiniStat.tsx`) тАФ small stat tile inside admin per-client cards (NEW ┬╖ 7D / 5-STAR / REQUEST тЖТ REVIEW). 20px Inter Tight value + mono uppercase label. Smaller than `StatCard`, intentionally тАФ sits inside a 3-up grid inside an already-bordered card.
- **`ReviewClientCard`** (`reviews/ReviewClientCard.tsx`) тАФ admin per-client card. White card composing logo + name+meta header row + right-aligned `ReviewSummaryHeader` (size `sm` + align `right`) + 3-up `ReviewMiniStat` grid + `// RECENT` block of `ReviewItem` (compact). Discriminated by `card.kind` тАФ `connected` renders the full content; `empty` (Voltline pre-launch) renders an opacity-dimmed card with description + "Connect Google Business" CTA.
- **`NegativeReviewActionRow`** (`shared/reviews/NegativeReviewActionRow.tsx`) тАФ numbered suggested-action row inside the negative-review modal. 3-column grid: 24px ink/rust-light digit circle + 1fr title+sub body + auto right-aligned "Recommended" pill. `recommended: true` flips the row to rust-soft bg + rust border + shows the pill. Structurally close to `shared/bookings/ConflictOptionRow` but adds the visible pill column тАФ parked-decision: extract a generic numbered-option-row shared primitive on the third instance.
- **`NegativeReviewModal`** (`shared/reviews/NegativeReviewModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Dialog (size `default` = 560px). Same viewport-safe header / scrollable body / footer rhythm as `NewBookingModal` (`p-0 gap-0` on `DialogContent`, custom paper-2 close button, paper footer with paper-2 top border). Header: warn-tinted tag (with leading warn dot) + 24px rust-em title + subtitle. Body: centered 56px warn-soft `!` icon + warn-tinted quote block (stars + italic quote + mono meta with `<strong>` ink emphasis) + numbered `NegativeReviewActionRow` list. Footer: muted footer info (`<strong>` = ink) + Dismiss / Call buttons (both close the modal тАФ wire to real call/dismiss when backend lands). Lives in `shared/` (reusable shape); currently only mounted on client `/reviews`.
- **`NegativeReviewAlertButton`** (`client/reviews/NegativeReviewAlertButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` trigger button + modal-open state owner. Stub-only entry point: the real build fires the modal from a low-rating webhook the moment Google surfaces a sub-4тШЕ review, but the stub layer mounts a "тЪа Show 2тШЕ alert" secondary `Button` next to the client `/reviews` `PageHeader`. Delete the button (and the data import) when the webhook trigger lands; keep `NegativeReviewModal` either way.

### `lib/reviews/` тАФ reviews stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for review shapes: `ReviewItem` (data shape used by both row variants), `ReviewDistributionRow`, `ReviewSummaryData`, `ReviewMiniStat`, `ReviewClientCardData` (discriminated `kind: 'connected' | 'empty'`), `ReviewCalloutData`, `ClientReviewsPage`, `AdminReviewsPage`, and the negative-review modal shapes (`NegativeReviewActionData`, `NegativeReviewQuoteData`, `NegativeReviewModalData`).
- **`client-negative-modal.tsx`** тАФ `voltlineNegativeReview`: Voltline 2тШЕ Jamie K. stub (reframed from the prototype's KeyHero/admin-side copy тАФ see prototype-disagreement note above). Quote + 4 suggested actions (action 1 recommended; action 4 = "Flag to Craig at Webnua for ad messaging review") + footer "first negative review in your first 14 days" reassurance. **Still a stub** тАФ the negative-review alert modal is a stub interaction (`NegativeReviewAlertButton` demo trigger), not wired to live data.
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ **Phase 3 ┬╖ the `/reviews` read surfaces are wired to live Supabase data.** `useClientReviews()` тАФ the signed-in client's `ClientReviewsPage` (reads `clients` + `reviews`, both RLS-bounded; a client with zero reviews still resolves via the single `clients` row). `useAdminReviews()` тАФ the operator `AdminReviewsPage`: one `ReviewClientCardData` per accessible client (`connected` when the client has reviews, `empty` otherwise) + the 4-up workspace stat row. The rating headline, the 5тШЕтЖТ1тШЕ distribution, the per-client mini-stats, the workspace stats and the relative age labels are all computed here from `reviews.stars` / `reviews.reviewed_at` per design ┬з5. Hero copy is composed in the query (the client eyebrow carries the client name). The `client-reviews.tsx` / `admin-reviews.tsx` stub files were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup; the `types.ts` shapes stay live.

### `shared/campaigns/` + `admin/campaigns/` тАФ `/campaigns` page (Phase 5 ┬╖ Cluster 4 ┬╖ Session B)

> **Architectural note тАФ campaigns lives outside the role route groups**, same reason as reviews / settings / tickets / etc. Single shared route `app/campaigns/` with `'use client'` layout + `'use client'` dispatcher + `_client-content.tsx` / `_admin-content.tsx` siblings. The two role bodies render **different shapes** тАФ client is a single-campaign deep dive (managed band + active hero card + 4-week trend chart + activity log + change CTA); admin is a flat cross-client roster (filter chips + 4 workspace stats + N campaign rows + Meta Ads info bar). Intentionally not converged тАФ they're genuinely different surfaces (single-campaign view vs multi-campaign roster), and forcing a shared shell would only produce a grab-bag of optional slots.

- **`CampaignManagedBand`** (`campaigns/CampaignManagedBand.tsx`) тАФ ink-bg reassurance band at the top of client `/campaigns`. 3-column grid: 56px rust-tinted icon tile + tag/title/sub body (`<em>` = rust-light, `<strong>` = paper-bold) + ghost "Text Craig" CTA on the right. Standalone тАФ distinct from `AutomationInfoBanner` (rust-soft chip) and from `BillingPlanCard` (plan-meta + headline + action). If a second ink-bg "managed by your operator" band lands elsewhere on the client side, revisit extraction.
- **`CampaignMetricTile`** (`campaigns/CampaignMetricTile.tsx`) тАФ single metric tile inside the active-campaign hero. 10px mono uppercase label + 32px Inter Tight value (`<em>` = rust) + sub trend line with `trendTone: 'good' | 'warn' | 'quiet'`. Sized larger than `StatCard` (32px vs 30px) AND lives inside a parent card with no border of its own тАФ the 1px paper-2 gap between tiles comes from the parent's grid background trick.
- **`CampaignPlainEnglish`** (`campaigns/CampaignPlainEnglish.tsx`) тАФ rust-soft tinted "In plain English" explainer card. 2-column grid: 32px rust circle with `i` glyph + ReactNode body (`<em>` = rust bold, `<strong>` = ink-bold). Sits below the metric grid inside the active-campaign hero.
- **`CampaignHeroCard`** (`campaigns/CampaignHeroCard.tsx`) тАФ active-campaign hero on client `/campaigns`. White card composing header row (pulsing-good-dot eyebrow + 22px name with `<em>` rust + meta line + good-soft status pill) + 4-tile `CampaignMetricTile` grid with 1px paper-2 separators + a `CampaignPlainEnglish` block in the footer. Single-campaign surface тАФ admin has no equivalent.
- **`CampaignTrendChart`** (`campaigns/CampaignTrendChart.tsx`) тАФ CSS-only 4-week grouped-bar chart (leads vs spend). Hand-rolled with a 60px y-axis column + a 1fr bars area; each week column renders two stacked-end bars (leads filled rust / spend paper-2 outlined) scaled against `leadsMax` / `spendMax`. Bar labels float above their bars; the "current" week gets a rust glow shadow + rust week label. No chart library тАФ the prototype shape is small enough that hand-rolling is cleaner than pulling in a dep; revisit if a second chart shape lands elsewhere.
- **`CampaignActivityCard`** (`campaigns/CampaignActivityCard.tsx`) тАФ "What Webnua's done lately" activity log on client `/campaigns`. **As of Cluster 6 ┬╖ Session 1a this is a thin domain adapter** over the shared `ActivityFeed` (see the `shared/` activity-feed entry above): it maps the campaign activity-category vocabulary (`creative`/`audience`/`budget`/`tune`) onto `ActivityFeed`'s colour-keyed tone slots and shapes `CampaignActivityItem` into `ActivityRowData`. Keeps its `{ data, className }` API so `/campaigns` is unchanged; `CampaignActivityItem` stays uncoupled from the row shape.
- **`CampaignChangeCard`** (`campaigns/CampaignChangeCard.tsx`) тАФ bottom "Want to change something?" CTA card on client `/campaigns`. White card + body text + N right-aligned `Button`s. Buttons render through the canonical `Button` primitive (`primary: true` тЖТ rust default; otherwise secondary).
- **`CampaignSparkline`** (`campaigns/CampaignSparkline.tsx`) тАФ small inline SVG sparkline used on admin `/campaigns` rows. Rust stroke with a soft rust fill below the line; dashed flat-line when `points` is omitted (pre-launch / pending rows). Lives in `shared/` because it's generic enough to be reusable.
- **`CampaignStatusPill`** (`admin/campaigns/CampaignStatusPill.tsx`) тАФ mono uppercase pill used on admin `/campaigns` rows. `active` = good-green with pulsing dot; `paused` / `pending` = ink-quiet with static dot. `label` overrides the status-keyed default. Distinct vocabulary from the existing tickets/leads status-pill families тАФ kept as its own component; revisit if a third campaign-status surface appears.
- **`CampaignClientRow`** (`admin/campaigns/CampaignClientRow.tsx`) тАФ admin-only cross-client roster row. 7-column grid: 36px ink-bg logo with rust-light glyph + 1.4fr name+meta + 110px `CampaignStatusPill` + three 100/110px metric cells (each with a ReactNode `value` for rust accent + small mono `sub`) + 100px `CampaignSparkline`. `row.dimmed` opacity-fades the whole row (used for Voltline pre-launch).

### `lib/campaigns/` тАФ campaigns stub data + types

- **`types.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for campaign shapes. Client side: `CampaignActivityIconTone` (`creative | audience | budget | tune`), `CampaignMetric`, `CampaignManagedBandData`, `CampaignHeroData`, `CampaignTrendWeek` + `CampaignTrendChartData`, `CampaignActivityItem` + `CampaignActivityData`, `CampaignChangeCardData`, top-level `ClientCampaignsPage`. Admin side: `AdminCampaignStatus` (`active | paused | pending`), `AdminCampaignRow`, top-level `AdminCampaignsPage` (hero + filters + stats + rows + footer info bar).
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ **Phase 3 ┬╖ partial wire тАФ the `/campaigns` pages are wired to live data for what the schema honestly carries.** `useClientCampaigns()` builds the client deep-dive (the running campaign, else most recent); `useAdminCampaigns()` builds the cross-client roster. **Schema gap (read the module header):** `campaigns` stores only the campaign *record* (name / status / budget / dates) and `campaign_activity_events` the operator activity log тАФ there are **no performance-metric columns and no `campaign_metrics` table**. Leads / spend / CPL / ROAS / the 4-week trend / the row sparklines are Meta Ads integration data, not yet modelled (design ┬з5 #7). So the record + the activity log are wired live (the activity log composes from `campaign_activity_events` joined to actor `users`); every metric renders an honest "Awaiting Meta Ads" placeholder, the client `trend` is omitted (`ClientCampaignsPage.trend` is now optional тАФ the content file renders a placeholder card), and the admin row sparklines fall back to the dashed flatline. When the Meta Ads integration lands, replace the placeholders; the record + activity wiring stays. The `client-campaigns.tsx` / `admin-campaigns.tsx` stub files were removed in the Phase 3 dead-stub cleanup; `types.ts` shapes stay live.

### `lib/auth/` тАФ user + capability layer (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 1a)

The spine of the cluster 5 builder access model. See `reference/builder-design.md` ┬з1 for full rationale. One editor renders for everyone; capabilities decide which controls are live. Role still drives sidebar shape (which nav set / workspace block); capabilities are the finer-grained layer inside the editor.

- **`capabilities.ts`** тАФ single source of truth for the cap layer. 14 capabilities (`viewBuilder`, `editCopy`, `editMedia`, `editSEO`, `editLayout`, `editSections`, `editForms`, `editTheme`, `editPages`, `useAI`, `publish`, `approve`, `rollback`, `manageDomain`) тАФ `editForms` (lead-capture form editing) was added with the form builder; see `reference/form-builder-design.md`. Exports `ALL_CAPABILITIES`, `ADMIN_DEFAULTS` (= all caps), `CLIENT_DEFAULTS` (= just `viewBuilder`), `CAPABILITY_LABEL` (`Record<Capability, string>` тАФ the affirmative display name per cap, e.g. `editCopy тЖТ 'Edit page copy'`; the SoT for labelling a capability in any human-facing UI тАФ added Cluster 6 ┬╖ team invite), plus `Role`, `CapabilityGrant` (`{ userId, websiteId | '*', capabilities }` тАФ shape stays preset-compatible per design doc ┬з1.4 forward-compat note), and `User` (`{ id, displayName, email, role, clientId: string | null, capabilities: Set<Capability> }` тАФ `clientId` is the user's home client business, null for operators; `capabilities` is **derived** from role defaults + grants every render). Force-publish is **not** a separate cap тАФ break-glass discipline is UI + audit log layered on top of `publish`, gated at the call site by `role === 'admin'`.
- **`explainers.ts`** тАФ `CAP_EXPLAINER: Record<Capability, { short, requestLabel }>` тАФ the per-cap human strings surfaced by `<CapabilityGate>` (tooltip in `disable` mode, affordance label in `request` mode). Empty `requestLabel` opts a cap out of `request` mode entirely (currently `viewBuilder` + `approve`). Hardcoded "your operator" / "your account" тАФ see the parked decision in Open decisions about an `{operatorLabel}` token for multi-operator deploys.
- **`user-stub.tsx`** тАФ **real Supabase Auth** (the filename is misleading and kept only so the ~50 import sites stay untouched тАФ this is NOT a stub). `<UserProvider>` resolves the signed-in user from a real Supabase session: `supabase.auth.getSession()` + `onAuthStateChange` тЖТ the `public.users` profile row тЖТ `capability_grants` rows тЖТ a `User` whose `capabilities` set is derived (`resolveCapabilities(role, grants)` тАФ role defaults тИк granted caps). Exports `<UserProvider>`, `useUser()` тЖТ `User | null`, `useUserContext()` (`{ user, effectiveCapabilities, hydrated, clearUser, refreshUser }`), `useCapabilities()` тЖТ `Set<Capability>`, `useCan(cap)` / `useCanAny` / `useCanAll`, a legacy `useRole()` shim (`{ role, hydrated, setRole (no-op), clearRole }` тАФ `setRole` is dead, role comes from the signed-in profile), `<CapabilityOverrideProvider>` (locks the effective cap set to a fixed list for the wizard-frame editor), and `resolveCapabilities`. **No user-switching, no view-as, no localStorage, no stub users** тАФ all removed when real auth landed (`7ceda3c` Phase 2, `341d19f` Phase 5). `clientId` resolves to the client's `slug`. The capability layer (`capabilities.ts` / `explainers.ts` / `resolver.ts`) is product code тАФ it did not move; only how the user is *resolved* changed. **Sign-in:** `app/(auth)/login/page.tsx` is a real `supabase.auth.signInWithPassword` screen.
- **`audit-stub.ts`** тАФ Phase 4: **type-only display module.** Just the `ForcePublishEntry` shape now. The audit log itself is the `force_publish_audit_log` table тАФ entries are written by `lib/website/mutations.ts` (`publishDraft` with `force`) and read by `useForcePublishLog` (`lib/website/queries.tsx`). `/settings/access` consumes the live read via that hook. The previous localStorage overlay (`webnua.dev.audit-log`) + `appendForcePublishEntry` / `getEffectiveAuditLog` / `subscribeAudit` exports are gone.
- **`roster-store.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`** (PR #43). The users-with-grants list that backs the cap grid + the access roster on `/settings/access`. Combines `public.users` rows with their `capability_grants` so the grid can render every operator-known user with the websites they hold caps on. Snapshot-cached for `useSyncExternalStore` stability. The previous localStorage stub vanished with `DevRoleSwitcher`.

### `lib/data/` тАФ auth-driven store hydration (Phase 5 ┬╖ PR #43)

- **`DataHydrationProvider.tsx`** тАФ mounted in `src/app/layout.tsx` inside `<UserProvider>`. The single point that pulls every Supabase-backed in-memory cache from the DB. On mount and on every `supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange`, calls `hydrateClients()` first (because the slugтЖФUUID map is the spine every other store depends on), then fires the rest in parallel: agency-policy, policy-overrides, plan-catalog, plan-assignments, client-invites, seat-limit history, team-invites, roster. Each store's `hydrate*()` function reads its table via the anon Supabase client (so RLS bounds the rows). A logged-out page load produces a wall of `401 permission denied` console warnings тАФ the `anon` role correctly refuses; the stores hydrate properly on sign-in. **Two-second knock-on:** every store is a `useSyncExternalStore` snapshot-cached store, so hydration must bump the version counter exactly once at the end of each `hydrate*()` тАФ never mid-loop тАФ or the snapshot stability rule breaks.

### `lib/clients/` (cont'd) тАФ client roster store

- **`clients-store.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider` first** (slugтЖФUUID is the spine every other store depends on тАФ PR #43). Replaces the previous static `lib/nav/admin-clients.ts` source for the live roster: hydrates from `public.clients`, exposes `getClientUuidBySlug(slug)` / `getClientSlugByUuid(uuid)` / `getAllClients()` / `subscribeClients()`. `lib/clients/queries.tsx` `useClientId(slug)` resolves through this; `lib/clients/seat-limit-stub.ts` uses it too. `create-client.ts` calls `hydrateClients()` after a successful insert so the new client appears in the sidebar picker immediately.

### `lib/team/` (cont'd) тАФ team-invite store (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 + PR #43)

- **`team-invite-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider` (PR #43 тАФ net-new in that PR; there was no localStorage predecessor).** Operator-side team-invite list backed by `team_invites`. `addTeamInvite` writes through; `getAllTeamInvites` (snapshot-cached), `subscribeTeamInvites`. Sibling of `lib/invites/client-invite-stub.ts` тАФ the same Supabase-cache + version-counter + `useSyncExternalStore` shape, different table + different lifecycle.

### `lib/website/` тАФ website data model + section registry (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 2)

The data shape every later session builds against. See `reference/builder-design.md` ┬з2 for the full design. Single-shape versioning (drafts and published share `Version`, distinguished by `status`). Section data is `Record<string, unknown>` at the registry boundary тАФ each section type's actual shape is exported from its own module and asserted at the Fields/Preview component boundary.

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `Website` (`{ id, clientId, name, domain, draftVersionId, publishedVersionId | null, createdAt, updatedAt }` тАФ no `brand`, that lives on the Client now), `Page` (`{ id, websiteId, slug, title, type: PageType, sections[], seo, createdAt, updatedAt }`), `Section` (`{ id, type: SectionType, enabled, data, ai? }`), `Version` (`{ id, websiteId, status, snapshot: { pages, header, footer, nav, pageOrder }, createdBy/At, publishedAt/By?, notes?, parentVersionId? }`), `NavLink` (`{ label, target: { kind: 'page', pageId } | { kind: 'href', href } }`), `BrandObject` + `VoiceTone` (kept here for now тАФ both Funnel and Website consume them; backend pass can hoist to `lib/brand/types.ts`), `WebsiteDomain`, `ContainerKind` (`'page' | 'funnelStep' | 'websiteHeader' | 'websiteFooter'` тАФ drives the registry's singleton constraint). **11 section types**: `hero | offer | trust | services | reviews | faq | cta | schedulePicker | thanksConfirmation | header | footer` тАФ the last two are website-level singletons (see registry). **5 page types**: `home | about | services | contact | generic` (funnel page types removed тАФ those live in `lib/funnel/types.ts`). `MAX_NAV_LINKS = 6` const exports the V1 forcing-function cap (design doc ┬з2.5).

- **`registry.ts`** тАФ `SectionTypeDefinition<TData>` (`{ type, label, description, defaultData, Fields, Preview, capabilityHints?, allowedContainers, allowedPageTypes?, implemented }`). `allowedContainers: readonly ContainerKind[]` enforces singleton vs stackable semantics: `'header'`/`'footer'` have `allowedContainers: ['websiteHeader' | 'websiteFooter']` and are not stackable in `Page.sections[]`; stackable types use `['page', 'funnelStep']`; funnel-only types (`schedulePicker`, `thanksConfirmation`) use `['funnelStep']`. `defineSection<TData>(def)` is a type-preserving helper for registrations.

- **`sections/index.ts`** тАФ the canonical const array `SECTION_REGISTRY` (no mutable registry; immutable list at module load). Order: stackable types first (hero / offer / trust / services / reviews / faq / cta), then funnel-only (schedulePicker / thanksConfirmation), then website-level singletons (header / footer). Accessors: `getSectionDefinition(type)`, `getImplementedSections()`, `getPlaceholderSections()`, `getSectionsForContainer(container: ContainerKind)`. Re-exports every section's `*Data` type for typed consumers. **Client-only consumers (the editor) read this.** Server-side consumers (the generation route's prompt builder + validation pipeline) MUST read `registry-meta.ts` instead тАФ see the next entry.

- **`sections/registry-meta.ts`** тАФ server-safe SSOT for section metadata. The section `*.tsx` modules carry `'use client'` because they ship React Fields/Preview components; Next's RSC bundler replaces every `'use client'` export with a `registerClientReference` stub in the server bundle. That made server reads of `SECTION_REGISTRY` crash with `TypeError: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'includes')` on `def.allowedContainers`. This module тАФ no `'use client'`, type imports only тАФ exports `SectionMeta` plus one `*Meta` const per section (`heroMeta`, `offerMeta`, тАж) and the `SECTION_REGISTRY_META` array. Each entry carries the metadata fields the generation server needs (`type`, `label`, `description`, `allowedContainers`, `allowedPageTypes?`, `implemented`, `capabilityHints?`, `elementLabels?`, plus `defaultDataKeys` тАФ a server-safe stand-in for `Object.keys(defaultData())`). Section modules import their `*Meta` entry and spread it into the `defineSection({...})` call, so the metadata lives here exactly once. **`SECTION_REGISTRY_META` and `SECTION_REGISTRY` in `index.ts` MUST stay aligned** тАФ adding a section type means adding it in both arrays (and adding its `defaultDataKeys` here when fields change).

- **`sections/_shared/CopyField.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ text/textarea field wired with per-field capability gating + AI controls. Wraps `BuilderField`/`BuilderInput`/`BuilderTextarea` in `<CapabilityGate capability="editCopy" mode="request">` so view-only users see the request-change affordance on hover. When `useAI` is held, renders inline rust-soft `тЬж Regen` and `тЖ╢ Original` buttons in the field's `hint` slot тАФ `Regen` cycles through a hardcoded `alternatives: readonly string[]` (stub-layer; Session 6 wires real AI), `Original` reverts to the `originalValue` prop. The `capability` prop defaults to `'editCopy'` but accepts `'editSEO'` for SEO-bound text. Every implemented section's Fields component uses this helper instead of raw `BuilderInput`.

- **`sections/_shared/MediaField.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ image-URL field gated on `editMedia`. Sibling to `CopyField`. Stub-layer is URL text input; real upload + crop UI lands when asset management ships.

- **`sections/hero.tsx`** (Session 2 тЖТ Session 4 тЖТ **Phase 6 uplift**) тАФ first section on the **element-inspector model**: its preview regions (`eyebrow` / `headline` / `subheadline` / `ctaPrimary` / `ctaSecondary`) are individually selectable; `Fields` switches on `selectedElement` and renders only that element's settings (text + that element's colour), or section-level settings (theme preset + background colour + layout/image-side cycles + image) when no element is selected. `HeroData`: `layout` (`split` | `overlay`), `theme` (`SectionTheme`), `imageSide`, eyebrow, two-line headline, sub, 2 CTAs, image. Preview renders full-bleed through `SectionShell`; the overlay scrim derives from the theme background so the theme drives both layouts. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.

- **`sections/offer.tsx`** (Session 2 тЖТ Session 4) тАФ `OfferData`: tag + title + price label/caption + newline-separated inclusions + scarcity copy + CTA. AI alts on title + scarcity. Preview: single-offer card with brand-tinted price + bulleted inclusions + warn-tinted scarcity + CTA. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.

- **`sections/services.tsx`** (Session 2 тЖТ Session 4) тАФ `ServicesData`: title + intro + `services: ServiceItem[]` (id/name/priceFrom/durationLabel/description). Add/remove buttons are `editLayout`-gated (`hide` mode on Remove, `disable` mode on the Add row). Per-item text fields use `CopyField` without alternatives (too item-specific to canonicalise). Preview: 2-col grid of service cards. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.

- **`sections/trust.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `TrustData`: eyebrow + rating value/max + rating source + years label + licence label + guarantee label. Preview: wrap-flex of trust pills, rating tile uses brand colour. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.

- **`sections/reviews.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `ReviewsData`: title + intro + `reviews: ReviewItem[]` (author/rating/body/age). Add/remove gated like services. Preview: 3-col grid of review cards with brand-coloured star strings. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`. Real GBP auto-pull arrives when the GBP integration wires in.

- **`sections/faq.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `FAQData`: title + intro + `items: FAQItem[]` (id/question/answer). Preview shows all Q/A pairs open (no accordion in the editor preview for scannability тАФ real frontend renders the accordion). Add/remove gated. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.

- **`sections/cta.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `CTAData`: tag + headline + sub + button label/href. AI alts on headline + sub. Preview: centred dark `bg-ink` callout block with brand-coloured tag, large headline, and a glowing brand-coloured CTA button. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.

- **`sections/schedulePicker.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `SchedulePickerData`: title + intro + duration label + earliest-slot caption. **Funnel-only** (`allowedContainers: ['funnelStep']`). Preview renders a 4-col mockup of available time slots with a "Mockup ┬╖ real availability pulls from the calendar integration" footer. Real picker wires in when bookings backend is ready.

- **`sections/thanksConfirmation.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `ThanksConfirmationData`: title + body + detail line + referral title/body/CTA. **Funnel-only** (`allowedContainers: ['funnelStep']`). Preview: centred success тЬУ + body + optional referral block. Leaving `referralTitle` blank hides the entire referral block in the preview.

- **`sections/header.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `HeaderData`: logo text + logo image URL + CTA label/href + `showCta` flag. **Website-level singleton** (`allowedContainers: ['websiteHeader']`). Preview: horizontal bar with brand-coloured logo + dashed-border `[ site nav ┬╖ from Website.nav ]` placeholder + brand-coloured CTA. **Important:** nav data lives on `Website.nav` (NOT in `HeaderData`); the Session 4 Header editor does NOT wire nav editing тАФ that requires extending the singleton editor's API to thread `Website`-level context into Fields, which is a deliberate punt for a future polish pass. The preview's nav placeholder communicates the boundary.

- **`sections/footer.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ `FooterData`: brand line + phone/email/address + 3 socials + legal copy. **Website-level singleton** (`allowedContainers: ['websiteFooter']`). Preview: 3-col footer on `bg-ink`, brand-coloured section labels, legal copy under a separator. Empty social handles hide rather than render.

- **`sections/placeholders.tsx`** (Session 4) тАФ **empty in Session 4** (all eight previously-stubbed types graduated). The file remains as the canonical home for any FUTURE V2 placeholder types тАФ `makePlaceholderSection` factory + `PlaceholderFields` + `makePlaceholderPreview` are still exported for that case.

- **`data-stub.tsx`** тАФ three stub websites demonstrating the publish lifecycle, plus the brand-by-client store (brand lives on the Client now per design doc ┬з2.3; no `brand` field on `Website`). **Voltline**: 3 pages (Home + About + Contact populated, Services page exists with empty sections тАФ partial-build state), published. **FreshHome**: 4 pages fully published (Home / About / Services / Contact), draft ahead of published with hero copy edits on Home тАФ demonstrates the Lane B submit-for-review flow when Session 5 lands. **KeyHero**: 1 home page, draft only, never published тАФ first-publish state for Session 8. NeatWorks has no website (empty state in the agency-mode roster). Exports `STUB_WEBSITES`, `STUB_VERSIONS`, `DEFAULT_PREVIEW_BRAND`, plus accessors `findWebsite`, `findWebsiteByClient`, `getWebsitesForClient`, `findVersion`, `getDraftForWebsite`, `getPublishedForWebsite`, and the brand resolver `getBrandForClient(clientId)`. **Distinct from `lib/funnel/data-stub.tsx`** тАФ that file holds the section-registry-backed funnel content; this one is the website data.

### `lib/website/` (cont'd) тАФ section-library uplift foundations (Phase 6 ┬╖ library uplift ┬╖ Phase 0)

> Phase 0 of the section-library uplift program. The library is being reworked so generated pages render like real websites, not editor schematics: each section type gains layout **variants** + a tonal **surface**, and the AI picks both. Phase 0 lays the shared foundations only тАФ it does NOT retrofit the existing 11 sections (each adopts these when uplifted). New section types `about / features / gallery / contact` were added to the `SectionType` union + the `section_type` Postgres enum (migration `0026`); their registry modules land in later phases.

- **`section-theme.ts`** тАФ the per-section colour model with **brand-default inheritance**. `SectionTheme` = three *optional* colour overrides (`background` / `heading` / `body`); `resolveTheme(overrides, brandDefaults, hardcoded)` resolves each colour down the chain `override ?? brand default ?? section hardcoded ?? platform fallback`, then derives `muted` / `border` / `card` / `cardBorder` / `isDark` via `mixHex`. `brandThemeDefaults(brand)` builds the brand-default layer from a brand's colour fields. `THEME_PRESETS` = 6 starter themes shown as circle swatches; `matchPresetId()` tells the picker which is active. So a brand default (set via "apply to all", or by the AI builder picking a palette) flows into every section that hasn't overridden the colour. Deliberately NOT global `@theme` tokens тАФ a section-library concern; plain hex.
- **`google-fonts.ts`** тАФ `CURATED_FONTS` (10 sans + serif display fonts) + `getFont(id)` + `googleFontsHref(ids)`. Brand stores a font *id* (`BrandObject.headingFont` / `bodyFont`, both optional тЖТ fall back to `inter-tight`). `next/font` is build-time so brand-chosen fonts load via the css2 API. Phase 0 ships a curated list; the browse-all-Google-Fonts picker lands later with a brand-editing surface.
- **`sections/_shared/SectionShell.tsx`** тАФ the shared full-bleed wrapper every uplifted section's `Preview` renders inside. Owns the section bg + base text colour (from the section's `theme`), the brand body font, Google-Font loading. Marks the section as a `@container` so section responsive classes use **container queries** (`@2xl:` etc.) тАФ they track the device-preview width, not the browser viewport. Props: `theme` (`ResolvedTheme`), `pad` (`none` | `tight` | `default` | `roomy`), `inset` (`band` = centred max-width column; `flush` = section self-manages its insets, for bleeding-image layouts), `maxWidth`, `backgroundLayer` (ReactNode rendered absolutely behind content тАФ overlay-hero scrims, image-backed CTAs). Replaces the old per-section `rounded-xl border bg-card` editor-card framing. `children` is a render-prop receiving `{ theme: ResolvedTheme, headingFont, bodyFont, accent }`.
- **`sections/_shared/GoogleFontLoader.tsx`** тАФ injects the css2 stylesheet `<link>` for a set of curated font ids. Rendered by `SectionShell`.
- **`sections/_shared/VariantField.tsx`** тАФ left/right cycle picker for a section's structural choices (layout / image-side). Sibling to `CopyField` / `MediaField`; gates on `editLayout` by default via `CapabilityGate mode="request"`.
- **`sections/_shared/ThemeField.tsx`** тАФ two theme controls: `ThemePresetField` (6 preset circles applying a whole `SectionTheme` тАФ a section-level quick start) and `ColorField` (a single labelled colour picker, placed under whichever element owns that colour). `ColorField` shows whether the colour is inherited from the brand default or locally overridden (with a Reset), and тАФ when `applyToAll` is set тАФ opens `ApplyToAllModal` after a change to offer promoting the colour to a brand default. Both gated on `editTheme`. `components/shared/website/ApplyToAllModal.tsx` is the modal ("Apply everywhere" = set brand default + drop the local override; "don't ask again" persists per-browser).
- **`sections/_shared/SelectableElement.tsx`** тАФ wraps a region of a section `Preview` so it is clickable to select in the editor (element-inspector model). Inert when given no `onSelect` (Preview rendered outside the editor / a non-selected section); otherwise clickable with a selection outline. `display: 'block' | 'inline-block'` for inline regions (CTA buttons).
- **`brand-style-stub.ts`** + **`use-brand-style.ts`** тАФ **STUB.** localStorage overlay for a client's brand-level style defaults тАФ fonts (heading / body) AND colour defaults (`headingColor` / `bodyColor` / `backgroundColor`), keyed by clientId; also the per-browser apply-to-all "don't ask again" flag. `BrandObject` carries these fields; `SectionEditor` merges the overlay over the resolved brand so changes propagate live to every section preview. Written by `SiteFontsMenu` (fonts) and the apply-to-all path (colours); the AI builder will write the same keys. `components/shared/website/SiteFontsMenu.tsx` is the toolbar font control. Replace with a brands-table write when a brand-editing surface ships.

### `lib/funnel/` тАФ funnel data model + publish lane (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 3.5 types; Session 7 stub; A3 publish + approval lane)

> **Architectural note.** Funnel types were locked shape-only in Session 3.5; Session 7 added the first stub data + editor wiring; **A3 wired the publish + approval lanes** (`mutations.ts` / `queries.tsx` / `approval.ts` / `preflight.ts`). The funnel data layer lives alongside the website data layer (same `Section` model, separate top-level type). See design doc ┬з2.0 for the funnel-vs-website distinction.
>
> **Naming overlap** with `lib/funnels/` (plural, Cluster 4) is intentional: `lib/funnel/` (singular) is the editable build model; `lib/funnels/` (plural) is the analytics-detail stub for `/funnels/[id]`. Different shape, different concern. The two coexist for the same Voltline funnel тАФ id `emergency-call-out` resolves in both stores. If a third domain joins, consider hoisting to `lib/funnel/{builder,analytics}/`.

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `Funnel` (`{ id, clientId, name, domain, draftVersionId, publishedVersionId, createdAt, updatedAt }` тАФ no `brand`, resolves through Client like Website does), `FunnelStep` (`{ id, funnelId, slug, title, type: FunnelStepType, sections[], seo, createdAt, updatedAt }`), `FunnelStepType` (`'landing' | 'schedule' | 'thanks' | 'optin' | 'upsell'` тАФ distinct from website's `PageType`; design doc ┬з2.0 spells out why), `FunnelVersion` + `FunnelVersionSnapshot` (`{ steps, stepOrder }`), `FunnelVersionStatus` (mirrors `VersionStatus`). Imports `Section` and `WebsiteDomain` from `lib/website/types.ts` тАФ sections and domain shape are shared, everything else is funnel-specific.

- **`data-stub.tsx`** (Session 7) тАФ Voltline's "$99 emergency call-out" funnel built against the section registry. Three steps: `landing` (hero + offer + trust + services + cta), `schedule` (schedulePicker), `thanks` (thanksConfirmation). Section content built against the section registry тАФ seed content for the funnel editor and the funnel queries' stub fallback. One published version + one draft (identical for now). Exports `STUB_FUNNELS`, `STUB_FUNNEL_VERSIONS`, plus accessors `findFunnel`, `getFunnelsForClient`, `findFunnelVersion`, `getDraftForFunnel`, `findStep`, `findStepBySlug`. FreshHome / KeyHero / NeatWorks ship without funnels тАФ the agency-mode roster on `/funnels` renders empty rows for them. When real backend lands, this stub is replaced by Supabase reads against `funnels` / `funnel_steps` / `funnel_versions` tables; the accessor surface stays the same.
- **`generation-stub.ts`** тАФ `generateFunnelStub(brief, options?)`, the funnel-generation handler. **Wired to real Claude** via `/api/generate-funnel` (Opus 4.7, ONE call for the seven-section landing step in the Sultanic / Suby order: `hero тЖТ offer тЖТ reviews тЖТ features тЖТ trust тЖТ reviews тЖТ form`); the schedule + thanks steps are built deterministically by the route + this module's `scheduleStepSections` / `thanksStepSections` helpers (chrome-only). Same fallback shape as `site-generation-stub.ts`: `503` (key unset) тЖТ silently fall back to the synchronous `generateFunnelSync` (deterministic passthrough through the website page generator); `500` тЖТ throw `AppError` so `CreateClientModal` surfaces the error; network throw (non-abort) тЖТ fallback. The legacy no-brief call still resolves to the registry-backed Voltline funnel (back-compat). The route assembles its `FunnelGenerationResult` by calling `buildFunnelSkeleton(brief, { landing, schedule, thanks })` тАФ exported here so the live + fallback paths produce identical shapes. Consumed by the create-client flow (`site-generation-stub.ts` / `lib/clients/create-client.ts`).
- **`mutations.ts`** тАФ the funnel publish + approval write path (A3 тАФ the funnel-shaped sibling of `lib/website/mutations.ts`). `publishFunnelDraft` (Lane A тАФ promote draft тЖТ published `funnel_version`, archive prior, move the funnel pointer, re-base the draft, clear `content_drafts`, and resolve any in-flight pending submission). `submitFunnelForApproval` (Lane B тАФ insert a `pending_approval` `funnel_version` + a `funnel_approval_submissions` row with the step-diff). `approveFunnelSubmission` / `rejectFunnelSubmission` / `recallFunnelSubmission` mirror the website operations. Also `updateFunnelSlug` + `saveSeoForSteps`. Each fires `notifyBuilder()` on success. **A funnel publishes as a unit** тАФ the whole step sequence ships together; no partial-step publish.
- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ funnel reads (`useFunnelsForClient` / `useAllFunnels` / `useFunnelVersions` / `useFunnelWithDraft`) **plus the A3 approval-lane hooks**: `useUserPendingFunnelSubmission(funnelId, userId)` (the submitter's pending submission тАФ drives the editor Lane B lock) and `useAllPendingFunnelApprovals()` (the operator `/tickets` queue). Both subscribe to `BUILDER_EVENT` so a publish / approve anywhere refetches.
- **`approval.ts`** (A3) тАФ `FunnelApprovalSubmission` + `FunnelApprovalStatus` display shapes (sibling of `lib/tickets/website-approval-stub.ts`; the submission state itself is the `funnel_approval_submissions` table, pre-aligned in migration 0015). `diffFunnelSnapshots` is the pure step-field diff producing the `{ pagesChanged, sectionsChanged, fieldsChanged }` approval summary (`FunnelApprovalDiff` reuses `WebsiteApprovalDiff` тАФ "pages" reads as "steps").
- **`preflight.ts`** (A3) тАФ the funnel-shaped preflight rule engine, sibling of `lib/website/preflight.ts`. Six rules over a `FunnelVersionSnapshot` (`{ steps, stepOrder }`, no header/footer chrome): step-has-sections + hero-content + cta-content + form-fields are `fail`; lead-capture-present + seo-title are `warn`. `runFunnelPreflight(snapshot, funnelId)` returns the same `PreflightReport` shape the website engine does, so `/funnels/[id]/review` reuses the shared `PreflightChecklist`.

### `lib/website/` (cont'd) тАФ autosave + publish lanes + approval store (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 5; **Phase 4: Supabase-wired** тАФ PR #41 / merge `534de96`)

The save тЖТ publish тЖТ approval pipeline behind the editor. **PR #41 deleted the localStorage `publish-stub.ts` / `draft-stub.ts` / `audit-stub.ts` modules and replaced them with Supabase reads + writes** against `website_versions` / `website_approval_submissions` / `force_publish_audit_log` / `content_drafts` / `brands` / `websites`. The reactive bus is the platform-standard event-bus pattern (`BUILDER_EVENT`) instead of the previous per-store custom events. Consumer hook surface (`useAutosave`, `useWebsitePublishState`, `useUserPendingSubmission`, `useAllPendingApprovals`) is unchanged.

- **`queries.tsx`** тАФ Phase 4 read path. Live Supabase reads over `websites` / `website_versions` / `content_drafts` / `website_approval_submissions` / `force_publish_audit_log` / `brands`. `useBuilderQuery` subscribes to `BUILDER_EVENT` and refetches, so every publish / approve / autosave anywhere refreshes every dependent surface. Exports the three reactive hooks (`useWebsitePublishState` / `useUserPendingSubmission` / `useAllPendingApprovals`) keeping their old return shapes тАФ `use-publish-state.ts` is now a re-export shim so existing consumers (`SectionEditor`, `VersionHistoryCard`, the `/tickets` approvals tab) are unchanged.
- **`mutations.ts`** тАФ Phase 4 write path. Async functions over Supabase, each firing `BUILDER_EVENT` on success. Operations (design doc ┬з3.3):
  - **`publishDraft(websiteId, actor, options?)`** тАФ Lane A. `mergeDraftsIntoSnapshot` overlays `content_drafts` onto the draft baseline, inserts a new `published` `website_versions` row, archives prior published, updates the website's `published_version_id` pointer, clears the website's `content_drafts` rows, resolves any in-flight pending submission to `approved`, and тАФ when `options.force` is set тАФ inserts a `force_publish_audit_log` row.
  - **`submitForApproval(websiteId, submitter, note?)`** тАФ Lane B. Same snapshot construction; inserts a `pending_approval` version + a `website_approval_submissions` row. Does NOT clear `content_drafts` тАФ submitter retains the draft so recall / reject puts them back in business. `diffSnapshots` (in `snapshot.ts`) computes the `{ pagesChanged, sectionsChanged, fieldsChanged }` summary stored on the submission.
  - **`approveSubmission(submissionId, approver)`** тАФ promotes the pending version тЖТ `published`, archives prior, updates pointer, clears drafts, marks submission `approved`.
  - **`rejectSubmission(submissionId, approver, reason)`** тАФ archives the pending version, marks submission `rejected` with the reason. Drafts untouched.
  - **`recallSubmission(submissionId)`** тАФ submitter recall; same end-state as reject but no reason recorded; status `recalled`.
  - **`restoreVersionAsDraft(websiteId, sourceVersionId, actor)`** тАФ Session 8 rollback (design ┬з7). Deep-copies a prior version's snapshot into a fresh `draft` version, archives any existing draft, wipes the website's `content_drafts` rows so the editor rehydrates from the restored snapshot. **Refuses while a pending submission is in flight** (would silently overwrite the submitter's diff). Returns `{ newDraftId }` or null.
- **`content-drafts.ts`** тАФ Phase 4 autosave write-buffer (replaces `draft-stub.ts`). A transient per-page / per-singleton / per-funnel-step buffer in the `content_drafts` table that overlays the draft version's baseline snapshot. One row per editable scope, keyed by the `(scope_kind, website_id, funnel_id, page_key)` unique constraint (NULLS NOT DISTINCT тАФ so the null funnel_id / null page_key collapse). `updated_by` must equal the signed-in user (RLS) тАФ the buffer is the user's own unsaved work; publish / approve clears the website's whole buffer. `DraftSlot` type kept from the stub layer: `{ kind: 'page', websiteId, pageId } | { kind: 'header', websiteId } | { kind: 'footer', websiteId } | { kind: 'funnelStep', funnelId, stepId }`. Public API: `loadDraft(slot)`, `loadDraftSections(slot)`, `saveDraftSections(slot, sections)` (upsert), `clearDraft(slot)`, `clearDraftsForWebsite(websiteId)`, `clearDraftsForFunnel(funnelId)`.
- **`snapshot.ts`** тАФ Phase 4 pure helpers (no I/O). `mergeDraftsIntoSnapshot(baseline, draftRows)` overlays the `content_drafts` buffer onto a draft version's baseline snapshot (slot wins where present, preserving `page.seo` тАФ the SEO panel writes straight to the draft version snapshot, not the per-section buffer). `diffSnapshots(prev, next)` produces the `{ pagesChanged, sectionsChanged, fieldsChanged }` approval summary тАФ lifted verbatim from the old `publish-stub` so the publish lanes keep identical behaviour.
- **`builder-events.ts`** тАФ Phase 4 reactivity bus. `BUILDER_EVENT = 'webnua:builder-change'` + `notifyBuilder()` + a subscriber helper. Replaces the previous `APPROVAL_EVENT` / `webnua:draft-change` custom events with one bus. Every mutation in `mutations.ts` and `content-drafts.ts` fires it; every reactive hook in `queries.tsx` subscribes.
- **`use-autosave.ts`** тАФ Session 5 (A) ┬╖ Phase 4 wiring. The hook driving section persistence. `useAutosave({ slot, sections, disabled? })` тЖТ `{ status: AutosaveStatus, lastSavedAt: number | null, retry }`. Statuses: `idle | pending | saving | synced | failed`. Behaviour (design doc ┬з3.2): every change to `sections` schedules a 500ms debounced flush; on flush, `saveDraftSections(slot, sections)` upserts the `content_drafts` row; status moves `saving тЖТ synced` (or `failed` on RLS / network error, with `retry()` to reattempt). First-render is skipped. `disabled: true` cancels any pending flush and parks at `idle` (used by the Lane B editor lock тАФ locked submitters mustn't keep writing). Submit-mid-edit edge case (┬з3.1) is docced тАФ server-snapshot defines the pending version's contents; in-flight 500ms edits stay in operator's local React state and fold forward on the next flush.
- **`use-publish-state.ts`** тАФ Phase 4 re-export shim. The three hooks (`useWebsitePublishState`, `useUserPendingSubmission`, `useAllPendingApprovals`) moved into `queries.tsx`; this module re-exports them so existing consumers' import paths are unchanged.
- **`preflight.ts`** тАФ Session 8 (design doc ┬з7). Declarative preflight rule engine. `PreflightRule` is `{ id, title, run(snapshot, context) тЖТ PreflightResult[] }` тАФ each rule is a pure function over a `VersionSnapshot` that emits zero-or-more results (one per affected page / section). `PreflightResult` carries `{ ruleId, status: 'pass' | 'warn' | 'fail', title, message, pageId?, sectionId?, fixHref? }`. `PREFLIGHT_RULES` is the const array (13 rules: page-has-sections, SEO title/description, hero content + CTA, offer content, CTA section, trust evidence, reviews/FAQ populated, header logo, footer contact, nav targets). `runPreflight(snapshot, context)` тЖТ `PreflightReport` (`{ results, counts, canPublish, allClear }`); `canPublish` is true when there are zero `fail`s, `allClear` adds zero `warn`s. `groupResultsByPage(results)` buckets results by `pageId` (with a `__site` bucket for header/footer/nav rules) for the per-page review cards. **Integration-prerequisite rules** (GBP for reviews, calendar for schedule) are deferred until the integrations data layer can answer "is X connected for this client" тАФ add a composable integration-aware rule set then. **B16 added `reviews-ai-placeholder`** тАФ a `warn` rule (one result per offending page) flagging reviews sections that still carry unedited AI-drafted placeholder testimonials; it reads `uneditedPlaceholderCount` from `placeholder-testimonials.ts`.
- **`placeholder-testimonials.ts`** тАФ **B16.** Detection layer for AI-invented testimonials. The website generator emits `reviews` sections with plausible-but-fake quotes + author names; shipping them live is a credibility risk. `toSection` (`generation-stub.ts`) snapshots the AI-drafted items onto `section.ai.placeholderSnapshot.reviews` (a `{ quote, authorName, authorRole }[]` тАФ added to `SectionAIMeta` in `types.ts`). **The detection heuristic is an EXACT content match:** a live review item is an "unedited placeholder" when its `quote` + `authorName` + `authorRole` still exactly equal a snapshot entry; the moment the operator edits any of that text it counts as a real review. **This is why the heuristic survives changes to the AI generator тАФ the snapshot is whatever was generated for THAT section, not a fixed string set.** Future edits to the generation prompts therefore need no change here; what MUST stay in lockstep is the snapshot shape тАФ if `toSection` ever stops writing `placeholderSnapshot`, or the reviews section renames `quote`/`authorName`/`authorRole`, detection silently returns 0 (fails open: no false warnings, but no nudge either). Exports `uneditedPlaceholderCount(section)` and `countUneditedPlaceholderTestimonials(snapshot)` (whole-site total, enabled sections only). Consumed by the `reviews-ai-placeholder` preflight rule, the `PlaceholderTestimonialBanner` editor nudge, and the `/website/review` publish-confirm copy. Funnel-generated reviews are NOT covered тАФ the funnel generator (`generate-funnel-live.ts`) is a separate path that does not call `toSection`, so funnel reviews never carry the snapshot and `uneditedPlaceholderCount` returns 0 for them (a safe no-op; CLAUDE.md's parked decision already says funnels never AI-generate testimonials).
- **`PlaceholderTestimonialBanner`** (`components/shared/website/PlaceholderTestimonialBanner.tsx`) тАФ **B16.** `'use client'` editor nudge shown at the top of `SectionFieldsPanel` when the open reviews section still has unedited AI placeholders. Amber-tinted; states the count and tells the operator to replace the placeholders with real reviews. Self-gates (renders null otherwise) so the mount site is unconditional. Dismissable per-section via a localStorage key (`webnua:testimonial-placeholder-ack:{sectionId}`) so an acknowledged section stops nagging on reopen. The banner clears automatically as the operator edits the last placeholder (count тЖТ 0).

### `lib/tickets/` (cont'd) тАФ website-approval submission shapes (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 5)

- **`website-approval-stub.ts`** тАФ Session 5 (B+C) ┬╖ Phase 4: **type-only display module.** The submission state is now the `website_approval_submissions` table тАФ written by `lib/website/mutations.ts`, read by the publish-state hooks in `lib/website/queries.tsx`. This module keeps only the display shapes the "Website approvals" tab and the Lane B editor-lock banner consume. `WebsiteApprovalSubmission` (`{ id, websiteId, pendingVersionId, submitterId, submitterName, submittedAt, status: 'pending' | 'approved' | 'rejected' | 'recalled', note?, diff: WebsiteApprovalDiff, snapshot, rejectionReason?, resolvedAt?, resolvedByName? }`). `WebsiteApprovalDiff` (`{ pagesChanged, sectionsChanged, fieldsChanged }`) тАФ shallow JSON-string compare counts, good for the V1 "X fields in Y sections" summary; per ┬з3.4 there's no field-level diff view V1.
- **`types.ts`** тАФ Session 5 added `'website-approval'` as a new `TicketCategory` enum value with `CATEGORY_LABEL['website-approval'] = 'Website approval'`. `pills.tsx` (`CategoryPill`) and `CategoryTile` got their record entries тАФ both render in rust on rust-soft to distinguish from the default `website` tone. The pills are wired but currently unused by the inbox row paths (the approvals tab uses `WebsiteApprovalRow` directly, not `TicketRow`); they're available if a future surface lists website-approvals alongside regular tickets.

### `admin/tickets/` (cont'd) тАФ website-approval row (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 5)

- **`WebsiteApprovalRow`** (`tickets/WebsiteApprovalRow.tsx`) тАФ Session 5 (E). Single pending-website-submission row inside the "Approvals" tab on `/tickets`. Admin-only. 4-cell grid: 36px rust-tinted client-initial avatar + `1fr` body (client name + diff summary + submitter / submitted-at / pages-touched meta) + 90px right-aligned relative age + actions row (Approve & publish тЬУ / Open in editor тЖТ / Reject тЬЧ). Reject expands inline (decision 3 in the Session 5 plan message): the actions row swaps for a warn-tinted reason `Textarea` + Cancel / Submit-rejection тЖй row. Submit button stays gated on non-empty reason. Approve calls `approveSubmission`; reject calls `rejectSubmission`. "Open in editor" routes to `/website` (per-page deep-link wasn't in the brief тАФ submissions are website-level since any of their pages could have changed).

### `admin/funnels/` тАФ funnel-approval row (A3 ┬╖ funnel publish + approval lane)

- **`FunnelApprovalRow`** (`funnels/FunnelApprovalRow.tsx`) тАФ the funnel-shaped sibling of `WebsiteApprovalRow`, rendered in the shared `/tickets` "Approvals" tab. Admin-only. Same 4-cell grid + inline-reject pattern; carries a rust `Funnel` pill to distinguish it from a website row, and a `Funnel: {name}` meta line. Approve calls `approveFunnelSubmission`, reject `rejectFunnelSubmission`. "Open in editor тЖТ" routes to `/funnels/[id]` (the funnel detail page carries the editor deep-link тАФ funnel submissions are funnel-level since the whole step sequence publishes as a unit).

### `app/tickets/_admin-content.tsx` тАФ augmented in Session 5 (E); A3

Now `'use client'`. Tab list is the static `adminTicketTabs` with a live `{ id: 'approvals', label: 'Approvals', count }` tab spliced in as the second entry. The count is `useAllPendingApprovals().length + useAllPendingFunnelApprovals().length` (website + funnel pending). `TicketTabsBar` runs in controlled mode (`value` + `onChange`). When the approvals tab is active the regular ticket table + filter bar both hide; `ApprovalsList` renders the `WebsiteApprovalRow`s then the `FunnelApprovalRow`s (one shared queue, empty-state card when both are clear).

### `lib/workspace/` тАФ agency vs sub-account context (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5)

The two-tier GoHighLevel-style workspace model. Operator's default view is **agency** (cross-client birds-eye, where triage/oversight happens). Drilling into a client via `AdminClientPicker` switches the context to **sub-account** mode for that client (where the actual managing/changes happen). Surfaces that exist in both modes (currently just `/settings/access`) dispatch on the context. Cross-client-only surfaces (`/tickets`, `/leads`, `/calendar`, `/automations`, `/campaigns`, the `/settings/integrations` matrix) stay agency-only for now; per-client sub-account variants land as each surface gets touched in future clusters. URL stays clean тАФ context is state-driven, not URL-driven.

- **`workspace-stub.tsx`** тАФ **STUB.** localStorage-backed React provider + hooks. Active client id lives in `webnua.dev.active-client-id`; absent = agency mode; populated = sub-account mode for that client. Exports `<WorkspaceProvider>` (mounted in `src/app/layout.tsx` inside `<UserProvider>`), `useWorkspace()` тЖТ `{ activeClientId, activeClient, hydrated, setActiveClientId, clearActiveClient }`, `useActiveClient()` (sugar), `useIsAgencyMode()` (sugar тАФ true when `activeClientId` is null). Defaults to agency mode (no key) on fresh load. Client-role users never see the picker (hidden in `ClientSidebar`), so the context has no effect for them. Two deletion points when real auth ships: this file, and the `<WorkspaceProvider>` mount.

### `lib/agency/` тАФ policy resolution layer (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 2)

> The three-layer model's spine (see the `## Agency / sub-account model` section near the top). Layer 2 (agency policy) + Layer 3 (sub-account overrides) + the resolver that merges them. Six policy keys, three wired to UI in Cluster 8, three typed + resolver-ready but deferred. **Supabase-backed caches**, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider` (PR #43); writes go straight to the policy tables and the in-memory caches update locally for snapshot stability. The resolver + hooks are unchanged from the stub-layer shape.

- **`types.ts`** тАФ the closed `PolicyKey` union (6 keys) + `POLICY_KEYS` / `LIVE_POLICY_KEYS` arrays + `POLICY_KEY_LABEL`. Per-key value types: `IntegrationDefaults`, `BrandDefaults`, `AutomationDefaults`, `PricingDefaults`. `PolicyValueMap` maps each key to its value type тАФ the resolver is typed to this, never `Record<string, unknown>`. `PolicyResolution<K>` (`{ effectiveValue, source: 'agency' | 'plan' | 'override', agencyValue, planValue }` тАФ Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 1 added `'plan'` + `planValue`) + `AllPolicyResolutions`. **Adding a policy key means amending this union AND the CLAUDE.md policy-key table тАФ don't widen it ad hoc.**
- **`agency-policy-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`** (filename is misleading; kept for import stability тАФ same trick as `auth/user-stub.tsx`). Layer-2 store. `AGENCY_POLICY_SEED` (frozen, derived from `CLIENT_DEFAULTS` + `adminDefaults*`) is the pre-hydration fallback; `hydrateAgencyPolicy()` overlays the real `agency_policy` table rows. `getAgencyPolicy(key)`, `getAllAgencyPolicy()`, `setAgencyPolicy(key, value)` (writes through to Supabase), `resetAgencyPolicy(key | '*')`, `subscribeAgencyPolicy(cb)`. Snapshot-cached per the CLAUDE.md stability rule.
- **`override-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`.** Layer-3 store backed by `policy_overrides` table (`Record<clientId, Partial<PolicyValueMap>>`). A key absent from a client's entry = inherit. Carries `SUB_ACCOUNT_OVERRIDE_SEED` (Session 4b) тАФ the per-client overrides that exist at platform start (the migrated former `AdminClient.seatLimit` values: Voltline `3`, KeyHero/NeatWorks `null`; FreshHome inherits). `hasOverride`, `getOverride`, `getOverridesForClient`, `setOverride`, `clearOverride`, `clearOverridesForClient`, `subscribeOverrides`.
- **`resolver.ts`** тАФ pure functions over the policy stores **and** (Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 1) the `lib/billing/` plan stores. `resolvePolicy(key, clientId)` тЖТ `PolicyResolution<K>`, walking `override тЖТ assigned-plan bundle тЖТ agency` (clientId null = agency mode, no plan layer). The first agency тЖФ billing link: resolver imports `getAssignedPlanId` / `getPlan` (value) from `lib/billing/`; `lib/billing/` imports `PolicyValueMap` (type-only) back тАФ no runtime cycle. `resolveAllPolicies(clientId)`.
- **`use-policy.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`. `usePolicy(key)` resolves against the active workspace (`useWorkspace`), reactive to the policy stores **and** the plan stores (catalog edits + reassignment move resolved values); `useAgencyPolicy(key)` is the raw Layer-2 value. Resolution snapshots cached per `(key, clientId)` against a JSON key (snapshot-stability rule).
- **`integration-providers.ts`** тАФ `INTEGRATION_PROVIDERS` тАФ display metadata (id / name / description) for the providers tracked by the `integrationDefaults` key. The ids must match the `sharedProviders` keys in `AGENCY_POLICY_SEED`. Shared by the `/settings/integrations` agency-mode connection-policy section + the sub-account integrations view.
- Verified by `/dev/agency-policy` (see `app/dev/` convention) тАФ the resolution matrix: every key ├Ч agency + each sub-account, with source flags + per-cell test-override toggle. Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 1 added per-plan columns (each plan's bundle value per key) so the plan layer reads straight against the resolved client cells.
- **Consuming surfaces:** the `/settings/integrations` agency-mode connection-policy section + `/settings/seats` (Session 3 тАФ agency-level, set Layer 2 via `useAgencyPolicy`/`setAgencyPolicy`). Session 4b тАФ sub-account override UI: `/settings/integrations` sub-account mode (`_sub-account-content.tsx`, per-provider `integrationDefaults` inherit/override via `usePolicy` + `setOverride`/`clearOverride`) and `ClientSeatLimitCard` (the seat limit resolves through `resolvePolicy('defaultSeatLimit', clientId)` тАФ see `lib/clients/seat-limit-stub.ts`).

> **Known follow-up (Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 1) тАФ RESOLVED (Session 7).** `/settings/integrations` sub-account mode (`_sub-account-content.tsx`) used to derive per-provider inherited-vs-overridden by comparing the *resolved* `integrationDefaults` against the *agency* value тАФ so a client on a plan whose integration bundle differed from the agency default showed every provider as "overridden". The design call: per-provider "revert" targets the **inherited** value тАФ the assigned plan's bundle when the client is on a plan, otherwise the agency default тАФ which is the value the client resolves to with no override. The view now computes `inherited = planValue ?? agencyValue` and compares against that; the source hint reads `plan ┬╖` vs `agency ┬╖` accordingly. A scan of the other resolver consumers (`/settings/billing` sub-account, `seat-limit-stub.ts`) confirmed neither carried the same pre-plan-layer shape.

### `lib/billing/` тАФ plan layer (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 9)

> The billing plan layer тАФ Layer 2.5 of the policy resolution stack (see the `## Agency / sub-account model` section). A plan packages a `Partial<PolicyValueMap>` bundle the agency offers as a tier; the resolver inserts it between the agency default and a per-sub-account override. **Supabase-backed caches**, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider` against `plan_catalog` + `plan_assignments` (PR #43 + migration `0025`). Real payment/Stripe is deliberately out of scope тАФ invoices stay display stubs.

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `Plan` (`{ id, name, description, price, currency, billingCycle, policy: Partial<PolicyValueMap> }`), `PlanAssignment` (`{ clientId, planId }`), `BillingCycle` (`'monthly' | 'yearly'`) + `BILLING_CYCLE_LABEL`. Imports `PolicyValueMap` from `lib/agency/` type-only (the agency тЖФ billing link тАФ no runtime cycle).
- **`plan-catalog-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`.** The catalog. `PLAN_CATALOG_SEED` (frozen тАФ Basic / Pro / Enterprise, each with a real seat-limit + capability-floor + integration-defaults bundle) is the pre-hydration fallback; the real catalog lives in `plan_catalog` (migration `0025`). `getPlanCatalog()`, `getPlan(id)`, `upsertPlan(plan)`, `removePlan(id)`, `resetPlanCatalog()`, `subscribePlanCatalog(cb)`. Snapshot-cached per the CLAUDE.md stability rule.
- **`plan-assignment-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`.** `Record<clientId, planId>` backed by `plan_assignments`. `PLAN_ASSIGNMENT_SEED` assigns voltlineтЖТbasic, freshhomeтЖТpro, keyheroтЖТpro (NeatWorks unassigned тАФ exercises the no-plan path). `getAssignedPlanId(clientId)`, `getAssignedPlan(clientId)`, `getAllPlanAssignments()`, `setPlanAssignment`, `clearPlanAssignment`, `subscribePlanAssignments`.
- **`hooks.ts`** тАФ `'use client'`. `usePlanCatalog()`, `usePlan(id)`, `useAssignedPlanId(clientId)`, `useAssignedPlan(clientId)` тАФ all `useSyncExternalStore` over the reference-stable stores.
- **Consuming surfaces:** `/settings/plans` (Session 2 тАФ agency-mode catalog editor). The resolver (`lib/agency/resolver.ts`) reads `getAssignedPlanId` + `getPlan`. **The sub-account `/settings/billing` plan-assignment UI was removed** (Phase 7 Stripe billing) тАФ sub-account billing now shows only the Stripe subscription; per-client plan assignment + the resolved-bundle view will return with the later-phase integrated upgrade path (plan tiers tied to access restrictions). The catalog + resolver are unchanged and still drive agency defaults.

### `lib/website/` (cont'd) тАФ form-to-page generation (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 6)

The Q&A-to-Page pipeline that backs `/website/new`. Spec lives in `reference/builder-generation-design.md`. Five locked questions (page type тЖТ primary intent тЖТ audience тЖТ specifics тЖТ avoid); stub generator deterministic on `(pageType, intent, audience)` with synthetic 4тАУ8s delay; validation pipeline + fallback log graduates straight to backend.

- **`generation-context.ts`** тАФ `GenerationContext` + the discriminated `PrimaryIntent` (including `'other'` with free-text fallback) + `Audience` + `ExistingPageSnapshot`. Chip-row data tables (`PAGE_TYPE_CHIPS`, `PRIMARY_INTENT_CHIPS`, `AUDIENCE_CHIPS`) + label helpers (`describeIntent`/`describeAudience`/`describePageType`) live here so the Q&A flow + review surface + dev preview share one source of truth.
- **`generation-prompt.ts`** тАФ pure prompt-block construction. Six blocks (`system | brand | page-questions | existing-pages | registry-catalog | example` тАФ the `example` block carries a fully-populated Voltline Electrical home page, see parked decision "Worked examples"). `buildPromptBlocks(ctx)` for the dev surface; `composePrompt(ctx)` glues them with `---` separators. The existing-pages block is omitted for first-page-of-website generation (empty `existingPages[]`). The registry-catalog block filters `SECTION_REGISTRY` by `allowedContainers.includes('page')` + `allowedPageTypes` (if set). Voice tone numeric axes тЖТ prose translation via `voiceToneToProse()`. Side-effect-free + no React; this is the piece that graduates to the real backend. **Per-section shape catalog** (`SECTION_SHAPE_CATALOG`): for every page-eligible section type, lists the variant key enum values (`layout`, `theme`, `imageSide`, `contentAlign`, `headerAlign`, `headlineSize`, `subSize`, `stackStyle`, `columns`, `mediaStyle`, `iconStyle`, `aspect`, `ctaStyle`, `nav`, `extra`, `mediaMode`, `mediaShape`, `overlay`, `footer`, `display`, `align`, `overlayOpacity`) with optional one-line picker guidance, and the per-array element object shape for `items` / `inclusions` / `signals` / `features` / `stats` / `badges`. **`SHARED_FIELD_NOTES`** (exported) is the appendix block both the website registry catalog AND the funnel field-keys block include: explains the `headlineAccent` / `titleAccent` semantic (an optional SECOND LINE in the accent colour, NOT a substring of the headline), lists the 74 curated icon ids, declares the item-`id` rule, and explains the `theme` object shape. **`formatSectionShape(type)`** (exported) is the helper the funnel prompt uses to emit a single section's catalog entry in the same shape as the website registry catalog. When the section module's TypeScript shape changes, update the matching `SECTION_SHAPE_CATALOG` entry тАФ these annotations are inline, not generated.
- **`generation-stub.ts`** тАФ handler + recipes + per-section copy library + validation pipeline (┬з4.4) + fallback log (┬з4.4a). `generatePageStub(ctx)` runs the synthetic delay then returns `{ generationId, page, fallbackLog, droppedSections }`; `generateSync(ctx)` is the no-delay variant for the dev preview. Per-page-type recipes (`home | services | about | contact | generic`) pick which sections appear and in what order. Three voice variants (`cold-ad-urgent | existing-calm | search-plain`) selected from `audience`. `GENERATION_PHASES` exports the three phase strings the status card cycles through. The free-text `specifics` + `avoid` answers are **received but not consumed** by the deterministic stub тАФ but the real generator (`generate-live.ts`) does consume them, since `composePrompt` feeds them to the model. **`assembleResult(ctx, rawSections, generationId, overrides?)`** is exported here тАФ it runs the ┬з4.4 validation pipeline + Page assembly and is shared by `generateSync` (the recipe path) and `generate-live.ts` (the real LLM path).
- **`generated-pages-stub.ts`** тАФ **STUB.** localStorage-backed overlay store. Key shape `webnua.dev.generated-pages.{websiteId}` тЖТ `Page[]`. `addGeneratedPage(websiteId, page)` writes; `mergeGeneratedPages(websiteId, seed)` returns seed-first list with the overlay appended (seed wins on id collision). Both the `/website` hub and the `/website/[pageId]` editor merge in at read time so the new page is visible and editable immediately. When real backend ships, replaced by a normal INSERT against the `pages` table; the merge helper goes away (seed = backend reads).

### `lib/website/` (cont'd) тАФ section library uplift (Phase 6 ┬╖ library uplift ┬╖ PR #45)

> PR #45 expanded the section library: four net-new section types (`about`, `features`, `gallery`, `contact`) and significant rewrites of the existing eight to add per-variant layouts + element inspectors. Migration `0026` extends the `section_type` Postgres enum to match. `services.tsx` was demoted to `implemented: false` in this pass (kept in the registry so seed pages still parse; new sections can't be added).

- **`sections/about.tsx`** (~1,060 lines) тАФ `about` section type. Variant set + element-inspector model + `CopyField` / `MediaField` per element. `allowedContainers: ['page']`; `allowedPageTypes: ['home', 'about', 'generic']`.
- **`sections/contact.tsx`** (~909 lines) тАФ `contact` section type. Variants with form / map / hours / address blocks; element inspector covers each region. `allowedContainers: ['page']`.
- **`sections/features.tsx`** (~956 lines) тАФ `features` section type. Variant set with N-column feature grids; per-feature `IconField` + `CopyField`s. Add/remove gated on `editLayout`. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`.
- **`sections/gallery.tsx`** (~821 lines) тАФ `gallery` section type. Variants for grid / carousel / masonry; per-image `MediaField`. `allowedContainers: ['page']`.
- **`sections/_shared/IconField.tsx`** тАФ capability-gated icon picker over `section-icons.ts`'s curated set. Gated on `editLayout`.
- **`sections/_shared/ColumnsField.tsx`** тАФ variant cycle for N-column layouts (used by `features`, `gallery`, etc.). Gated on `editLayout`.
- **`sections/_shared/SocialGlyph.tsx`** тАФ small inline social-icon glyph used by `footer.tsx` + `contact.tsx`.
- **`sections/_shared/StarRow.tsx`** тАФ N-star row used by `reviews.tsx` + `trust.tsx` previews; brand-coloured.
- **`sections/_shared/section-icons.ts`** (~214 lines) тАФ the curated icon library `IconField` chooses from. Closed set + label + the icon SVG path.
- **`sections/_shared/grid.ts`** тАФ grid maths helpers (column-count тЖТ Tailwind classes, etc.) for the variant layouts.

### `lib/website/` (cont'd) тАФ lead-capture form builder (Phase 6 ┬╖ form builder ┬╖ PR #46)

> PR #46 added the entire form-builder feature тАФ see `reference/form-builder-design.md` for the retroactive design doc. New `editForms` capability + new `form` section type + the `Section.form?: FormConfig` envelope. Migration `0029` adds `editforms` to the `capability` Postgres enum; `0030` adds `form` to the `section_type` enum; `0031` adds the `lead_attachments` Storage bucket + RLS. The `form_submitted` `lead_events` kind carries the captured submission.

- **`form-config.ts`** (~176 lines) тАФ the form's field shape + per-field config. Field types: `text | email | phone | textarea | select | checkbox | image | date`. `date` was added with the funnel qualification step (native `<input type="date">`, no calendar-availability lookup тАФ kept simple for V1; the funnel's qualification form pairs it with a Morning/Afternoon/Evening `select` to ask for the request, not pick a confirmed slot). `FormConfig = { fields: FormField[]; submitLabel: string; successMessage: string }`. Field-level config: `required`, `placeholder`, `options` (for `select`), `accept` (for `image`).
- **`sections/form.tsx`** (~196 lines) тАФ registers the `form` section type. `allowedContainers: ['page', 'funnelStep']`. Preview renders the form via `FormBlock`; editor renders the form-controls panel via `SectionFormControls`. Distinct concern from a section's `Section.form` envelope тАФ the section type IS-a form; the envelope ATTACHES-a form to another section (currently `hero`).
- **`section-form-slot.ts`** тАФ declares which section types may host a `Section.form` envelope (currently `hero` only тАФ see the form-builder design doc). One source of truth for "can this section type carry a form?".
- **`components/shared/website/FormBlock.tsx`** (~399 lines) тАФ the rendered form. Used inside the `form` section's preview AND inside any envelope-hosting section's preview. Validates required fields client-side; submission lands in `leads` + `lead_events` (`form_submitted`).
- **`components/shared/website/SectionFormControls.tsx`** (~714 lines) тАФ the per-field editor surface. Add / remove / reorder fields (each gated on `editForms` via `CapabilityGate`); per-field name / label / required / options / etc. Lives in the editor's fields panel.
- **`components/shared/website/FormFieldTypePicker.tsx`** (~60 lines) тАФ small picker `Dialog` invoked by the `+ Add field` button. Shows the seven field types + an icon glyph + description; picking one appends a fresh field at the registry's default config.
- **`lib/leads/upload-attachment.ts`** (~47 lines) тАФ image-attachment upload helper for the `image`-typed form field. Uploads to the `lead_attachments` Storage bucket (migration `0031`); returns the public URL the form-submit then stores on the `lead_events.payload`. RLS on the bucket: anonymous read of objects under `{client_slug}/{lead_id}/`; writes from the public-submit flow only.

### `lib/website/` (cont'd) тАФ real Claude generator (Phase 6 ┬╖ PR #47 ┬╖ this PR)

The Phase 6 generator pair, called via the `/api/generate-site` route. See the parked decision "Phase 6 generation fallback policy" for the silent-vs-thrown contract. `generation_log` writes documented inline in the API-routes section below.

- **`generate-live.ts`** тАФ server-only. `generatePageLive(ctx, generationId?)` тАФ the real Claude call: `composePrompt(ctx)` тЖТ `claude-opus-4-7` (adaptive thinking, streamed, `max_tokens: 64000`, cached system prompt) тЖТ defensively-parsed JSON тЖТ `assembleResult` (same ┬з4.4 validation pipeline the deterministic stub uses). Optional `generationId` lets the route share one uuid across all per-page calls so `generation_log` rows group cleanly; defaults to `crypto.randomUUID()` standalone. Imported only by the route handler so `@anthropic-ai/sdk` stays out of the client bundle. `SYSTEM_PROMPT` is the conversion-copywriter persona + the strict JSON output contract.
