- **`site-generation-stub.ts`** тАФ browser-side caller. `generateSiteStub(brief, options?)` POSTs the brief (plus the optional `clientId` for `generation_log` attribution) to `/api/generate-site` and returns the `SiteGenerationResult`. **Fallback policy:** `503` (key not configured) тЖТ silent fallback to `generateSiteSync` for dev; `500` (real failure) тЖТ throw `AppError` with the server's `{ name, status, detail }` body so `CreateClientModal` surfaces the actual error; network throw (non-abort) тЖТ fallback with `console.warn`. `generateSiteSync(brief)` is the deterministic no-I/O variant (dev / test).

### `app/api/` тАФ server routes

- **`generate-site/route.ts`** тАФ see the entry in `admin/` create-client flow above for the full contract. Real Claude website generator with `generation_log` observability.
- **`generate-seo/route.ts`** тАФ server-only Claude-backed SEO drafter. Called by `lib/website/seo-generate.ts` via `fetch('/api/generate-seo')`; runs an Anthropic message per target (page or funnel step) and returns `{ title, description }` per id. Returns `503` when `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is unset (the client's caller falls back to the deterministic generator), `500` on failure. Server-only тАФ the SDK stays out of the client bundle. Same fallback shape as the website generator.
- **`generate-offer/route.ts`** тАФ server-only Sonnet-backed funnel-offer drafter (the four-field offer the wizard captures: `{ headline, promise, riskReversal, ctaText }`). Called by `lib/website/offer-generate.ts` via `fetch('/api/generate-offer')`. **Sonnet 4.6, not Opus** тАФ short structured copy doesn't need Opus pricing; thinking enabled (`budget_tokens: 2000`, `max_tokens: 4000` тАФ Anthropic requires `max_tokens > thinking.budget_tokens`, hence the 4000-token envelope ahead of a ~150-token output). System prompt is a Suby/Sultanic direct-response brief with concrete examples per field, a hard ban list of AI corporate-speak ("comprehensive", "leverage", "elevate", etc.), and length caps (headline тЙд12 words, promise тЙд25, risk-reversal тЙд15, CTA тЙд6). Returns `503` (key unset тЖТ caller throws `AppError.validation` so the wizard surfaces "configure ANTHROPIC_API_KEY" rather than degrading silently тАФ a stub offer at this step would be misleading), `400` (missing required brief fields), `500` (real failure with `{ name, status, detail }` body, PR #58 pattern). **No `generation_log` write** тАФ the wizard runs offer generation BEFORE the client row exists, and `generation_log.client_id` is NOT NULL; failures land in console + the 500 detail. Matches the `generate-seo` precedent.
- **`enhance-offer/route.ts`** тАФ server-only Sonnet-backed offer-text polish. Called by `lib/website/offer-generate.ts` `enhanceFunnelOfferText` from the wizard's brief step "тЬж Enhance with AI" button. Takes a rough offer paragraph the operator typed + light context (industry / business name / service area) and returns a tighter polished version (`{ text: string }`) тАФ same voice, more concrete, no invented facts, same banned-corporate-speak list as `/api/generate-offer`. **Sonnet 4.6** (matches the offer-generation model choice); `thinking: { type: 'enabled', budget_tokens: 2000 }`, `max_tokens: 4000`. Returns `503` (key unset тЖТ caller throws `AppError.validation`), `400` (missing `rawText` or bad body), `500` (real failure with `{ name, status, detail }` body, PR #58 pattern). **No `generation_log` write** тАФ the wizard runs this BEFORE the client row exists, same as `/api/generate-offer`. Replaces the previous `enhanceOffer` deterministic stub in `CreateClientModal.tsx` (4-rule text rewriter that did nothing when the input already passed all rules тАФ the cause of the "Enhance with AI not working" report). Sibling of `/api/generate-offer`, distinct concern (polish a free-form paragraph vs draft the four-field structured offer).
- **`enhance-field/route.ts`** тАФ server-only generic Sonnet-backed freeform-field enhancer. Sibling of `/api/enhance-offer` but with a different framing: research-grade copywriter who interviews the operator to draw out specificity, vs offer-route's direct-response conversion-copy framing. Body: `{ fieldName, currentValue, briefContext?: { businessName, industry, serviceArea, funnelService } }`. Response: `{ enhanced: string }`. **Sonnet 4.6**, `thinking: { type: 'enabled', budget_tokens: 2000 }`, `max_tokens: 4000` (Anthropic requires `max_tokens > budget_tokens`). Same fallback contract as `enhance-offer`: `503` (key unset тЖТ caller throws `AppError.validation`), `400` (missing `fieldName` or `currentValue`), `500` (real failure with `{ name, status, detail }` body, PR #58 pattern). **No `generation_log` write** тАФ same precedent as `enhance-offer` / `generate-offer` / `generate-seo`: wizard runs before client row exists, `generation_log.client_id` is NOT NULL. Browser caller is `lib/website/field-enhance.ts` `enhanceField`. UI is `components/shared/EnhanceableTextarea` (accept/reject preview, see parked decision below). Used today by the wizard's `funnel_customer_pain` field. The offer field keeps `/api/enhance-offer` тАФ different system prompt fits direct-response copy better than the generic specificity-drawing-out framing. Add new freeform brief-step fields to this route as the wizard grows; use `enhance-offer` only for offer-shaped copy.
- **`generate-funnel/route.ts`** тАФ server-only Claude-backed funnel generator. **Two parallel Opus 4.7 calls** тАФ one per non-deterministic step. Step 1 (lead-capture landing) = 7 sections in Sultanic / Suby order (`hero тЖТ offer тЖТ reviews тЖТ features тЖТ trust тЖТ reviews тЖТ form`); the form is restricted to **name + email only** and the same form is attached to the hero via the `Section.form` envelope so the visitor can convert above the fold OR at the bottom. Step 2 (qualification) = 4 sections (`hero тЖТ reviews тЖТ features тЖТ form`) reinforcing the booking decision and qualifying the lead тАФ phone, service address, preferred date (`date` field), preferred time of day (`select`: Morning / Afternoon / Evening), budget (`select` with trade-typical bands). Step 3 (thanks) is deterministic chrome from `funnel/generation-stub.ts` reading the thanks-section defaults from `registry-meta.ts`'s `defaultDataValues` snapshot тАФ the `schedulePicker` section type is no longer used. Both Claude calls share one `generation_id` so their combined fallback log writes as one group. Same fallback contract as `/api/generate-site`: `503` (key unset), `400` (bad body), `500` (real failure with `{ name, status, detail }` body). `maxDuration = 300`. **Lead-link across steps тАФ WIRED.** The public `/api/forms/submit` route accepts an optional `existingLeadId`; when present and the lead belongs to the same `clientId`, the route appends a second `form_submitted` `lead_events` row to that lead instead of inserting a new one (mirrors the editor-side `submitLead(existingLeadId)` branch in `lib/leads/queries.tsx`). `FormBlock` reads `?lead=` from `window.location.search` on mount and posts it as `existingLeadId`; after a step-1 submission with `afterSubmit.kind === 'nextStep'`, it appends `?lead=<createdLeadId>` to the next-step URL. Step 1 + step 2 from one visitor therefore land as a single lead with two timeline events. See the parked decision "Funnel lead threading uses ?lead=<id> URL parameter" below for the trigger to revisit. Called by `lib/funnel/generation-stub.ts` `generateFunnelStub` via `fetch('/api/generate-funnel')`. **ONE Opus 4.7 call** generates the seven-section funnel-landing step in the locked Suby/Sultanic order (`hero тЖТ offer тЖТ reviews тЖТ features тЖТ trust тЖТ reviews тЖТ form`); the schedule + thanks steps stay deterministic (chrome-only, no inputs an LLM would need to differentiate them). Body is a `ClientBrief` + optional `clientId`. Returns a `FunnelGenerationResult` тАФ same shape `generateFunnelSync` returns, so the client swaps stub for live transparently. Same fallback contract as `/api/generate-site`: `503` (key unset, caller silently falls back), `400` (bad body), `500` (real failure with `{ name, status, detail }` body тАФ surfaced in `CreateClientModal` via `AppError`). Writes `generation_log` rows for every missing-field fallback via the service-role client, gated on `clientId`. Server-only тАФ `@anthropic-ai/sdk` stays out of the browser bundle. `maxDuration = 300`. See the parked decision "Funnel vs offer generator model choice" for the Opus-here / Sonnet-on-offer split.

- **`lib/website/generate-funnel-live.ts`** тАФ server-only counterpart to `generate-live.ts`. Exports two functions: `generateFunnelLandingLive` (Step 1 тАФ 7 sections) and `generateFunnelQualificationLive` (Step 2 тАФ 4 sections). Both run Opus 4.7 with `thinking: { type: 'adaptive' }` (`max_tokens: 16000`, streamed, cached system prompt). Two separate system prompts: the lead-capture prompt enforces the Sultanic / Suby section order and frames the form as name+email-only minimum-friction; the qualification prompt frames the page as homestretch reassurance ("you're almost booked") and frames the features section as a concrete what-happens-next sequence. Both consume the same brand + funnel-brief + offer + testimonial set; the chosen offer's headline / promise / risk-reversal / CTA flow into Step 1 verbatim and are not re-pitched in Step 2. Defensive JSON parsing tolerant of code fences. The output runs through a funnelStep-typed validation pipeline (mirror of `runValidationPipeline` in `generation-stub.ts` тАФ the website version is page-typed, so we duplicate that slice rather than refactor the registry pipeline). **Form-config builders live here**: Step 1's `buildLeadCaptureFormConfig` returns `{ name, email }` (submit label from the offer's CTA text), Step 2's `buildQualificationFormConfig` returns `{ phone, service-address, preferred-date (date), time-of-day (select Morning/Afternoon/Evening), budget (select with trade bands) }`. Both forms use `afterSubmit: { kind: 'nextStep' }` so the public renderer's step-router moves the visitor forward. On Step 1 the same form is also attached to the `hero` section via `Section.form` envelope (so the form appears above-the-fold AND at the bottom тАФ both feed the same lead when leadId threading lands). Imported only by `/api/generate-funnel` so the Anthropic SDK never reaches the client bundle.

### `shared/website/` (cont'd) тАФ form-to-page UI primitives (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 6)

- **`QuestionCard`** (`website/QuestionCard.tsx`) тАФ single Q&A step inside `/website/new`. Composes `BuilderStepHeader` + body slot + `BuilderFooterActions`. Discriminates Continue vs Skip via `required` + `isAnswered`: required & empty disables Continue; optional & empty shows both "Skip тЖТ" and "Continue тЖТ". Body slot is open тАФ chip rows, textareas, or the chip-or-free-text dual mode used by Q2's "Other" option.
- **`GenerationStatusCard`** (`website/GenerationStatusCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` ink-bg "// GENERATING тЬж" card. Rotating тЬж glyph + "Drafting your pageтАж" + phase copy cycling on a 1.6s interval (`GENERATION_PHASES`). When Q4 or Q5 had content, the card mounts a separate "// RECEIVED" footer block with тЬУ-prefixed lines reading "Got your specifics тАФ will shape the final draft." / "Got your avoid notes тАФ will be honoured." **Framing rule locked in the design doc ┬з1:** never echo Q4/Q5 inline with phase copy as the AI consuming them in real time тАФ that would mislead users into thinking the stub-output ignoring those answers is a bug.
- **`NewPageEntry`** (`website/NewPageEntry.tsx`) тАФ the "+ New page" / "тЬж New page" CTA on `/website`. Encapsulates the two-cap gating story (`editPages` + `useAI`): both тЖТ rust `Link` to `/website/new`; `editPages` only тЖТ hidden (V2 manual-new-page modal lands here later); missing `editPages` тЖТ `<CapabilityGate mode="request">` reveals the request-change affordance. Inlining this on the hub would force every reader to re-derive the three-state gating from the JSX; the wrapper keeps the hub readable.

### `app/website/new/` тАФ Q&A generation flow (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 5 ┬╖ Session 6)

- **`page.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'` flow root. State lives in URL search params (`?step=N&pageType=...&intent=...&intentOther=...&audience=...&specifics=...&avoid=...`), no localStorage тАФ refresh + back/forward work natively; 90-second form doesn't warrant cross-tab merge complexity. Six logical steps: 1-5 questions (each via `QuestionCard`) тЖТ 6 review summary with inline "Edit тЬО" links bouncing back to the relevant question while preserving the rest. On Generate, mounts `GenerationStatusCard` with `specifics`/`avoid` passed through, calls `generatePageStub(ctx)`, writes via `addGeneratedPage`, routes to `/website/[newPageId]`. The route doesn't re-check caps (the gated `NewPageEntry` already filtered); the review-card Generate button is disabled with a fallback explainer if the user somehow lacks `editPages + useAI` on this workspace.

### `app/dev/generation-preview/` тАФ Session 6 dev surface

- **`page.tsx`** тАФ Off-nav dev utility per the `app/dev/` convention (deletion-point: same lifecycle as `/dev/capabilities` + `/dev/sections`). Three-column layout: inputs (page-type chips / intent chips + Other input / audience chips / specifics + avoid textareas) тЖТ prompt blocks (expandable per-block details) тЖТ stub output (Generated page summary + validation log + full JSON). All three columns re-render on every input change тАФ no Generate button, the live linkage is the whole point. Validates the prompt-construction layer (which graduates to real backend) in isolation from the stub recipes (which don't).

### `admin/team/` тАФ team-invite flow (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ team invite)

> **Architectural note тАФ `/settings/team` is a shared-slug dispatcher (Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite).** Both roles now reach a "Team" tab from their own nav, so `app/settings/team/page.tsx` is a `'use client'` role dispatcher (same pattern as `/settings/integrations`): operator тЖТ `_admin-content.tsx` (the workspace team-invite flow below); client тЖТ `_client-content.tsx` (the client's own-account teammate list тАФ see `app/settings/team/` entry). The 3-step operator modal stays admin-only by virtue of mounting only inside `_admin-content.tsx`.

> The first real management UI for the capability layer. A 3-step `Dialog`-based modal launched from the operator `/settings/team`. Screens 37-39 in the platform prototype. The flow captures org-structure decisions (who / what role / which clients) as a discrete attributable `TeamInvite` record (vision ┬з7). Built as pure composition over `Dialog` / `Button` / `Input` / `Textarea` + the capability layer.
>
> **Prototype disagreements converged:** (1) the prototype's Step 2 allow/deny bullets ("Edit Meta ad campaigns", "See revenue/billing") are off the 13-cap builder model тАФ the preview is driven **purely from the 13 real capabilities** instead (see the parked decision below). (2) The prototype shows a pre-filled readonly demo; the real modal is an empty interactive form. (3) The prototype sizes Step 3 narrower than Steps 1-2 тАФ a single step-switching `Dialog` can't resize per step, so the flow uses one `size="lg"` (920px) throughout.

- **`TeamInviteModal`** (`team/TeamInviteModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` orchestrator. Owns step state (`1 | 2 | 3`) + the `TeamInviteDraft` form state + the committed `TeamInvite` once sent. Modal chrome comes from `shared/invite/InviteModalChrome` (extracted at the second use тАФ see that entry). Step 1 = invite form (email / full name / role pick / client-access selection / personal note); Step 2 = invitee ink card + `PermissionPreview` + "what happens after" box; Step 3 = success state + copyable magic link + "what happens next". Step 1тЖТ2 is gated on a non-empty email and (for junior) тЙе1 assigned client. On send, builds one `TeamInvite` record and (stub) `console.log`s it. Step-2 invitee card + Step-1 client-access row stay local subcomponents (operator-specific, single-use).
- **`InviteTeamButton`** (`team/InviteTeamButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` trigger: a `size="sm"` "+ Invite member" `Button` + `TeamInviteModal` open-state owner. Mounted on `/settings/team`. Same pattern as `AddBookingButton` / `NegativeReviewAlertButton`.
- **`InviteStepper`** (`team/InviteStepper.tsx`) тАФ generic N-dot progress indicator. Props: `steps` + `current` (1-indexed). Steps before `current` render done (good check), `current` renders rust with a soft ring, the rest paper-2. First stepper primitive in the codebase тАФ kept in `admin/team/` (only consumer); move to `shared/` if a second flow needs it.
- **`RoleSelectCard`** (`team/RoleSelectCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` selectable role card (icon tile + name + description), used 3-up in Step 1. Borrows `ReframeOptionCard`'s `data-selected` + rust-border-on-active idiom but is its own shape (compact icon-tile card vs `ReframeOptionCard`'s 22px display-headline card тАФ reuse would have fought both).
- **`PermissionPreview`** (`team/PermissionPreview.tsx`) тАФ **the cap-wired component.** Iterates `ALL_CAPABILITIES`, partitions allow/deny by membership in `TEAM_ROLE_CAPABILITIES[role]`, labels each with `CAPABILITY_LABEL`, and uses `CAP_EXPLAINER[cap].short` as the deny-line hover title. Never a hand-written list тАФ role тЖТ permissions is computed. Renders a one-line note for owner/operator explaining they look identical here because they only diverge on billing/governance (outside the cap model).

### `shared/invite/` тАФ invite-modal chrome (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite)

> Extracted at the second use (operator `TeamInviteModal` + client `ClientTeamInviteModal`). Deliberately the **intersection** of what both modals need тАФ the structural rhythm + the two in-body form primitives тАФ not the union. Anything one modal needs and the other never does (operator role-pick, client seat-meter) stays composed in that modal, never bolted on here as an optional prop.

- **`InviteModalChrome`** (`invite/InviteModalChrome.tsx`) тАФ exports: `INVITE_DIALOG_CONTENT_CLASS` (the shared `DialogContent` className тАФ each modal still composes its own `Dialog`/`DialogContent size="lg"`), `InviteModalHeader` (rust/good mono tag + `<em>`-rust title + subtitle + close), `InviteModalFooter` (mono info line + action-button slot), `InviteSection` (labelled form section with `last` rhythm flag), `InviteFieldLabel` (mono uppercase field label + optional `required` asterisk), `InviteCopyLinkRow` (the dashed-border magic-link + copy button on both confirmation steps), and the `inviteInitials(fullName, email)` helper.

### `client/team/` тАФ client-side teammate invite (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite)

> The client-role counterpart to the operator team-invite. A client business owner invites a user into their **own** client account тАФ fixed client (no picker), flat access (no role pick): every invitee resolves to the `CLIENT_DEFAULTS` floor (`viewBuilder` only); per-website edit grants stay an operator concern via `/settings/access`. With no role/access decision to review, the flow is **2 steps, not 3** тАФ inventing a review step for a flat invite would be drift (same logic as Session 3's Step-2 call). The access reality is communicated inline on Step 1. Net-new тАФ the client prototype has no team surface.

- **`ClientTeamInviteModal`** (`team/ClientTeamInviteModal.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` 2-step `Dialog` modal. Composes `shared/invite/InviteModalChrome`. Step 1 = form (email required / optional full name / default-access explainer / `SeatUsageMeter` + seat-blocked warn block / optional note); Step 2 = success state + `InviteCopyLinkRow` + "what happens next". The send is seat-gated тАФ `canInviteToClient(clientId)` disables the Send button AND re-guards inside `handleSend` (the count can move while the modal is open). On send, commits one attributable `ClientUserInvite` via `addClientInvite`.
- **`InviteTeammateButton`** (`team/InviteTeammateButton.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` "+ Invite teammate" trigger + modal open-state owner. Resolves the inviter's own `clientId` from `useUser()`; renders null for a user with no client. Sibling of `admin/team/InviteTeamButton`.
- **`SeatUsageMeter`** (`team/SeatUsageMeter.tsx`) тАФ presentational "N of M seats used" indicator (bar + count, or uncapped variant when `limit` is null). Takes a resolved `SeatUsage` тАФ the caller fetches it reactively via `useClientSeatUsage`. Used on the client Team tab, inside `ClientTeamInviteModal`, and inside the operator `ClientSeatLimitCard`.

### `shared/settings/` (cont'd) тАФ client seat-limit control (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite)

- **`ClientSeatLimitCard`** (`settings/ClientSeatLimitCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` operator control for one client's seat limit, mounted on `/settings/access` in **sub-account mode** as a visually-distinct `SettingsSection` separate from the capability grid (the seat limit is a contract/plan axis тАФ how many users тАФ not the capability axis тАФ what users can do). Number input + "No limit" checkbox + Save (disabled until dirty); shows the live `SeatUsageMeter` and the most-recent `SeatLimitChange`. **Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4b** тАФ resolver-backed: the limit resolves through `resolvePolicy('defaultSeatLimit', clientId)`, so the card shows a `PolicySourceBadge` (inherited vs a per-account override) and a "Revert to agency" affordance (`inheritSeatLimit`) when overridden. **Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 1** тАФ the inherited-source hint distinguishes "from plan" vs "from agency" via `getInheritedSeatLimit` (the plan layer can supply the inherited seat limit). Admin-only тАФ placed in `shared/settings/` following the `CapabilityToggleGrid` precedent. Calls `setSeatLimit` with the operator's id for attribution.
- **`PlanEditorCard`** (`settings/PlanEditorCard.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Cluster 9 ┬╖ Session 2. Operator editor for one billing plan, mounted on `/settings/plans` (agency mode). Edits the plan's identity (name / description / price / currency / billing cycle) and its policy bundle тАФ seat limit, capability floor (`Switch` per `ALL_CAPABILITIES`), integration defaults (`Switch` per `INTEGRATION_PROVIDERS`). Local draft state with a previous-render re-sync; Save writes through `upsertPlan`, Delete (confirm) through `removePlan`. Admin-only тАФ in `shared/settings/` following the `CapabilityToggleGrid` / `ClientSeatLimitCard` precedent.
- **`PolicyOverrideRow`** (`settings/PolicyOverrideRow.tsx`) тАФ `'use client'` Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4b. The canonical "inherited from agency / overridden here" affordance for sub-account settings: a label + an inherited/overridden source badge + the agency value hint when inherited + a "Revert to agency" action when overridden; the control is `children` (the parent owns what "override" means for its policy key). Sibling export **`PolicySourceBadge`** is the standalone pill (used by `ClientSeatLimitCard`). Consumed today by the sub-account integrations view.

### `app/settings/team/` тАФ shared-slug Team tab (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite)

- **`page.tsx`** тАФ `'use client'` role dispatcher (operator тЖТ `_admin-content`, client тЖТ `_client-content`).
- **`_admin-content.tsx`** тАФ the operator workspace team page (`AdminSettingsTeamContent`) тАФ team members + role-permission matrix + the `InviteTeamButton`.
- **`_client-content.tsx`** тАФ the client's own-account view (`ClientSettingsTeamContent`) тАФ `SeatUsageMeter` + `InviteTeammateButton`, the current-users list + pending invites (both via the shared `TeamRow`), and a "what teammates can do" explainer. Reactive to the client-invite store so a freshly-sent invite appears immediately.

### `lib/team/` тАФ team-invite data shapes + roles

- **`types.ts`** тАФ `TeamInviteStatus` (now a re-alias of `InviteStatus` from `lib/invites/shared-types` тАФ single-sourced so the operator + client invite siblings can't drift), `TeamInviteDraft` (mutable form state тАФ `{ email, fullName, role, assignedClientIds, personalNote }`), and the committed `TeamInvite` (draft + `id`, `invitedBy` (operator user id тАФ an invite without it is unattributable, vision ┬з7), `invitedAt` / `expiresAt` (ISO strings), `magicLink`, `status`). Stub-becomes-schema-contract: every field is producible from real DB rows + lookups with no narrative interpretation.
- **`roles.ts`** тАФ `TeamRole` (`'owner' | 'operator' | 'junior'` тАФ the operator-tier org role, distinct from `Role` in `capabilities.ts`), `TEAM_ROLES` (the 3 role defs: id / name / icon glyph / description), and `TEAM_ROLE_CAPABILITIES: Record<TeamRole, readonly Capability[]>` тАФ **derived** from the cap layer: owner + operator inherit `ADMIN_DEFAULTS` verbatim; junior is a deliberate subset (`viewBuilder`, `editCopy`, `editMedia`, `editSEO`, `useAI` тАФ `editSEO` is deliberately in, since SEO drafts тЙа SEO publishes and the `publish` gate still requires operator). `getTeamRoleDef(role)` helper.

### `lib/invites/` тАФ invite primitives + client teammate invite (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6 ┬╖ client invite)

> `ClientUserInvite` is a **sibling** of `lib/team/types.ts` `TeamInvite`, NOT a generalization тАФ the dimensions genuinely differ (no Webnua-org role; a single fixed `clientId` not `assignedClientIds[]`; a client-user inviter; different RLS/lifecycle). Two clean siblings beat one record with conditional optional fields. Only the genuinely-common primitives are shared.

- **`shared-types.ts`** тАФ `InviteStatus` (`'pending' | 'accepted' | 'expired' | 'revoked'` тАФ the lifecycle union both invite siblings use; `lib/team` `TeamInviteStatus` re-aliases it), `IsoTimestamp` / `MagicLink` (convention-carrying string aliases), `INVITE_TTL_DAYS` (= 7).
- **`client-invite.ts`** тАФ `ClientUserInviteDraft` (mutable form state тАФ `{ email, fullName, personalNote }`) + the committed `ClientUserInvite` (`id`, `email`, `fullName`, fixed `clientId`, `invitedBy` (client user id тАФ attributable, vision ┬з7), `invitedAt` / `expiresAt`, `magicLink`, `status: InviteStatus`, `personalNote: string | null`). Stub-becomes-schema-contract.
- **`client-invite-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`.** Invite list backed by `client_user_invites`. `addClientInvite` writes through; `getInvitesForClient` (pending only), `getAllClientInvites` (snapshot-cached for `useSyncExternalStore` stability), `subscribeClientInvites`.
- **`seats.ts`** тАФ seat accounting. `getClientSeatUsage(clientId)` тЖТ `SeatUsage` (`usedByUsers` + `usedByInvites` + `total` + `limit`); usage is **derived** (existing client users + pending invites тАФ pending counts so the limit can't be gamed by bulk-inviting). `canInviteToClient(clientId)` тЖТ `{ allowed, reason? }` (`reason: InviteBlockReason` тАФ `'seat_limit_reached'` today, union kept open) тАФ backs both the modal's Continue gate and the send guard.
- **`use-seat-usage.ts`** тАФ `useClientSeatUsage(clientId)` hook тАФ `useSyncExternalStore` over both feeder stores (client invites + seat limits), snapshot-cached against a derived key so the reference only changes when the counts change.

### `lib/clients/` тАФ per-client seat limit + identity tones (Phase 6 ┬╖ Cluster 6тАУ7)

- **`tones.ts`** (Session 7) тАФ the canonical **solid per-client identity colour** map: `ClientTone` (the superset union тАФ `voltline | freshhome | keyhero | neatworks | flowline | generic`) + `CLIENT_TONE_BG` / `CLIENT_TONE_BORDER_L` (pre-composed Tailwind class records, because arbitrary-value classes can't be built from runtime strings). Consumed by `BookingPill`, `CalendarLegend`, `CalendarTodayPanel`, `AdminBookingHero`, and `AutomationFlowMini`. Promoted out of `lib/calendar/tones.ts` in Session 7 once automations became the fourth consumer (calendar was the wrong home for a cross-domain map). Feature modules keep their narrower tone unions (`CalendarClientTone`, `AutomationClientTone`) and index the wider record. The muted pill-tint vocabularies (`LeadClientTone` / `AdminTicketClientTone`) are a separate concern тАФ not here (see the resolved parked decision).
- **`seat-limit.ts`** тАФ `SeatLimitChange` (`{ changedBy, changedAt, clientId, previousLimit, newLimit }`, limits `number | null`) тАФ every limit change is an attributable event (vision ┬з7); history is an array of these, not a single overwritten value.
- **`seat-limit-stub.ts`** тАФ **Supabase-backed cache, hydrated by `DataHydrationProvider`.** **Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4b тАФ a facade over the agency policy resolver**, not a standalone store. The seat limit is the `defaultSeatLimit` policy key: the effective limit resolves down the layers (`resolvePolicy('defaultSeatLimit', clientId)`) тАФ agency default (Layer 2) тЖТ per-account override (Layer 3, `override-stub`). This module keeps the seat-limit export surface (`getSeatLimit`, `getAgencySeatLimit`, `isSeatLimitOverridden`, `setSeatLimit` = set an override, `inheritSeatLimit` = clear it, `subscribeSeatLimits`) and owns the change-history log (Supabase `seat_limit_changes` table тАФ `getSeatLimitHistory`, `subscribeSeatLimitHistory`), which the generic override store doesn't track. `getSeatLimit`/`subscribeSeatLimits` keep their old names so `lib/invites/seats.ts` + `use-seat-usage.ts` are unchanged.

> Note: `AdminClient` (`lib/nav/admin-clients.ts`) carried a `seatLimit` field through Cluster 6; **Cluster 8 ┬╖ Session 4b retired it** тАФ the per-client seed values moved into `SUB_ACCOUNT_OVERRIDE_SEED` (`lib/agency/override-stub.ts`) and the seat limit now resolves through the `defaultSeatLimit` policy key.

---

## Migration log (recent)

> One line per migration since the May 2026 audit found inventory drift.
> Older migrations are referenced inline in the relevant inventory entries.

- **`0023_seed_builder_websites_funnels.sql`** тАФ PR #41. Seed rows for the builder family (websites + funnels + their draft versions) so the editor has something to open after a fresh hydration.
- **`0024_brands_capability_rls.sql`** тАФ PR #43. RLS policies for `brands` + `capability_grants` once the auth + cap layer landed.
- **`0025_seed_agency_billing.sql`** тАФ PR #43. Seed rows for the agency policy + plan catalog + plan assignment tables (the Layer-2 / Layer-2.5 of the policy resolver).
- **`0026_section_type_enum_additions.sql`** тАФ PR #45. Adds `features`, `gallery`, `about`, `contact` to the `section_type` Postgres enum to match the section-library uplift.
- **`0027_section_media_bucket.sql`** тАФ PR #45 era. Storage bucket + RLS for the per-section media uploads (`uploadSectionImage`).
- **`0028_fix_clients_select_returning.sql`** тАФ PR #45. Drop / re-add `clients_select` policy so `INSERT тАж RETURNING *` from `create-client.ts` works.
- **`0029_capability_enum_add_editforms.sql`** тАФ PR #46. Adds `editforms` to the `capability` Postgres enum.
- **`0030_section_type_add_form.sql`** тАФ PR #46. Adds `form` to the `section_type` enum.
- **`0031_lead_attachments_bucket.sql`** тАФ PR #46. Storage bucket + RLS for the form-builder image-attachment uploads.
- **`0032_notification_write_path.sql`** тАФ Phase 9. `AFTER INSERT` triggers fanning notifications + the `supabase_realtime` publication entries (already referenced inline above).
- **`0033_funnel_slug.sql`** тАФ funnel-slug add.
- **`0034_normalise_site_domains.sql`** тАФ domain-host normalisation pass.
- **`0035_analytics_tables.sql`** тАФ visitor-engagement tracking tables (PR #52 era).
- **`0036_funnel_brief_fields.sql`** тАФ adds `funnel_service` / `funnel_customer_pain` / `funnel_guarantee` (text) + `funnel_testimonials` (jsonb, default `[]`) to `public.funnels`. Captured by the wizard's brief step; consumed by the AI funnel offer generator in a later session. No standalone `briefs` table тАФ funnel-specific brief data lives with the funnel, matching the existing pattern where brief data lands on the entity tables it semantically belongs to (business identity on `clients`, brand voice on `brands`).
- **`0037_funnel_offer.sql`** тАФ adds `funnel_offer jsonb` (nullable) to `public.funnels`. Shape: `{ headline, promise, risk_reversal, cta_text }`. Populated by the wizard's funnel-offer step (Sonnet-backed `/api/generate-offer`) when the operator runs offer generation; NULL when the operator skipped the step or the run failed. Single jsonb (not four text columns) because the four fields are one unit of data тАФ always created, edited and rendered together. Matches the `funnel_testimonials` shape.
- **`0038_form_submit_error_enum.sql`** + **`0039_form_submit_error_aggregation.sql`** тАФ analytics-audit ┬з5.2 gap #1. Added `form_submit_error` to `analytics_event_type` and the matching `form_failed` rollup stage so a failed `/api/forms/submit` no longer counts as a success.
- **`0040_form_abandon_aggregation.sql`** тАФ analytics-audit ┬з5.2 gap #2. Added the missing `when event_type = 'form_abandon' then 'form_abandoned'` branch so abandons roll up instead of being pruned at 90d.
- **`0041_scroll_and_click_aggregation.sql`** тАФ closes analytics-audit ┬з3 / ┬з4 website-side gaps. Adds three previously-dropped scroll-depth stages (`scrolled_25`, `scrolled_75`, `scrolled_90`; existing `engaged` keeps the canonical 50% label so prior consumers stay wired). Adds `element_label text not null default ''` to `analytics_funnel_daily` and extends the PK to `(surface_id, day, stage, element_label)`, so per-CTA click rollup rows are queryable. The aggregator populates `element_label` from `payload->>'label'` (truncated 120 chars) for `element_click` events; all other stages write `''`. Surfaced on `/website` via the new `WebsiteEngagementCard` (scroll-depth breakdown + top CTAs + form completion) and per-page `PageGridCard` visit/avg-time stats from a new `fetchPageTotalsByRef` helper. Does NOT touch the funnel rollup's `page_ref` step-granularity (audit ┬з2.2) тАФ that's closed by 0042.
- **`0042_funnel_step_granularity.sql`** тАФ closes analytics-audit ┬з2.2 / ┬з2.6 + the CLAUDE.md parked decision "Funnel analytics gaps that remain after lead threading". Adds `page_ref text not null default ''` to `analytics_funnel_daily` and extends the PK to `(surface_id, day, stage, element_label, page_ref)`; the aggregator's GROUP BY gains `page_ref`. A funnel's step-1 (`page_ref = ''`, served at the funnel root) and step-2 (`page_ref = <step.slug>`) now roll up as distinct rows, so step-by-step drop-off is queryable. Empty-string sentinel matches the `element_label` convention from 0041 тАФ no NULL in PK. Backwards-compatible: website surfaces typically have a single `page_ref` per surface, and the existing `fetchSurfaceFunnelTotals` reads (which sum across all `page_ref` rows) produce the same totals. The new `fetchFunnelStepBreakdown(surfaceId, pageRefs)` consumes the per-step axis; surfaced on `/funnels/[id]` (the prototype Screen 23 detail). The 90-day raw-event window means existing events back-fill on the next aggregator tick тАФ rollup table was empty at apply time so no data preservation concern.
- **`0043_lead_source_kind.sql`** тАФ adds `source_kind text not null default 'website'` to `public.leads`, check-constrained to `'website' | 'funnel' | 'meta'`. Surfaces the categorical surface attribution on the inbox as a Source column / pill (`LeadSourcePill`). Written by `/api/forms/submit` from a new `surfaceKind` body field (`'website' | 'funnel'`) the public renderer + the editor test-submit both populate via `PublicFormSubmit.surfaceKind` and `FormTestSubmitContext.surfaceKind`. `meta` is reserved for the future Meta lead-ads integration тАФ the value is in the constraint now so the enum doesn't churn when it lands. Plain text + check (not a Postgres enum) тАФ cheaper to extend later when new surfaces (e.g. `'gbp'`, `'referral'`) are added.
- **`0044_lead_source_funnel_id.sql`** тАФ adds `source_funnel_id uuid` to `public.leads` (nullable, FK to `public.funnels`, `on delete set null`) + a single-column index on the FK. Pairs with `source_kind` from `0043`: the kind is *categorical* (website / funnel / meta) for the inbox column; this is the *entity FK* a client can run multiple funnels against. NULL = captured outside a funnel (every website-form submission + every lead created before this migration). Written by `/api/forms/submit` (only when `surfaceKind === 'funnel'`, with a cross-tenant guard that the funnel belongs to the posted `clientId`). The public renderer threads it through via a new `funnelId` field on `PublicFormSubmit` + the `PublicSiteRenderer` `funnel`-case prop. Powers `getBookedFromFunnelCount` (`lib/analytics/queries.tsx`) тАФ one count over `leads` filtered by `source_funnel_id` + `status in ('booked', 'completed')` + capture window (`leads.created_at`, default 7 days matching the funnel hero's "Funnel performance ┬╖ 7 days"). Closes the CLAUDE.md "Funnel-to-lead attribution" parked decision; the `/funnels/[id]` hero "booked from this funnel" tile now renders real numbers instead of `тАФ`. Leads created before this migration carry NULL and are correctly excluded. **Editor test-submit attribution is intentionally NOT wired** тАФ `submitLead` (`lib/leads/queries.tsx`) and `FormTestSubmitContext` (`lib/website/form-config.ts`) don't carry a `funnelId`, so editor test leads from a funnel preview carry `source_kind = 'funnel'` but `source_funnel_id = NULL`. Test leads are vanishingly rare in production analytics; thread `funnelId` through `FormTestSubmitContext` + `submitLead` later if test traffic starts polluting the count.
- **`0045_rls_cross_tenant_fixes.sql`** тАФ closes three cross-tenant RLS holes the Section-A validation pass found (harness: `tests/rls/`, run with `pnpm test:rls`; doc: `reference/rls-test-suite.md`). (1) **`users` privilege escalation** тАФ `users_update`'s `WITH CHECK` only re-asserts row ownership, so a client could `update public.users set role='admin', client_id=null, team_role='owner' where id=auth.uid()` and become an operator (or move `client_id` to another tenant); fixed with a `BEFORE UPDATE` trigger (`private.guard_user_identity_columns`) that makes `role`/`client_id`/`team_role` immutable to non-operators (RLS `WITH CHECK` can't compare OLD vs NEW тАФ a trigger can). (2) **`website_versions_insert`** + (3) **`website_approval_submissions_insert`** gated `INSERT` purely on `private.has_capability()`, which is true for a workspace-wide (`website_id IS NULL`) grant on *any* website тАФ so a client holding such a grant could write versions/approvals into another tenant's website; fixed by ANDing a tenant-membership `EXISTS` clause onto each `WITH CHECK`. All three verified live before + after the fix. The funnel-side equivalents already carried the tenant check and were unaffected.
- **`0046_funnel_publish_realtime.sql`** тАФ A3 (funnel publish + approval lane). Adds the four builder tables тАФ `website_approval_submissions`, `funnel_approval_submissions`, `website_versions`, `funnel_versions` тАФ to the `supabase_realtime` publication so `RealtimeProvider` can subscribe to `postgres_changes` and fan a `BUILDER_EVENT` (a submitter's editor lock clears when an operator resolves; a published version surfaces on the detail / roster). RLS still scopes which change events each user receives. Each `alter publication` is wrapped in a `duplicate_object`-tolerant `DO` block. The `funnel_approval_submissions` *table* already existed (pre-aligned in migration 0015) тАФ this migration adds no tables. **It supersedes B1's separate `0046_realtime_website_approvals.sql`** (which added `website_approval_submissions` only) тАФ that file was a same-numbered duplicate from a parallel branch and was folded into this superset migration during the B1тЖФA3 merge.
- **`0047_integration_call_log.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. Audit log of every external API call + inbound webhook (provider / operation / direction / redacted request+response shapes / status / latency / error class+message / client_id / correlation_id). Operator-only tenant-scoped RLS; service-role writes. Single table for V1 тАФ monthly-partition path documented in the migration comment.
- **`0048_integration_jobs.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. The async-work queue (status / attempts / run_after / provider / job_type / payload / result / error). Internal infrastructure тАФ RLS on with zero policies, all `authenticated` privileges revoked; service-role only.
- **`0049_integration_jobs_cron.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. `pg_cron` poller (every minute) dispatching due jobs to `/api/internal/job-executor` via `pg_net`; reclaims stale `running` jobs after a 10-min lease. Adds `private.integration_runtime_config` (single-row table holding the executor base URL + shared secret тАФ operator populates once post-deploy; see the table comment).
- **`0050_client_sms_senders.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. Per-client Twilio alphanumeric one-way SMS sender assignment (one per client, тЙд11-char, registration-status lifecycle). Operator-only tenant-scoped RLS; service-role writes.
- **`0051_client_email_senders.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. Per-client Resend email sub-address slug (the sending address `[slug]@mail.webnua.com` is composed in app code, not stored). Operator-only RLS; service-role writes.
- **`0052_client_stripe_customers.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. Per-client Stripe Customer mapping (standard scope, no Connect). Operator-only RLS; service-role writes.
- **`0053_notifications_outbound.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 1. Audit log of operator-facing notification emails sent (throttle + audit; carries the Resend message id). Operator-only tenant-scoped RLS.
- **`0054_vault_setup.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 2. Supabase Vault (`supabase_vault`) + four `public` SECURITY DEFINER wrapper functions (`webnua_vault_create_secret` / `_read_secret` / `_update_secret` / `_delete_secret`) so server code can mint/read/rotate/delete encrypted secrets тАФ EXECUTE revoked from `public` / `anon` / `authenticated`, granted to `service_role` only. The `vault` schema is not PostgREST-reachable; the wrappers bridge it. Fallback (pgsodium) documented in the migration comment.
- **`0055_integration_connections.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 2. The per-tenant OAuth connection table тАФ one row per customer account per provider. Generic across providers; supports both token models (`token_model`: `refresh_access` / `long_lived`). The persistent secret lives in Vault (`token_secret_id`); only the short-lived Google access token is plain (`access_token_cached`). Operator-only tenant-scoped RLS; service-role writes; clients get no access.
- **`0056_token_refresh_cron.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Session 2. Daily `pg_cron` schedule that enqueues a `token_refresh_check` job onto the Session 1 jobs spine тАФ the handler proactively refreshes `long_lived` (Meta) connections before expiry.
- **`0057_stripe_pricing.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Stripe billing. Extends `client_stripe_customers` (from `0052`) with the subscription posture the Stripe webhook keeps current: `stripe_subscription_id`, `stripe_price_id`, `current_period_end`, `cancel_at_period_end`, `last_payment_at`, `last_payment_status`, `past_due_since`, `updated_at`. Adds `'incomplete'` to the `status` check (a customer record with no subscription yet тАФ the checkout route inserts the row before Checkout completes) and re-defaults `status` to `'incomplete'`. Pricing stays env config тАФ the тВм299/month Price id lives in `STRIPE_PRICE_ID_STANDARD`, not a table; the migration comment documents the path to a `stripe_prices` table once there is more than one tier. RLS unchanged (`client_stripe_customers` stays operator-SELECT / service-role-write).
- **`0058_client_sms_sender_registration.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Twilio SMS. Adds `twilio_registration_sid` to `client_sms_senders` (from `0050`) тАФ the Twilio AlphaSender resource SID `registerSenderID()` writes and `getSenderIDStatus()` polls. NULL until the operator submits a sender id. RLS / grants unchanged (the column inherits the table's operator-SELECT / service-role-write policy).
- **`0059_sms_messages.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Twilio SMS. The SMS send log тАФ one row per outbound send: `client_id`, `sender_id` (the alphanumeric value snapshot), `recipient_phone`, `message_body`, `segments_count` + `encoding` (computed by the SMS validator at send), `twilio_message_sid`, `status` (queued/sent/delivered/failed/undelivered), `error_code`/`error_message`, `related_lead_id`, `cost_eur`. Indexed by client+sent_at and by Twilio SID (the status-webhook lookup). RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()` (operators see their clients' messages, a client sees its own); writes service-role only.
- **`0060_sms_templates.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Twilio SMS. Per-client SMS templates тАФ `(client_id, template_key)` unique, `body`, `is_default`, `last_edited_at`/`by`. `template_key` check-constrained to the closed 4 (`lead_acknowledgment` / `job_confirmation` / `arrival_notification` / `review_request`). A `private.seed_sms_templates()` helper + an `AFTER INSERT` trigger on `clients` seed the four defaults for every new client (SECURITY DEFINER тАФ a seed is a system event); existing clients are backfilled. The default bodies here must stay in lockstep with `DEFAULT_SMS_TEMPLATES` (`lib/sms/default-templates.ts`). RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()`; writes service-role only. Editor UI is deferred to the Automations feature тАФ until then the `send_sms` job reads the seeded body straight from the row.
- **`0061_email_messages.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Resend. The email conversation log тАФ one row per outbound send + per inbound reply, discriminated by `direction`. Columns: `client_id`, `sender_address` / `recipient_address` / `reply_to_address` snapshots, `subject` + `body_text` + `body_html`, `resend_message_id` (status webhook lookup), `in_reply_to_message_id` (RFC 2822 threading), `status` (queued/sent/delivered/bounced/complained/failed/received), `related_lead_id`, `thread_token`, `attachments` jsonb, `is_auto_responder`, `sent_by`. Indexed by `(related_lead_id, occurred_at)` for the conversation read, by `resend_message_id` for the delivery webhook, by `thread_token` for inbound routing debug. RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()` (operators see their clients' messages, a client sees their own); writes service-role only.
- **`0062_email_templates.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Resend. Per-client email templates тАФ `(client_id, template_key)` unique. `template_key` check-constrained to the closed 5 (`lead_followup` / `review_request` / `quote_followup` / `lead_notification` / `lead_digest`). Each row carries `subject` + `body_html` + `body_text` (Resend sends both; mail clients pick). A `private.seed_email_templates()` helper + AFTER INSERT trigger on `clients` seed all five defaults per client (SECURITY DEFINER, same pattern as 0060); existing clients are backfilled. **Default bodies stay in lockstep with `DEFAULT_EMAIL_TEMPLATES`** (`lib/email/default-templates.ts`) тАФ editing the defaults means BOTH files. Operator template editor is deferred (same precedent as SMS templates).
- **`0063_notification_preferences.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Resend. Per-client operator notification recipients. `(client_id, operator_email)` unique, with per-event flags (`notify_on_new_lead` / `notify_on_payment_failure` / `notify_on_review_received`, all default true) + `digest_frequency` (`immediate` / `hourly` / `daily`). Adds `leads.notification_pending_at` (timestamptz, NULL when no notification has been deferred тАФ set by the throttle path of `send_lead_notification`, cleared by the digest worker). AFTER INSERT trigger on `leads` enqueues a `send_lead_notification` job. `pg_cron` schedule enqueues `batch_notification_digest` hourly. RLS: operators see their accessible clients' preferences; writes service-role only.
- **`0064_email_attachments_bucket.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Resend. Supabase Storage bucket for email attachments (outbound: operator-attached files on a reply; inbound: re-uploaded from the inbound MIME so the conversation view can display them). Private bucket; reads gated on `accessible_client_ids()` via the path's first segment (the client slug). Writes service-role only. Path convention: `{client_slug}/{direction}/{email_message_id}/{filename}`.
- **`0066_client_gbp_locations.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 GBP. Per-client Google Business Profile location selection тАФ one row per client (UNIQUE on `client_id`; V1 forcing function тАФ multi-location clients need this loosened + a `primary` flag). Stores the resource-name pair `gbp_account_id` (`accounts/...`) + `gbp_location_id` (`locations/...`), plus cached `location_title` / `address` / `phone` / `website` / `review_link` (the substitution target for `{{review.link}}`), `current_rating` + `review_count` (refreshed by the daily sync), and `last_synced_at`. RLS: operators see their accessible clients' locations; writes service-role only.
- **`0067_gbp_reviews.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 GBP. Local cache of GBP reviews тАФ upserted by the daily `gbp_sync_reviews` job. UNIQUE on `(client_id, gbp_review_id)` so per-client upsert is trivial. Stores reviewer name + photo (may be NULL for anonymous reviews), 1-5 `rating`, comment, Google timestamps (`created_at_google` / `updated_at_google`), and operator `reply_text` + `reply_created_at` once one is published. `is_new_since_last_view` powers the operator dashboard badge тАФ preserved across syncs (the handler's two-pass strategy never touches it for known reviews). `deleted_at_google` marks reviews removed at Google so they drop out of the visible list but stay for audit. RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()`; writes service-role only.
- **`0068_gbp_review_requests.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 GBP. Audit log of review-request SMS/email sends. One row per send attempt, written by the `gbp_send_review_request` job. Channel-agnostic vocabulary (`channel` = sms|email, `status` = queued/sent/delivered/failed) тАФ per-channel detail (segments, delivery status, Resend message id) is in `sms_messages` / `email_messages`. `resulted_in_review_id` FK is populated by the sync job's 7-day attribution window so the conversion rate is queryable. RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()`; writes service-role only.
- **`0069_gbp_triggers_and_cron.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 GBP. Four pieces of plumbing: (1) `AFTER UPDATE` trigger on `bookings` that fires `gbp_send_review_request` with a **2-hour `run_after` delay** on the transition to `status='completed'` (matches the "let the customer experience the work first" UX intent). Looks up the customer's phone/email so the job has a payload to act on; skips cleanly when no contact channel exists. Same swallow-errors pattern as `0063`'s lead-notification trigger тАФ an enqueue failure must not fail the booking update. (2) Daily `pg_cron` schedule at 06:00 UTC enqueueing one `gbp_sync_reviews` job per `client_gbp_locations` with an active GBP `integration_connections`. (3) `AFTER INSERT` trigger on `gbp_reviews` that fans an in-app `notification_kind='review'` via `private.notify_client_users` from migration `0032` (operator + client users see the new review notification immediately). (4) Adds `gbp_reviews` + `gbp_review_requests` to the `supabase_realtime` publication so `RealtimeProvider` can keep operator dashboards live.
- **`0070_client_meta_ad_accounts.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Meta Ads. Per-client mapping of "which Meta ad account does Webnua manage for this client". UNIQUE on `client_id` (V1 forcing function тАФ one ad account per client; the multi-ad-account / agency-of-agency case loosens this + adds a `primary` flag later). Stores Meta's `act_*` ad-account id + business id + cached posture (name / currency / status code / balance / amount spent / timezone) + the operator-confirmed customer-agreement audit snapshot (`customer_agreed_at` / `customer_agreed_by_email`). RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()`; writes service-role only.
- **`0071_meta_lead_forms.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Meta Ads. Catalogue of Meta lead-form records. Unique on `meta_form_id`. Stores Page id, form name, the field structure snapshot (so the lead-sync job can map field values to display labels without extra round-trips), and `archived_at` for Meta-side soft-deleted forms (kept for late-arriving leads + audit). RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()`; service-role writes.
- **`0072_meta_campaigns.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Meta Ads. The Meta-side record for every campaign Webnua launched (or imported). Unique on both `meta_campaign_id` AND `campaign_id` (each Meta campaign maps 1:1 to one operator-facing `public.campaigns` row). The launch orchestrator inserts both rows in lockstep so the existing `/campaigns` surfaces light up automatically; `campaign_id` CASCADE-deletes keep them aligned. New enums: `meta_campaign_status` (`active | paused | archived | in_review | with_issues`) and `meta_campaign_created_via` (`webnua_month_1 | webnua_ongoing | external`) тАФ the month-1 / ongoing split is what the тВм200 ad-credit accounting reads.
- **`0073_meta_ads_insights.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Meta Ads. Daily per-campaign metrics. Unique on `(meta_campaign_id, date_recorded)` so the upsert from the sync job is trivially idempotent. Stores impressions / clicks / leads (extracted from Meta's `actions` array) / spend (minor units) / CPL / CTR (basis points) + the raw `/insights` payload as jsonb for diagnostics + future-metric extraction without a re-pull. RLS: SELECT for `accessible_client_ids()`; service-role writes.
- **`0074_meta_ads_cron.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Meta Ads. Two `pg_cron` schedules + realtime publication. **Daily `04:00 UTC`** enqueues one `meta_sync_insights` job per active campaign on a client with an active Meta `integration_connections`. **Every 15 minutes** enqueues one `meta_sync_leads` job per active campaign that has a wired lead form (polling rather than push because Meta's lead webhooks aren't reliable enough to depend on). Adds `meta_campaigns` + `meta_ads_insights` to the `supabase_realtime` publication so the operator `/campaigns` surface refreshes when a sync completes.
- **`0075_meta_sync_campaigns_cron.sql`** тАФ Phase 7 Meta Ads campaign-ingest cron. Adds an **hourly** `pg_cron` schedule (`7 * * * *`) that enqueues one `meta_sync_campaigns` job per client with an active Meta `integration_connections` AND a `client_meta_ad_accounts` row. The handler (server: `meta-ads/job-handlers.ts`) calls `/act_{id}/campaigns` via `callWithToken()` and upserts both `public.campaigns` + `meta_campaigns` for every campaign on the ad account. The job is also enqueued immediately by the ad-account `select` route so a freshly-connected customer sees their campaigns within seconds; the operator can trigger it manually via the "тЖ╗ Sync campaigns" button on `/campaigns`. Closes the V1 follow-up flagged on the previous Meta migration set тАФ campaigns built in Meta Ads Manager now flow into Webnua's `/campaigns` roster automatically.

---

## Remaining build phases

> The roadmap to a finished platform. The frontend + the wired-data backend
> (Phases 1тАУ6 / Clusters 1тАУ9 + the form builder) are done. What is left:

- **Phase 7 тАФ Integrations.** OAuth + API for GBP, Meta Ads, GA4, Google Ads
  (business) and Stripe, Resend, Twilio (platform). Makes the
  `/settings/integrations` connect flows real; unlocks review auto-pull,
  campaign metrics, email/SMS sending, real billing.
  **Session 1 (platform integration spine) тАФ DONE.** The shared foundation is
  built: `lib/env.ts` (typed/boot-validated env), `callExternal()`, the
  retry helper, the `integration_jobs` queue + `pg_cron` poller + executor
  route, `integration_call_log`, the three client-assignment tables, and
  `notifications_outbound` (migrations `0047`тАУ`0053`).
  **Session 2 (per-tenant OAuth foundation) тАФ DONE.** Supabase Vault
  (token encryption), the `integration_connections` table, the OAuth provider
  registry (GBP fully implemented; Meta written but unverified тАФ `TODO(meta)`),
  the connect / callback / disconnect routes, `callWithToken()`, the daily
  token-refresh job, and the operator connections UI (migrations `0054`тАУ`0056`).
  See `reference/integration-foundation-audit.md`.
  **Stripe billing тАФ DONE.** Subscription billing for clients: тВм299/month via
  Stripe Checkout, the webhook тЖТ `client_stripe_customers` sync, the
  payment-failed operator alert (on the jobs queue), and the operator billing
  UI on sub-account `/settings/billing`. See the "Stripe billing" inventory +
  the "Stripe billing тАФ operator setup" steps above; migration `0057`.
  **Twilio SMS тАФ DONE.** One-way alphanumeric SMS sending: the Twilio client
  wrapper, the SMS character validator + template renderer + cost estimator,
  the per-client sender registration + template editor UI on sub-account
  `/settings/sms`, the `send_sms` job handler, the status-callback webhook, and
  the lead-acknowledgment auto-trigger on the public form-submit flow. See the
  "Twilio SMS" inventory + the "Twilio SMS тАФ operator setup" steps above;
  migrations `0058`тАУ`0060`.
  **Resend email тАФ DONE.** Two-way email integration with inbound reply
  routing: the Resend wrapper, HMAC-signed plus-addressed thread tokens
  (`{clientSlug}+lead-{token}@mail.webnua.com`), per-client sender slug
  + display name provisioning UI, the five seeded templates (`lead_followup`
  / `review_request` / `quote_followup` / `lead_notification` /
  `lead_digest`), the inbound webhook (signature-verified, cross-tenant-
  guarded, auto-responder-detecting, attachment-reuploading), the delivery
  webhook (status reconciliation by Resend message id), the operator-side
  reply flow from inside the lead inbox, and operator notification
  preferences with per-client recipients, per-event flags, and an
  immediate/hourly/daily digest model. The lead-followup customer email is
  enqueued from the public form-submit route when an email is captured;
  the operator new-lead notification fans automatically via the migration
  0063 trigger. See the "Resend email" inventory + the "Resend email тАФ
  operator setup" steps above; migrations `0061`тАУ`0064`. The remaining
  per-provider business logic тАФ GBP review pull, Meta campaign metrics тАФ
  follows.
  **Google Business Profile тАФ DONE.** Per-tenant GBP integration end-to-end:
  the API client (`listAccounts` / `listLocations` / `getLocation` /
  `listReviews` / `replyToReview` through `callWithToken`), the
  post-OAuth location-picker modal (auto-opened from
  `/settings/integrations`), the daily review-pull cron with seen-state
  preserved across syncs, the booking-completion trigger that auto-fires
  a review request 2 hours later through SMS (preferred) or email
  (fallback), and the operator + client dashboard widgets. **UI
  consolidation (PR #100):** every GBP affordance lives on Webnua's
  established surfaces тАФ reviews + inline reply on `/reviews` (both
  contexts), review-request audit on the lead timeline, manual "Send
  review request" on lead + booking detail, connection management on
  `/settings/integrations` with a GBP-only footer for location summary
  + Sync / Change. No dedicated GBP tab. SMS/email `{{review.link}}`
  substitution resolved via `getReviewLinkForClient`. GBP Posts +
  insights deferred to V1.1. See the "Google Business Profile (Phase 7)"
  inventory + "Google Business Profile тАФ operator setup" steps;
  migrations `0066`тАУ`0069`.
  **Meta Ads тАФ DONE (FINAL Phase 7 session).** Per-tenant Meta Ads
  integration: the API client (`listAdAccounts` / `listPages` /
  `listCampaignsForAdAccount` / `pause`+`activate` / `getCampaign` /
  `getCampaignInsights` / `getLeads`, all through `callWithToken` тАФ
  the `create*` family is exported but un-called, kept for a future
  in-app launch path if one ever ships), the post-OAuth ad-account
  picker + customer-agreement capture (`MetaAdAccountPickerModal`),
  the **Open Meta Ads Manager тЖТ** deep-link button +
  **тЖ╗ Sync campaigns** trigger (`LaunchMetaCampaignButton`), the
  hourly `meta_sync_campaigns` ingest cron (minute 7 of every hour,
  migration `0075`) + daily insights cron + quarter-hour leads cron,
  and `lib/campaigns/queries.tsx` joined to `meta_campaigns` +
  `meta_ads_insights` so the previously-`тАФ` per-row metrics and the
  4-week trend chart render real numbers. **V1 model**: Webnua does
  NOT build campaigns in-app тАФ the customer's OAuth grant gives
  Webnua business-manager access, and the operator manages campaigns
  directly in Meta Ads Manager. The `meta_sync_campaigns` job pulls
  Ads-Manager-launched campaigns BACK into Webnua so they surface on
  `/campaigns` (auto-fires post-pick, hourly thereafter, manual
  trigger via the "тЖ╗ Sync campaigns" button). The in-app launch
  wizard + 9 trade templates + 5-step orchestrator were removed in a
  follow-up once that V1 model settled. The **тВм200 month-1 ad-credit
  funding transfer is a manual operator process** (V2 to automate via
  Meta's funding APIs). **Outstanding follow-up**: lead-form discovery
  тАФ the campaign ingest fills `meta_lead_form_id` as null, so the
  `meta_sync_leads` job has nothing to attach to for Ads-Manager-
  launched campaigns. Discovering lead forms requires walking the
  campaign тЖТ ad-set тЖТ ad тЖТ creative chain or pulling per-Page; not in
  the campaign-ingest session. See the "Meta Ads (Phase 7 тАФ FINAL
  Phase 7 session)" inventory + "Meta Ads тАФ operator setup" steps;
  migrations `0070`тАУ`0075`. **Phase 7 тАФ DONE.**
- **Phase 8 тАФ Automation / messaging execution engine.** Automations are
  definitions only тАФ nothing sends. Needs a scheduler (edge function + cron),
  a `messaging_events` send-log table, and the suppression / anti-spam rules
  (see the parked decision). Closes the campaign + automation metrics gap.
  **Depends on Phase 7** (needs a working sender).
- **Phase 9 тАФ Realtime + notification writes тАФ DONE.**
  Notification write path: `AFTER INSERT` triggers fan notifications to a
  client's users on new leads / one-off bookings / reviews / operator ticket
  replies (migration `0032`, all `SECURITY DEFINER`). Realtime:
  `notifications` / `tickets` / `ticket_messages` are in the
  `supabase_realtime` publication (migration `0032`) and `RealtimeProvider`
  invalidates query keys on `postgres_changes`. **Builder approval Realtime
  is wired (B1 тЖТ A3)** тАФ B1 first added `website_approval_submissions` to the
  publication with targeted query-key invalidations; A3 unified all four
  builder tables (`website_approval_submissions` / `funnel_approval_submissions`
  / `website_versions` / `funnel_versions`, migration `0046`) under one
  `BUILDER_EVENT` fan, so the approval queue + the submitter's editor lock +
  the version surfaces react across tabs and users.
- **Phase 10 тАФ Production hardening.** Domain management (V2), deploy config,
  env/secrets, error monitoring, security review + Supabase advisors, live
  browser E2E.
- **Phase 11 тАФ Proof Page prospecting tool.** The deferred admin feature
  (audit тЖТ proof-page тЖТ outreach) тАФ see the section below. Build last.

**Additional gaps found in the May 2026 audit (not in the original 7тАУ11 list):**
- **Public site rendering.** Generated websites / funnels / lead-capture forms
  have no public render or hosting pipeline тАФ the editor builds them, nothing
  serves them. Its own workstream; Phase 10's domain management implies it but
  does not cover rendering.
- **Editor publish/approval layer тАФ DONE (PR #41 / merge `534de96`).**
  `publish-stub.ts` + `draft-stub.ts` are deleted; the layer is
  Supabase-backed via `lib/website/queries.tsx` + `mutations.ts` +
  `content-drafts.ts` + `snapshot.ts` + `builder-events.ts` against
  `website_versions` / `website_approval_submissions` /
  `force_publish_audit_log` / `content_drafts`. `audit-stub.ts` and
  `website-approval-stub.ts` collapsed to type-only display modules.
  Hook surface (`use-autosave`, `use-publish-state`) preserved.
- **Funnel publish / preflight unbuilt** тАФ see the parked decision.

## Deferred / out of scope until end

The admin **Proof Page / prospecting tool** (the audit тЖТ proof-page тЖТ outreach
pipeline, sourced from `reference/webnua-proof-page-tool.html` and
`reference/webnua-finding-library.json`) is a real platform feature **but is
deferred until the full platform тАФ front and back end тАФ is working.**

Until then:
- **Do not** scaffold routes, components, lib/types, or data for it.
- **Do not** add it to nav, sidebar, or any role's settings.
- **Do not** treat the prototype HTML or the finding-library JSON as current spec.
- The files stay in `/reference` тАФ they are the spec for the future build, not for now.

If a session has a reason to touch this area, stop and confirm with the user
first.
